乾县（好畤） (出生地)

-----title
西安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='61c3872909444f19bdc8f98c65b85010_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("61c3872909444f19bdc8f98c65b85010");'><span id='61c3872909444f19bdc8f98c65b85010_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=731&endYear=736')">731-736年</a>，7-12岁</div><div id='61c3872909444f19bdc8f98c65b85010' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=731&endYear=731')">731年</a>　父任监察御史，随父在长安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=732&endYear=732')">732年</a>　父转殿中侍御史，随父在长安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=733&endYear=733')">733年</a>　父为殿中侍御史，忤吏部侍郎李林甫，贬庐州长史，或在此年前后。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　父迁武功令，未到官，病免。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　父除宁州司马。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　在长安入学。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a12c788d8d0c4f728b9c2bbe90aef112_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a12c788d8d0c4f728b9c2bbe90aef112");'><span id='a12c788d8d0c4f728b9c2bbe90aef112_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=754&endYear=755')">754-755年</a>，30-31岁</div><div id='a12c788d8d0c4f728b9c2bbe90aef112' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=754&endYear=754')">754年2月</a>　应诏至长安，李隆基朝群臣，受大号曰开元天地大宝圣文神武证道皇帝，大赦天下,独孤及有文称颂。作品：《庆鸿名颂并序》<div id='poem_1367624' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367624' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367624?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庆鸿名颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（754年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367624")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367624_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367624'>唐兴百三十有八载。皇帝在宥。天下铸五兵为农器。栖万姓于寿域。道證德洽。神人以和。春正月。冢臣上将。卿士庶尹。洎三老五更。公侯伯子男。相与揭厉皇猷。请增明号。上撝谦而未许也。佥曰。陛下孝达神明。道超先帝。以德则符广运。以时则复大朴。以功则保定丕业。格于上下。而尊称犹浅。鸿名未光。亿兆之心何戴。神祇之望何塞。天子南向而让者九。不得已而俞之。乃命有司。具昭告之礼。二月乙酉。备法驾。朝太清宫。敕宫神以洒扫。诏月将使警跸。云动天旋。至于灵坛。报功乎三清。祈禠乎上元。景戌。享太庙。用明水越席玉豆彫篹之礼。焫萧以合芗。灌鬯以报魄。神休拥而万灵接。精意陈而六幽感。丁亥。朝群臣于蓬莱前殿。于是四方人大和会。命太尉班五瑞。合六乐。遂展礼奉策。虔受大号。曰开元天地大宝圣文神武證道孝德皇帝。是日也。解商野之三网。受涂山之万玉。大赦天下。与人更始。协时月。同度量。赞俊杰。书云物。恤高年。礼大祇。接天瑞。受地釐。抚柔万邦。存省其安危。遂迎日推筴。布庆行赐。扇薰风。调元气。拓千岁之大统。操三皇之遗珠。垂其衣裳。与天地合符。乐遍礼崇。乘舆乃入。然后屏椒房而彻黄屋。徜徉乎大庭氏之馆。泊兮凝神。恍兮存真。想洪崖广成之伦。披霓裳而下凤阙。蹁跹左右。上千万寿。凡遭逢昌运。沐浴圣涯。而不能颂烝人赋江汉。吉甫仍叔之罪也。臣敢有二事。乃作颂曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367624_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367624'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367624'>穆穆閟宫，敷时绎思。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367624'>天有成命，孝孙受之。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367624'>铺衍下土，报功神祇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367624'>我瑞如山，我福孔夷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367624'>圣敬攸感，上元岂私。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367624'>诞受鸿名，载扬缉熙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367624'>风动云行，雨飞露垂。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367624'>昆虫昭苏，草木阜滋。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367624'>恭已南面，无为之师。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367624'>柏皇尊卢，万代一时。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1367624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1367624'>昭假迟迟，上帝是祗。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1367624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1367624'>永锡多祜，万寿无期。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1367624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1367624'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1367624_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=754&endYear=754')">754年10月</a>　十月以洞晓元经科对策高第，解褐拜华阴尉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=754&endYear=754')">754年</a>　与贾至等再次欢叙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年1月</a>　在华阴任，因公务至长安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年</a>　年初在长安，得房琯赏识，并与李华、苏源明等有过从。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9e5b346e966c447a844e0dee2223c5b5_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>，39岁</div><div id='9e5b346e966c447a844e0dee2223c5b5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　召为左拾遗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　在左拾遗任。作品：《尚书祠部员外郎赠陕州刺史裴公行状》《送贺若员外巡按毕归朝序》《贺元傪破贼表》<div id='poem_1367790' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367790' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367790?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故尚书祠部员外郎赠陕州刺史裴公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367790")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367790_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367790'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367790'>曾祖仁基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367790_comment'></div>隋光禄大夫行左光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367790_comment'></div>皇朝赠使持节都督原州诸军事原州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367790_comment'></div>谥曰忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367790_comment'></div>祖行俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367790_comment'></div>皇朝银青光禄大夫礼部尚书闻喜县开国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367790_comment'></div>赠太尉扬州大都督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367790_comment'></div>谥曰献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367790_comment'></div>父光庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367790_comment'></div>皇朝光禄大夫行侍中兼吏部尚书正平县开国男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367790_comment'></div>赠太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367790_comment'></div>谥曰忠献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367790_comment'></div>绛州闻喜县崇庆乡太平里裴稹年若干行状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367790_comment'></div>公天姿英拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367790_comment'></div>德宇宏旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367790_comment'></div>禺昂公器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367790_comment'></div>磊砢高节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367790_comment'></div>武库森戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367790_comment'></div>玉山照人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367790_comment'></div>起家以门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367790_comment'></div>调补千牛备身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367790_comment'></div>历太子通事舍人太常寺主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367790_comment'></div>是时万邦方乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367790_comment'></div>献公当国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367790_comment'></div>天子垂衣穆清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367790_comment'></div>以有天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367790_comment'></div>而衮职之阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367790_comment'></div>畴咨之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367790_comment'></div>公入则竭力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367790_comment'></div>出则匪躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367790_comment'></div>外询舆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367790_comment'></div>以备过庭之问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367790_comment'></div>阴荐多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367790_comment'></div>用宏审官之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367790_comment'></div>既而济济俊乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367790_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1367790", 1367790, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>烂盈</span>东阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367790_comment'></div>邦之得贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367790_comment'></div>于斯为盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367790_comment'></div>画一之诗作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367790_comment'></div>而嘉鱼之颂兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367790_comment'></div>公之干蛊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367790_comment'></div>转京兆府司录参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367790_comment'></div>辇毂之大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367790_comment'></div>纲辖之剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367790_comment'></div>牒诉浩穰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367790_comment'></div>文墨填委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367790_comment'></div>公游刃馀地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367790_comment'></div>而大郤斯批。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367790_comment'></div>若网在条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367790_comment'></div>而众目不紊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367790_comment'></div>谈笑之隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367790_comment'></div>簿领肃如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367790_comment'></div>论者知逸骥之足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367790_comment'></div>方自此始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367790_comment'></div>开元二十一年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367790_comment'></div>忠献公捐馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367790_comment'></div>茕然在疚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367790_comment'></div>哀越乎礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367790_comment'></div>会执事者丑正作福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367790_comment'></div>怙宠匿怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367790_comment'></div>乃因丧乘衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367790_comment'></div>将逞憾于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367790_comment'></div>言之如簧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367790_comment'></div>上亦投杼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367790_comment'></div>公乃衔恤进牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367790_comment'></div>叫阍抗愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367790_comment'></div>危言自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367790_comment'></div>至诚旁感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367790_comment'></div>由是宗祏垂祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367790_comment'></div>高天听回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367790_comment'></div>恩方照微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367790_comment'></div>神亦悔祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367790_comment'></div>卒令臧孙有加等之葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367790_comment'></div>公业有不忘之叹。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367790_comment'></div>书法不隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367790_comment'></div>开元二十四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367790_comment'></div>三庶人以罪废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367790_comment'></div>事出宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367790_comment'></div>变生飞语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367790_comment'></div>时寿王以母宠子爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367790_comment'></div>议者颇有夺宗之嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367790_comment'></div>道路悯默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367790_comment'></div>朝野疑惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367790_comment'></div>公乃从容请间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367790_comment'></div>慷慨献谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367790_comment'></div>上述新城之殷鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367790_comment'></div>下陈戾园之元龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1367790_comment'></div>谓兴亡之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1367790_comment'></div>在废立之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1367790_comment'></div>天子感悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1367790_comment'></div>改容以谢。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1367790_comment'></div>为日固久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1367790_comment'></div>今臣一言而荷殊宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1367790_comment'></div>则言者众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1367790_comment'></div>何以锡之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1367790_comment'></div>上善其敏而多其让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1367790_comment'></div>乃止不拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1367790_comment'></div>寻除尚书祠部员外郎。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1367790_comment'></div>因为已任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1367790_comment'></div>于时搢绅高议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1367790_comment'></div>方以青云期公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1367790_comment'></div>不吊昊天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1367790_comment'></div>降此短历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1367790_comment'></div>开元二十九年某月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1367790_comment'></div>薨于私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1367790_comment'></div>春秋若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1367790_comment'></div>君子谓公貂蝉之叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1367790_comment'></div>瑚琏之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1367790_comment'></div>寿不及黄耇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1367790_comment'></div>名不登明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1367790_comment'></div>天其未亡狐赵之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1367790_comment'></div>成宣之德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1367790_comment'></div>非昌其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1367790_comment'></div>必大于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1367790_comment'></div>果介繁祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1367790_comment'></div>有才子四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1367790_comment'></div>长曰倩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1367790_comment'></div>尚书驾部员外郎兼殿中侍御史江西道租庸盐铁等使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1367790_comment'></div>次曰儆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1367790_comment'></div>尚书司勋员外郎兼殿中侍御史参中军元帅雍王军事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1367790_comment'></div>次曰倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1367790_comment'></div>殿中侍御史试守万年县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1367790_comment'></div>季曰侑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1367790_comment'></div>太原府榆次县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1367790_comment'></div>构厦瑰材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1367790_comment'></div>切玉利器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1367790_comment'></div>价敌三虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1367790_comment'></div>族拟八王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1367790_comment'></div>朝廷褎之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1367790_comment'></div>方倚以成务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1367790_comment'></div>元年春建辰月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1367790_comment'></div>肆大眚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1367790_comment'></div>命有司录勋追旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1367790_comment'></div>于是诏赠公谏议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1367790_comment'></div>犹以礼未超伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1367790_comment'></div>位不充德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1367790_comment'></div>秋八月下诏曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1367790_comment'></div>赠谏议大夫裴某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1367790_comment'></div>操履贞纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1367790_comment'></div>器能温敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1367790_comment'></div>素推雅望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1367790_comment'></div>尝践清班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1367790_comment'></div>志业屈于当时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1367790_comment'></div>风猷悲于既往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1367790_comment'></div>顾其允嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1367790_comment'></div>久在周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1367790_comment'></div>虽礼及前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1367790_comment'></div>已申追远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1367790_comment'></div>而恩沾后命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1367790_comment'></div>宜有赠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1367790_comment'></div>俾高列岳之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1367790_comment'></div>更表重泉之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1367790_comment'></div>可赠使持节陕州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1367790_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1367790_comment'></div>公天机超迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1367790_comment'></div>雅有大略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1367790_comment'></div>气直而温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1367790_comment'></div>性扰而毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1367790_comment'></div>贞可干事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1367790_comment'></div>善足救物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1367790_comment'></div>外坦荡豪举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1367790_comment'></div>朗然不羁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1367790_comment'></div>内敦敏纯固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1367790_comment'></div>忠而能力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1367790_comment'></div>至若轻死重义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1367790_comment'></div>贵身贱名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1367790_comment'></div>视钱帛如粪土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1367790_comment'></div>戏公卿若草芥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1367790_comment'></div>其于履危机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1367790_comment'></div>临大节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1367790_comment'></div>则气冠贲育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1367790_comment'></div>劲侔风霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1367790_comment'></div>未尝以得丧夷险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1367790_comment'></div>虿芥于胸臆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1367790_comment'></div>诗云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1367790_comment'></div>昭明有融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1367790_comment'></div>高朗令终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1367790_comment'></div>公实有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1367790_comment'></div>谓宜荷天之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1367790_comment'></div>俾炽而大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1367790_comment'></div>龙泉未试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1367790_comment'></div>隙驷先往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1367790_comment'></div>天乎斯才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1367790_comment'></div>而有斯寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1367790_comment'></div>今宠优八命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1367790_comment'></div>泽及九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1367790_comment'></div>已申追远之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1367790_comment'></div>请遵易名之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1367790_comment'></div>宝应二年某月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1367790_comment'></div>故吏某官某谨上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_198_1367790_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送贺若员外巡按毕归朝序</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367684")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367684'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367684'>今年春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367684_comment'></div>上以富人侯为丞相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367684_comment'></div>百揆时叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367684_comment'></div>九州赋错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367684_comment'></div>方欲齐职贡之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367684_comment'></div>崇厎慎之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367684_comment'></div>使六府修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367684_comment'></div>九叙成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367684_comment'></div>谓尚书吏部郎贺若公贞明直躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367684_comment'></div>特达公器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367684_comment'></div>才足以茂功蒇事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367684_comment'></div>政足以宏道救物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367684_comment'></div>故俾绣衣持斧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367684_comment'></div>巡抚江介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367684_comment'></div>分王命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367684_comment'></div>公电发神机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367684_comment'></div>霜淬智刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367684_comment'></div>其始至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367684_comment'></div>问谣俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367684_comment'></div>省疾苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367684_comment'></div>命司书示年数之上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367684_comment'></div>削郡县之版图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367684_comment'></div>且为之实其多与寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367684_comment'></div>以差等井赋焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367684_comment'></div>然后劳之来之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367684_comment'></div>安之集之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367684_comment'></div>俾其有宁宇而族聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367684_comment'></div>以宣天子之宏恩而煦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367684_comment'></div>于是乎民之乐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367684_comment'></div>如饥者之得以食也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367684_comment'></div>寒者之获以纩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367684_comment'></div>乃使苞茅之贡必叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367684_comment'></div>而杼轴之诗亦不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367684_comment'></div>冬十一月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367684_comment'></div>爰命郡吏致事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367684_comment'></div>言旋于京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367684_comment'></div>且将捧府檄于南陔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367684_comment'></div>侍版舆以西上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367684_comment'></div>事有成而功不伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367684_comment'></div>以是觐扬天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367684_comment'></div>以尽考绩之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367684_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367684_comment'></div>夫其由家以及于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367684_comment'></div>资事亲以事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367684_comment'></div>甘旨之未遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367684_comment'></div>勤于王家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367684_comment'></div>奔走之不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367684_comment'></div>以显亲身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367684_comment'></div>斯真能奉慈训不废陈力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367684_comment'></div>将君命不违色养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367684_comment'></div>忠孝之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367684_comment'></div>又人子人臣之所难及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367684_comment'></div>而况奸宄已弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367684_comment'></div>干戈将戢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367684_comment'></div>天子方以律令章程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367684_comment'></div>责成三府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367684_comment'></div>然则操六辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367684_comment'></div>骤四骆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367684_comment'></div>周爰咨询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367684_comment'></div>以成天下之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367684_comment'></div>在是行乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367684_comment'></div>翰飞方骋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367684_comment'></div>瞻望何及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367684_comment'></div>唯献酬东阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367684_comment'></div>弼成大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367684_comment'></div>使烝人粒海水静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367684_comment'></div>农夫高枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367684_comment'></div>及亦预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367684_comment'></div>凡执手于路者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367684_comment'></div>请偕赋鸿雁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367684_comment'></div>取之子于征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367684_comment'></div>劬劳于野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367684_comment'></div>爰及矜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367684_comment'></div>哀此𩻴寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367684_comment'></div>以为善颂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1367684_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367633' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367633' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367633?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺袁傪破贼表</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367633")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367633_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367633'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367633'>臣某等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367633_comment'></div>臣等伏见河南副元帅行军司马太子右庶子兼御史中丞袁傪露布奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367633_comment'></div>今年五月十七日破石埭城贼方清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367633_comment'></div>并降乌石山贼陈㽵等徒党二万五千五百人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367633_comment'></div>臣閒圣人之生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367633_comment'></div>不能使大盗不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367633_comment'></div>故唐虞之代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367633_comment'></div>时则有三苗之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367633_comment'></div>奸宄草窃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367633_comment'></div>为患旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367633_comment'></div>山贼方清等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367633_comment'></div>蕞尔狂狡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367633_comment'></div>敢干天诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367633_comment'></div>聚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1367633", 1367633, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>椎剽</span>之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367633_comment'></div>谓险远可恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367633_comment'></div>作为蛇豕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367633_comment'></div>以荐食勾吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367633_comment'></div>乃有跨据大江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367633_comment'></div>吞噬东土之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367633_comment'></div>七州之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367633_comment'></div>人罢耕织。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367633_comment'></div>百姓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1367633", 1367633, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>业业</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367633_comment'></div>全活无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367633_comment'></div>陛下方<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1367633", 1367633, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>锐志</span>于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1367633", 1367633, "Clauses/23/Comments/1")'>偃武</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367633_comment'></div>不得已而用兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367633_comment'></div>乃命将受略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367633_comment'></div>使先胜后战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367633_comment'></div>故傪等役不再举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367633_comment'></div>而师有成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367633_comment'></div>巢窟皆倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367633_comment'></div>俾无遗类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367633_comment'></div>诖误之辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367633_comment'></div>得返故业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367633_comment'></div>污俗更始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367633_comment'></div>流人汔康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367633_comment'></div>此三代之举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367633_comment'></div>非陛下齐圣格天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367633_comment'></div>文思柔远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367633_comment'></div>岂能厎绥盗乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367633_comment'></div>如此其速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367633_comment'></div>臣等幸睹成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367633_comment'></div>不胜大庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367633_comment'></div>臣无任抃跃之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1367633_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f12e907ca8da46c89ee0e63750977533_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=768')">765-768年</a>，41-44岁</div><div id='f12e907ca8da46c89ee0e63750977533' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年3月</a>　在左拾遗任，三月，上谏表论政，代宗不能用。作品：《直谏表》<div id='poem_1367638' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367638' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367638?labeling=true' target='_blank'>直谏表</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367638")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367638_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367638'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367638'>臣等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367638_comment'></div>伏见陛下屡发德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367638_comment'></div>招延献纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367638_comment'></div>使左右侍臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367638_comment'></div>得直言极谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367638_comment'></div>忠謇者无不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367638_comment'></div>狂讦者无不容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367638_comment'></div>又辛丑诏书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367638_comment'></div>诏裴冕崔涣等十有三人并集贤殿待制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367638_comment'></div>以备询事考言之问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367638_comment'></div>此五帝之盛德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367638_comment'></div>而臣以目睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367638_comment'></div>生则幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367638_comment'></div>然顷者陛下虽容其直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367638_comment'></div>而不用其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367638_comment'></div>进匦上封者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367638_comment'></div>大抵皆事寝不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367638_comment'></div>书留不下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367638_comment'></div>但有容谏之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367638_comment'></div>竟无听谏之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367638_comment'></div>遂使谏者稍稍自引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367638_comment'></div>钳口就列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367638_comment'></div>饱食偷安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367638_comment'></div>相招为禄仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367638_comment'></div>此忠鲠之士所以窃叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367638_comment'></div>而臣亦耻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367638_comment'></div>十室之邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367638_comment'></div>必有忠信如孔某者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367638_comment'></div>况以朝廷之大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367638_comment'></div>卿大夫之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367638_comment'></div>而陛下选受之精与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367638_comment'></div>假令不能如文王之多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367638_comment'></div>尧舜之比屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367638_comment'></div>其中岂不有温故知新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367638_comment'></div>可使懋陈政要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367638_comment'></div>而亿则屡中者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367638_comment'></div>陛下唯虚存其仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367638_comment'></div>令条奏不旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367638_comment'></div>及议政之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367638_comment'></div>曾不采其一说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367638_comment'></div>尧之畴咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367638_comment'></div>禹之昌言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367638_comment'></div>岂若是耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367638_comment'></div>昔尧设谤木于五达之衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367638_comment'></div>孔子亦曰以能问于不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367638_comment'></div>以多问于寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367638_comment'></div>又曰某也幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367638_comment'></div>苟有过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367638_comment'></div>人必知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367638_comment'></div>然则多闻阙疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367638_comment'></div>不耻下问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367638_comment'></div>圣人之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367638_comment'></div>臣不胜大愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367638_comment'></div>愿陛下试以尧孔之心为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367638_comment'></div>日降清问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367638_comment'></div>启其宏议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367638_comment'></div>不可者罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367638_comment'></div>可者议之于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367638_comment'></div>与执事者共之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367638_comment'></div>使知之必言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367638_comment'></div>言之必行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367638_comment'></div>行之必公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367638_comment'></div>则君臣无私论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367638_comment'></div>朝廷无私政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367638_comment'></div>天下无私是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367638_comment'></div>陛下以此辨可否于献替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367638_comment'></div>而建太平之阶可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367638_comment'></div>况国体乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367638_comment'></div>自师兴不息十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367638_comment'></div>万姓之生产空于杼轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367638_comment'></div>拥兵者第馆亘街陌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367638_comment'></div>奴婢厌酒肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367638_comment'></div>而贫人羸饿就役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367638_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1367638", 1367638, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>剥肤及髓</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367638_comment'></div>长安城中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367638_comment'></div>白昼椎剽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367638_comment'></div>京兆尹不敢诘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367638_comment'></div>加以官乱职废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367638_comment'></div>将惰卒暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367638_comment'></div>百揆隳刺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367638_comment'></div>如纷麻沸粥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367638_comment'></div>百姓不敢诉于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367638_comment'></div>有司不敢闻于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_82_1367638", 1367638, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>天听</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367638_comment'></div>士庶茹毒饮痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367638_comment'></div>穷而无告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367638_comment'></div>今其心禺禺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367638_comment'></div>独恃于麦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367638_comment'></div>麦不登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367638_comment'></div>则易子咬骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367638_comment'></div>可跂而待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1367638_comment'></div>眠于焚薪之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1367638_comment'></div>岂危于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1367638_comment'></div>陛下不以此时轸薄冰朽索之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1367638_comment'></div>励精更始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1367638_comment'></div>思所以救之之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1367638_comment'></div>忍令宗庙有累卵之危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1367638_comment'></div>万姓悼心而失图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1367638_comment'></div>臣实惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1367638_comment'></div>去岁十二月丁巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1367638_comment'></div>夜中星陨如雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1367638_comment'></div>昨者清明降霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1367638_comment'></div>三月苦热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1367638_comment'></div>寒暑气候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1367638_comment'></div>错缪颠倒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1367638_comment'></div>沴莫大焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1367638_comment'></div>岂下凌上替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1367638_comment'></div>怨讟之气焰以取之耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1367638_comment'></div>不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1367638_comment'></div>天意之丁宁谴诫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1367638_comment'></div>以此儆陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1367638_comment'></div>宜反躬罪已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1367638_comment'></div>旁求贤良者而师友之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1367638_comment'></div>黜弃贪佞不肖而窃位者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1367638_comment'></div>下哀痛之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1367638_comment'></div>去天下所疾苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1367638_comment'></div>废无用之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1367638_comment'></div>罢不急之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1367638_comment'></div>禁止暴兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1367638_comment'></div>节用爱人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1367638_comment'></div>罔使宦官乱国政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1367638_comment'></div>佞言败厥度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1367638_comment'></div>兢兢乾乾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1367638_comment'></div>以徼福于上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1367638_comment'></div>必能使天諴感而神心应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1367638_comment'></div>反妖灾以为和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1367638_comment'></div>彼太戊<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_125_1367638", 1367638, "Clauses/125/Comments/0")'>桑谷</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1367638_comment'></div>宋景荧惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1367638_comment'></div>焉足为陛下道哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1367638_comment'></div>臣一昨陈奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1367638_comment'></div>请减江淮山南等诸道兵马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1367638_comment'></div>以赡国用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1367638_comment'></div>陛下初不以臣言为愚妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1367638_comment'></div>许即施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1367638_comment'></div>然及今竟未有沛然之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1367638_comment'></div>臣窃迟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1367638_comment'></div>今天下唯朔方陇西有吐蕃仆固之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1367638_comment'></div>邠泾凤翔等兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1367638_comment'></div>足当之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1367638_comment'></div>自此而往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1367638_comment'></div>东洎海南至番禺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1367638_comment'></div>西尽巴蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1367638_comment'></div>万里无鼠窃之盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1367638_comment'></div>已积岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1367638_comment'></div>而兵不为之解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1367638_comment'></div>倾天下之货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1367638_comment'></div>竭天下之谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1367638_comment'></div>以给不用之军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1367638_comment'></div>而为无端之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1367638_comment'></div>臣不知其故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1367638_comment'></div>假令居安思危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1367638_comment'></div>用备不虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1367638_comment'></div>自可于阨要之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1367638_comment'></div>少置<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_152_1367638", 1367638, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>屯御</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1367638_comment'></div>馀悉休之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1367638_comment'></div>以其粮储<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_154_1367638", 1367638, "Clauses/154/Comments/0")'>屝屦</span>之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1367638_comment'></div>充疲人贡赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1367638_comment'></div>岁可减国赋之半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1367638_comment'></div>陛下岂迟疑于改作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1367638_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_158_1367638", 1367638, "Clauses/158/Comments/0")'>逡巡</span>于旧贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1367638_comment'></div>使大议有所壅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1367638_comment'></div>而率土之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1367638_comment'></div>日甚一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1367638_comment'></div>是益其弊而厚其疾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1367638_comment'></div>臣窃惑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1367638_comment'></div>夫疗痈者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1367638_comment'></div>必决之使溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1367638_comment'></div>今兵之为患犹痈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1367638_comment'></div>不以渐戢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1367638_comment'></div>其害滋大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1367638_comment'></div>大而图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1367638_comment'></div>必力倍而功寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1367638_comment'></div>岂周易不俟终日之义与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1367638_comment'></div>伏惟图其始而要其终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1367638_comment'></div>天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1367638_comment'></div>臣无任恳款之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_174_1367638_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　在左拾遗任。作品：《贺潞州芝草表》<div id='poem_1367637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367637?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺潞州芝草嘉禾表</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367637")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367637_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367637'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367637'>臣某等言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367637_comment'></div>臣伏见陈郑泽潞陇右节度使奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367637_comment'></div>潞州使院行军司马裴政厅事柱上生紫芝草七茎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367637_comment'></div>长子县厚载乡生嘉禾两茎同一穗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367637_comment'></div>臣闻灵芝嘉禾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367637_comment'></div>太平之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367637_comment'></div>昔在周汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367637_comment'></div>尝表休徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367637_comment'></div>当时福应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367637_comment'></div>疾如影响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367637_comment'></div>今庶政方乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367637_comment'></div>而二瑞荐臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367637_comment'></div>是天降殊祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367637_comment'></div>用彰有德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367637_comment'></div>岂非陛下宝持慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367637_comment'></div>辑柔远迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367637_comment'></div>克俾天下和平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367637_comment'></div>当如周汉之盛乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367637_comment'></div>神祇景贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367637_comment'></div>实甚昭晰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367637_comment'></div>彼唐叔之献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367637_comment'></div>与斋房之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367637_comment'></div>明德所感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367637_comment'></div>古今同契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367637_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1367637_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　在左拾遗任，有文送李抱真赴镇。作品：《送泽州李使君兼侍御史充泽潞陈郑节度副使赴本道序》<div id='poem_1367691' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367691' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367691?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送泽州李使君兼侍御史充泽潞陈郑节度副使赴本道序</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367691")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367691_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367691'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367691'>今岁皇帝择可以守四方之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367691_comment'></div>分命大司徒凉公作蕃汧阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367691_comment'></div>平秩西夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367691_comment'></div>凉公季弟曰抱真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367691_comment'></div>敬事好学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367691_comment'></div>仁勇忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367691_comment'></div>凡仁则不偷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367691_comment'></div>勇则不挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367691_comment'></div>忠则能宣力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367691_comment'></div>信则人任焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367691_comment'></div>故天子器之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367691_comment'></div>方倚以胥附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367691_comment'></div>使宅高平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367691_comment'></div>绥厥有众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367691_comment'></div>董次将之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367691_comment'></div>且以柱后惠文冠冠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367691_comment'></div>诏下之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367691_comment'></div>军府胥悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367691_comment'></div>盖萧何守关中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367691_comment'></div>举宗诣军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367691_comment'></div>而凉公荷方召之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367691_comment'></div>亦以爱弟居东旅于行间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367691_comment'></div>忠之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367691_comment'></div>夫高平上党之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367691_comment'></div>当赵魏燕代潞之咽喉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367691_comment'></div>太行恒山为之襟带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367691_comment'></div>公居有专城之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367691_comment'></div>行有亚旅之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367691_comment'></div>其略足以固其封疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367691_comment'></div>其惠足以柔其民人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367691_comment'></div>勖哉夫子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367691_comment'></div>进吾往也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367691_comment'></div>伯兮仲兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367691_comment'></div>执兵之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367691_comment'></div>谨身以肥家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367691_comment'></div>自家以刑国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367691_comment'></div>高平之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367691_comment'></div>可以未行而窥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367691_comment'></div>彼瞻望伫立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367691_comment'></div>壮夫耻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367691_comment'></div>非歌诗莫足以赠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1367691_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年6月</a>　在左拾遗任，有文送梁公镇归幕府。作品：《送梁郎中奏事毕归幕府序》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　在左拾遗任。作品：《吏部郎中厅壁记》《金刚经报应述并序》《送韦员外充副元帅判官之东都序》《送孙侍御赴凤翔幕府序》《江州刺史厅壁记》《为元相祭严尚书文》《为郭令公请停亲征表》<div id='poem_1367731' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367731' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367731?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吏部郎中厅壁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367731")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367731_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367731'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367731'>太微五帝星座后十五星曰郎位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367731_comment'></div>秦汉之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367731_comment'></div>则而象之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367731_comment'></div>乃建郎官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367731_comment'></div>至魏世祖分尚书曹为六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367731_comment'></div>郎各六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367731_comment'></div>今之吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367731_comment'></div>魏之选曹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367731_comment'></div>掌选举铨覈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367731_comment'></div>以正公卿大夫士群吏之品位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367731_comment'></div>凡废置之柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367731_comment'></div>官府之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367731_comment'></div>岁终令天下郡县会计致事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367731_comment'></div>而郎官起草立议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367731_comment'></div>操而成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367731_comment'></div>然后尚书受成于郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367731_comment'></div>郎中之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367731_comment'></div>非楚金百鍊玈弓六钧弗与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367731_comment'></div>故居官者不由选曹而进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367731_comment'></div>罔以见其才之馀地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367731_comment'></div>亦犹剑刀之刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367731_comment'></div>未尝刲大軱切大玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367731_comment'></div>则虽曰我且必为镆铘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367731_comment'></div>人犹疑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367731_comment'></div>由其途而升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367731_comment'></div>必骤周三台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367731_comment'></div>翰飞两掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367731_comment'></div>登喉舌秉刀尺者什六七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367731_comment'></div>诸曹郎莫敌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367731_comment'></div>岁在乙已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367731_comment'></div>河南贺若公用贞干谅直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367731_comment'></div>实莅厥位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367731_comment'></div>往岁公为员外郎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367731_comment'></div>东曹朗然如得水镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367731_comment'></div>治馀杭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367731_comment'></div>吴人熙熙若逢阳春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367731_comment'></div>今也来斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367731_comment'></div>八法在手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367731_comment'></div>操割成务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367731_comment'></div>弥纶旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367731_comment'></div>悉如初政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367731_comment'></div>尝以前哲轨躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367731_comment'></div>我之韦弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367731_comment'></div>而武德以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367731_comment'></div>廨署鼎新者数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367731_comment'></div>官曹易名者五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367731_comment'></div>若姓不表年不纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367731_comment'></div>是废德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367731_comment'></div>将来何观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367731_comment'></div>故谨而列之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367731_comment'></div>俾我曹之春秋存乎座右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367731_comment'></div>其选部司列天官文部之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367731_comment'></div>各因其所革时之先后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367731_comment'></div>冠于其首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367731_comment'></div>以为志云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1367731_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367752' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367752' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367752?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金刚经报应述</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367752")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367752_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367752'>洪州牧刑部尚书兼御史大夫魏公。身挂元冕。心冥真如。昔尝奉般若法。以宏正见。虽颠沛造次。心与经俱。十有若干年矣。皇帝中元年冬十月。车驾有避狄之师。百僚仓皇。南驰商于。公为盗所攘。而亡其经。其往也。匪家之念。惟经是悼。行与其获七宝也。宁见经。生与其亡四句也。宁舍身。明年王正月。大驾返正。公为京兆尹。痛宏誓之未从也。则惟经是图。末于元法寺之藏。藏人以送。公发函披卷。乃商于所亡之本也。问守藏者。亦曰不知其所自而能得。公瞻礼悲喜。捧持而泣。然后知精专感达。故随心而至。昭报肸蚃。其疾若答。顾谓孟子太常博士友顺志之。或曰。得与丧。偶然尔。何必谓诚感乎。及对曰。诚于此者形于彼。故出其言善。千里之外应之。此仁义忠信感于物者也。况第一义谛。超贯仁义。自在慧力。不啻忠信。则因发而果从。心诚而经还。是法味幽赞。非思议所可及。岂佛以般若之雨。启公善牙。使因相以次获愿。进启乎无愿法之法欤。不然。何心境元合。若律吕相召。岁在乙酉。公以异见告。及跪而述之曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367752_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367752'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367752'>上士勤道。精应若驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367752_comment'></div>愿形于心。报亦随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367752_comment'></div>至感无碍。经斯来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367752_comment'></div>护公身田。俾公断疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367752_comment'></div>公之善根。畴可度思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367752_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1367752_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367688' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367688' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367688?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送韦员外充副元帅判官之东都序</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367688")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367688_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367688'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367688'>太尉临淮王之秉旄淮沂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367688_comment'></div>天子命公为介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367688_comment'></div>洎临淮薨而相国太原公继授兵符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367688_comment'></div>尽护东夏诸将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367688_comment'></div>亦表公参成周军事如初命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367688_comment'></div>故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367688_comment'></div>登掖垣者不驱传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367688_comment'></div>居谏臣者不就辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367688_comment'></div>将使其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367688_comment'></div>必易其秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367688_comment'></div>故自左补阙为尚书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367688_comment'></div>元年仲春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367688_comment'></div>始以使节赴洛阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367688_comment'></div>经大盗虔刘之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367688_comment'></div>顽民虽迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367688_comment'></div>污俗未返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367688_comment'></div>三军之心注于帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367688_comment'></div>帅之耳目属于参佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367688_comment'></div>以公贞谅文敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367688_comment'></div>能恤大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367688_comment'></div>且成宣之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367688_comment'></div>故以部从事咨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367688_comment'></div>夫民残则讹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367688_comment'></div>讹则流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367688_comment'></div>禁流莫若以德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367688_comment'></div>兵不戢则玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367688_comment'></div>玩则暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367688_comment'></div>禁暴莫若以信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367688_comment'></div>建信与德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367688_comment'></div>以为幕中之画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367688_comment'></div>繄吾子是冀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367688_comment'></div>将贺不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367688_comment'></div>别于何有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367688_comment'></div>我饮饯者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367688_comment'></div>姑以诗代路车乘马。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1367688_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367689' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367689' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367689?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送孙侍御赴凤翔幕府序</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367689")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367689_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367689'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367689'>右扶风之地。枕跨陇蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367689_comment'></div>扼秦西门。帝命司徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367689_comment'></div>为唐方叔。开府之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367689_comment'></div>搜贤自贰。于是孙侯以监察御史领司徒掾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367689_comment'></div>夫子卿族也。用文学缵绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367689_comment'></div>而兄弟皆材。伯曰宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367689_comment'></div>以秋官郎辟丞相府。仲曰绛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367689_comment'></div>拾遗君前。及余为寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367689_comment'></div>夫子则以贞干肃恪之能。入主方书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367689_comment'></div>出佐戎政。花萼灼于三台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367689_comment'></div>时人荣之。二月丙午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367689_comment'></div>乘传诣部。人谓扶风于是乎有三幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367689_comment'></div>获白额而南山有采藜藿者。一幸也<span class='inlineComment2'>（先是司徒于南山擒贼帅高玉）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367689_comment'></div>今夫操兵者如虎。而司徒仁而爱人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367689_comment'></div>二幸也。其府君则贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367689_comment'></div>其幕府多士。而孙侯懿之以文德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367689_comment'></div>三幸也。恪于德以临事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367689_comment'></div>度于义以从政。力于忠以成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367689_comment'></div>吾子勉之。其蔑不济矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367689_comment'></div>士为知已者用。岂干荣乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367689_comment'></div>请居者歌之。子其行乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367689_comment'></div>君子赠人以言。亦以是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367689_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1367689_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367734' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367734' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367734?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江州刺史厅壁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367734")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367734_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367734'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367734'>古者国有史氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367734_comment'></div>君举必书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367734_comment'></div>倚相董狐史䲡史嚚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367734_comment'></div>即其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367734_comment'></div>秦已来国化为郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367734_comment'></div>史官废职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367734_comment'></div>策牍之制寖灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367734_comment'></div>记事者但用名氏岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367734_comment'></div>书于公堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367734_comment'></div>而春秋梼杌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367734_comment'></div>存乎屋壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367734_comment'></div>其来旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367734_comment'></div>是州也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367734_comment'></div>在荆之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367734_comment'></div>于浔之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367734_comment'></div>江从岷山东注渤澥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367734_comment'></div>洪涛至是派分为九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367734_comment'></div>而庐山湓水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367734_comment'></div>周于雉堞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367734_comment'></div>洞庭彭蠡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367734_comment'></div>为之襟带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367734_comment'></div>故自晋元康讫于梁陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367734_comment'></div>出入五代四百馀载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367734_comment'></div>世称<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1367734", 1367734, id='poem_sentence_25_1367734_comment'></div>莫荷其寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367734_comment'></div>唐有天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367734_comment'></div>六合一轨。<div id='poem_sentence_45_1367734_comment'></div>功倍他郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367734_comment'></div>故亦大其任而难其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367734_comment'></div>今年春。<div id='poem_sentence_50_1367734_comment'></div>得于手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367734_comment'></div>应于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367734_comment'></div>则盘曲拥肿。<div id='poem_sentence_75_1367734_comment'></div>善恶成败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367734_comment'></div>我之元龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367734_comment'></div>酌而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367734_comment'></div>吾师存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367734_comment'></div>于是徵诸故老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367734_comment'></div>鸠其名氏之存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367734_comment'></div>凡若干人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367734_comment'></div>揭而书之。<div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367792'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367792'>年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367792_comment'></div>某官某乙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367792_comment'></div>谨以清酌少牢之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367792_comment'></div>敬祭于黄门侍郎兼吏部尚书御史大夫严公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367792_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367792_comment'></div>天惟匪忱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367792_comment'></div>才不必寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367792_comment'></div>冉耕斯疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367792_comment'></div>颜回短命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367792_comment'></div>吉凶兆眹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367792_comment'></div>凡圣共惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367792_comment'></div>惟公茂质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367792_comment'></div>见于芳年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367792_comment'></div>菌蠢九葩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367792_comment'></div>磊砢千丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367792_comment'></div>顷尝戮力当代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367792_comment'></div>以智开物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367792_comment'></div>若发硎之刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367792_comment'></div>决云切泥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367792_comment'></div>长安浩穰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367792_comment'></div>宪网疏漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367792_comment'></div>天子命公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367792_comment'></div>尹京执法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367792_comment'></div>能秉直道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367792_comment'></div>以张皇纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367792_comment'></div>盗奔讼清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367792_comment'></div>周月报政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367792_comment'></div>巴蜀亟扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367792_comment'></div>上为旰食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367792_comment'></div>公之攸徂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367792_comment'></div>乱亦遄已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367792_comment'></div>昆夷授首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367666_comment'></div>窃谓非便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367666_comment'></div>凶虏伤沮。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367666_comment'></div>陛下责成之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367666_comment'></div>愚臣死难之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367666_comment'></div>伏望付臣以专征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367666_comment'></div>委臣以集事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367666_comment'></div>回銮上国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367666_comment'></div>端拱中朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367666_comment'></div>岂惟微臣受赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367666_comment'></div>抑亦万方幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367666_comment'></div>谨奉表以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1367666_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年11月</a>　在左拾遗任，有文送郭英乂赴镇剑南。作品：《送成都成少尹赴蜀序》<div id='poem_1367693' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367693' class='poemTitle class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367693_comment'></div>谋亚尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367693_comment'></div>佥曰左司郎成公可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367693_comment'></div>温良而文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367693_comment'></div>贞固能干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367693_comment'></div>力足以参大略。<div id='poem_sentence_20_1367693_comment'></div>姑务忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367693_comment'></div>夷险一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367693_comment'></div>患已不称于位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367693_comment'></div>于行迈乎何有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367693_comment'></div>言讫抗手。<div class='inline'
