class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367639_comment'></div>至于成立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367639_comment'></div>遭罹二京覆没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367639_comment'></div>弱弟以宗室见害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367639_comment'></div>臣茕然茹痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367639_comment'></div>独侍板舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367639_comment'></div>备尝险阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367639_comment'></div>冀及荣养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367639_comment'></div>才擢掖垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367639_comment'></div>慈颜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1367639", 1367639, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>违代</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367639_comment'></div>罔极之痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367639_comment'></div>终天莫追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367639_comment'></div>今灵筵未尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367639_comment'></div>坟土尚湿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367639_comment'></div>遽令臣荷金印之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367639_comment'></div>处黄华之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367639_comment'></div>使繐帷廓然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367639_comment'></div>奠祭无主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367639_comment'></div>此恒情之所不忍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367639_comment'></div>陛下其忍之乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367639_comment'></div>伏乞以圣慈曲临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367639_comment'></div>皇明下照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367639_comment'></div>矜臣尪瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367639_comment'></div>察臣不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367639_comment'></div>更择时彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367639_comment'></div>授之使职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367639_comment'></div>许臣得以羸骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367639_comment'></div>终其丧纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367639_comment'></div>实天地之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367639_comment'></div>钟于臣身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367639_comment'></div>倘残魂未灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367639_comment'></div>朽质可委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367639_comment'></div>誓当摩顶至踵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367639_comment'></div>以答圣造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1367639_comment'></div>臣无任哀瘵恳迫之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_90_1367639_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　在左拾遗任上，有文赞杨炎古松树画。作品：《杨起居画古松树赞》<div id='poem_1367743' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367743' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367743?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨起居画古松树赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367743")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367743_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367743'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367743'>道在毫末，神凝意注。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367743'>闯然雷生，千岁古树。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367743'>龙蠖屈盘，精魅固护。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367743'>霜封雪埋，翠幄如故。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367743'>宜构大厦，胡为中路。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367743'>岂犹有待，公输之顾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367743'>落落贞姿，传之绘素。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367743'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1367743_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　在左拾遗任上。作品：《唐故尚书库部郎中荥阳郑公墓志铭》《唐新平长公主故季女姜氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1367775' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367775' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367775?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故尚书库部郎中荥阳郑公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367775")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367775_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367775'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367775'>永泰元年六月四日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367775_comment'></div>尚书库部郎中郑公卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367775_comment'></div>春秋四十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367775_comment'></div>知旧茹痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367775_comment'></div>行路嗟悼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367775_comment'></div>谓公口无择言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367775_comment'></div>身无择行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367775_comment'></div>得乾之贞固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367775_comment'></div>损之元吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367775_comment'></div>坎之常德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367775_comment'></div>明夷之正志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367775_comment'></div>宜荷福履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367775_comment'></div>俾如山阜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367775_comment'></div>而秩止于三百石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367775_comment'></div>年不及知天命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367775_comment'></div>明神岂子欺乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367775_comment'></div>嗣子正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367775_comment'></div>藐然始孩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367775_comment'></div>孤穷何怙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367775_comment'></div>八月四日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367775_comment'></div>葬于先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367775_comment'></div>宗人家老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367775_comment'></div>于是乎以果行实录贲于丰石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367775_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367775_comment'></div>公讳宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367775_comment'></div>字若惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367775_comment'></div>荥阳开封人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367775_comment'></div>其先建国命氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367775_comment'></div>有郑世家言之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367775_comment'></div>大王父某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367775_comment'></div>澧州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367775_comment'></div>赠卫州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367775_comment'></div>卫州生襄阳令某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367775_comment'></div>襄阳生临汾令某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367775_comment'></div>临汾生郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367775_comment'></div>纯懿休祉之所丛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367775_comment'></div>贞亮忠厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367775_comment'></div>仁让孝敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367775_comment'></div>融明而温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367775_comment'></div>性与道并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367775_comment'></div>二十举明经高第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367775_comment'></div>解褐邺尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367775_comment'></div>太尉房公之由邺郡而为右扶风也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367775_comment'></div>表公茂才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367775_comment'></div>擢虢县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367775_comment'></div>虢土狭而人窳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367775_comment'></div>公用教化渍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367775_comment'></div>谓任力不及任人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367775_comment'></div>听讼不及使无讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367775_comment'></div>故以直宏道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367775_comment'></div>以信齐政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367775_comment'></div>以礼肃堕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367775_comment'></div>以让息竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367775_comment'></div>莅止一岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367775_comment'></div>虢人耻格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367775_comment'></div>至德二年拜监察御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367775_comment'></div>徙太原户曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367775_comment'></div>领平遥令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367775_comment'></div>真拜太谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367775_comment'></div>其在晋如在虢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367775_comment'></div>诏书劳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367775_comment'></div>锡以命服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367775_comment'></div>迁华原令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367775_comment'></div>拜尚书工部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367775_comment'></div>而唐人晋人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367775_comment'></div>犹歌咏盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367775_comment'></div>愿得公常居其邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367775_comment'></div>莫有由也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367775_comment'></div>太原守上其状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367775_comment'></div>诏迁太原少尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367775_comment'></div>未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367775_comment'></div>转库部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367775_comment'></div>凡历十官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367775_comment'></div>宰四县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367775_comment'></div>一持斧而再起草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367775_comment'></div>其政先道德而后刑法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367775_comment'></div>内精辨而外若讷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367775_comment'></div>戮力事上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367775_comment'></div>吐诚率下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367775_comment'></div>罔曲物而直已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367775_comment'></div>罔咈百姓以干名声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367775_comment'></div>惟畏清之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367775_comment'></div>善之彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367775_comment'></div>饮其教者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367775_comment'></div>忻然乐康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367775_comment'></div>而不知其惠之所由生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367775_comment'></div>与公游者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367775_comment'></div>靡亲靡疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367775_comment'></div>悉饱醇德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367775_comment'></div>而莫见其天机之弛张也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1367775_comment'></div>其学而知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1367775_comment'></div>惟济南之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1367775_comment'></div>淹中之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1367775_comment'></div>田何之易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1367775_comment'></div>胡毋之春秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1367775_comment'></div>酌其微言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1367775_comment'></div>以治其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1367775_comment'></div>身之治移于闺门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1367775_comment'></div>闺门之治移于官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1367775_comment'></div>官之治可移于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1367775_comment'></div>而寿不可踰于域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1367775_comment'></div>故位量未半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1367775_comment'></div>良史无述焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1367775_comment'></div>自古有死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1367775_comment'></div>彭殇同途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1367775_comment'></div>独有其身殁而其名存乎故老之口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1367775_comment'></div>此之谓不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1367775_comment'></div>不可以不识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1367775_comment'></div>其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1367775_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_109_1367775'>刚德干时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1367775_comment'></div>道家所忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1367775_comment'></div>抑抑郑公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1367775_comment'></div>直温柔毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1367775_comment'></div>众人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_113_1367775", 1367775, "Clauses/113/Comments/0")'>缺缺</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1367775_comment'></div>郑公见朴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1367775_comment'></div>众人昭昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1367775_comment'></div>郑公若浊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1367775_comment'></div>布政四邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1367775_comment'></div>四邑和乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1367775_comment'></div>雷震风偃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1367775_comment'></div>物亦允若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1367775_comment'></div>御史执法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1367775_comment'></div>郎官草奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1367775_comment'></div>郑公莅止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1367775_comment'></div>德音是茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1367775_comment'></div>于以经术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1367775_comment'></div>润色王度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1367775_comment'></div>宗族叙惇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1367775_comment'></div>乡党归仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1367775_comment'></div>孝谨之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1367775_comment'></div>万石之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1367775_comment'></div>兄也弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1367775_comment'></div>夭夭申申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1367775_comment'></div>善则无报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1367775_comment'></div>天地不仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1367775_comment'></div>抑抑郑公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1367775_comment'></div>执德之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1367775_comment'></div>生不近其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1367775_comment'></div>殁不隤其声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1367775_comment'></div>吁嗟乎郑公。</div><div id='poem_sentence_139_1367775_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367767' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367767' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367767?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐新平长公主故季女姜氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367767")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367767_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367767'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367767'>乙已岁四月二十六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367767_comment'></div>有唐新平长公主季女姜氏卒于京师昊天观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367767_comment'></div>五月六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367767_comment'></div>葬于某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367767_comment'></div>长公主叹季女姿度荣茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367767_comment'></div>温惠淑慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367767_comment'></div>能修女师之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367767_comment'></div>动中礼范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367767_comment'></div>其曾祖柔远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367767_comment'></div>位至尚书地官侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367767_comment'></div>祖皎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367767_comment'></div>以勋旧历太常秘书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367767_comment'></div>剖符封楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367767_comment'></div>其父庆初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367767_comment'></div>能践修祖考之耿光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367767_comment'></div>嗣爵旧国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367767_comment'></div>复居太常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367767_comment'></div>玄宗其外王父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367767_comment'></div>肃宗其舅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367767_comment'></div>天池波澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367767_comment'></div>泽润本根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367767_comment'></div>谓德钟下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367767_comment'></div>锡祉与寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367767_comment'></div>宜君子家室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367767_comment'></div>且贻芳于彤管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367767_comment'></div>乃未笄而夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367767_comment'></div>命也夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367767_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367767_comment'></div>窈窕专柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367767_comment'></div>含德而未形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367767_comment'></div>虽当鹊巢小星采蘩殷雷之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367767_comment'></div>今已矣夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367767_comment'></div>史氏蔑由记之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367767_comment'></div>长公主之恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367767_comment'></div>其庸可及乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367767_comment'></div>故月而日之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367767_comment'></div>铭诸坚石焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367767_comment'></div>其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367767_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1367767'>思娈季女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367767_comment'></div>生于公族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367767_comment'></div>禀懿德兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367767_comment'></div>天世其禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367767_comment'></div>不遐其福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367767_comment'></div>胡不淑兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367767_comment'></div>彭殇同躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367767_comment'></div>数不可续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367767_comment'></div>哀靡极兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1367767_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　迁太常博士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　在太常博士任。作品：《唐故范阳郡仓曹参军京兆韦公墓志铭》《敕与吐蕃赞普书》《请降诞日置天兴节表》《唐故右金吾卫将军河南阎公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1367777' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367777' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367777?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故范阳郡仓曹参军京兆韦公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367777")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367777_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367777'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367777'>永泰二年五月七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367777_comment'></div>有唐故衢州刺史鲁县子京兆韦璆第三子范阳郡仓曹参军讳元诚葬于少陵原先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367777_comment'></div>夫人范阳卢氏祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367777_comment'></div>从周礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367777_comment'></div>公少时为坊州参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367777_comment'></div>历襄州司法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367777_comment'></div>试守枣阳县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367777_comment'></div>真授蒙城令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367777_comment'></div>凡五迁至范阳仓曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367777_comment'></div>初安禄山以范阳叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367777_comment'></div>劫胁元元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367777_comment'></div>以杀整众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367777_comment'></div>士之因官因居而困窘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1367777", 1367777, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>颠踬</span>堕围中者数千计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367777_comment'></div>凶威所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367777_comment'></div>不死则污。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367777_comment'></div>公掾吏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367777_comment'></div>在伪署伍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367777_comment'></div>溷迹佯狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367777_comment'></div>冀以病免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367777_comment'></div>盗憎之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367777_comment'></div>乃加害焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367777_comment'></div>春秋若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367777_comment'></div>夫阳九厄会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367777_comment'></div>天地鞠凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367777_comment'></div>燎火炎冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367777_comment'></div>玉石何诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367777_comment'></div>是岁天宝十五年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367777_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367777_comment'></div>人皆筮仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367777_comment'></div>必以廉平公干称于州里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367777_comment'></div>人谁无死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367777_comment'></div>死则名不辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367777_comment'></div>志不夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367777_comment'></div>不咽盗哺以易其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367777_comment'></div>生且不苟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367777_comment'></div>其事亲事君之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367777_comment'></div>不待史氏而自明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367777_comment'></div>在官必闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367777_comment'></div>则居家正身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367777_comment'></div>与朋友临财之节可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367777_comment'></div>有子曰彤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367777_comment'></div>龙钟崎岖于险阻之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367777_comment'></div>十年不克返葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367777_comment'></div>哀有何极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367777_comment'></div>岁在乙已冬某月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367777_comment'></div>始跋涉太行恒山之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367777_comment'></div>以公之丧至自某郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367777_comment'></div>公季弟吏部郎中元曾既得吉卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367777_comment'></div>痛天伦之欢莫之追也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367777_comment'></div>愿以兄之忠于君恪于官友于家之德之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367777_comment'></div>以播后嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367777_comment'></div>庶几陵岸迁而德音不磨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367777_comment'></div>谬以及为习于礼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367777_comment'></div>故使之为志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367777_comment'></div>其词云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367777_comment'></div>天地横隤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367777_comment'></div>二象霾兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367777_comment'></div>枭獍择肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367777_comment'></div>鸑鷟惧兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367777_comment'></div>明夷于飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367777_comment'></div>罹其故兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367777_comment'></div>美玉宁折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367777_comment'></div>质不污兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367777_comment'></div>子子孙孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367777_comment'></div>荷馀裕兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1367777_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367626' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367626' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367626?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敕与吐蕃赞普书</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367626")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367626_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367626'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367626'>敕吐蕃赞普外甥。朕共赞普。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367626_comment'></div>代为与国。自我玄宗至道大明孝皇帝与生<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作甥）</span>赞普和亲结好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367626_comment'></div>将六十年。仰思当时之约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367626_comment'></div>岂为一朝之故。实欲相恤灾患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367626_comment'></div>永同休戚。使代代子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367626_comment'></div>为兄弟甥舅。如手足之相卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367626_comment'></div>唇齿之相依。自尔便息戍罢兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367626_comment'></div>二境无征战之苦。金玉绮绣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367626_comment'></div>问遗往来。道路相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367626_comment'></div>欢好不绝。赞普宁忘之乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367626_comment'></div>自我国家有安禄山史思明之难。朕谓言赞普必有恤邻救患之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367626_comment'></div>岂知乘我之舋。恣其侵轶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367626_comment'></div>煞略河湟之人。争夺汧陇之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367626_comment'></div>又与朕叛臣仆固怀恩共扇诱回纥等诸蕃。同恶相济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367626_comment'></div>犯我都邑。三年之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367626_comment'></div>三至城下。此实赞普苟窥分寸之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367626_comment'></div>自弃一家之信。不念婚姻之好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367626_comment'></div>忍绝甥舅之欢。累代亲邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367626_comment'></div>一朝并弃。有目有耳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367626_comment'></div>皆为赞普羞之。夫以小国伐大国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367626_comment'></div>且劳师袭远。而助叛臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367626_comment'></div>有是三者。神宜悔怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367626_comment'></div>果然怀恩自毙。回纥来降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367626_comment'></div>羌浑诸蕃。内难外散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367626_comment'></div>天实有眼。心可负乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367626_comment'></div>朕顷以背盟不祥。绝亲不义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367626_comment'></div>宁人负我。我不负人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367626_comment'></div>所以含垢数年。未忍致讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367626_comment'></div>既不得已。方思用师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367626_comment'></div>正欲悉天下精兵。长驱西向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367626_comment'></div>吊人问罪。然后凯旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367626_comment'></div>上以雪宗庙之雠耻。下以释将士之愤怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367626_comment'></div>自料以德征暴。以大攻小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367626_comment'></div>以信讨诈。以义伐不义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367626_comment'></div>当如沸汤沃雪。猛火焚枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367626_comment'></div>人神同力。何往不济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367626_comment'></div>筹议之次。适会彼国使来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367626_comment'></div>云愿修前好。复如旧日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367626_comment'></div>览书见意。良用怃然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367626_comment'></div>欲不许则人来归我。欲许则信不可恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367626_comment'></div>是以遣御史中丞杨济往谕朕意。且探诚款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367626_comment'></div>九月。济与彼国宰相某乙等同到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367626_comment'></div>得所寄书。然后知事皆由衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367626_comment'></div>言无虚谬。再披来旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367626_comment'></div>朕甚嘉之。何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367626_comment'></div>自非圣哲。人谁无过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367626_comment'></div>过而能改。亦古人之所善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367626_comment'></div>追思六十年之舅甥。有先祖先赞普之誓约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367626_comment'></div>言在史册。信结天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367626_comment'></div>岂以小不忍而隳大体。使百姓疲于甲兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367626_comment'></div>两主遂为仇雠。贰过迁怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367626_comment'></div>朕所不取。敬依来请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367626_comment'></div>彼此结和。而今而后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367626_comment'></div>不复念恶。已令内外屯戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367626_comment'></div>罢柝解严。凡我二国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367626_comment'></div>洗瑕迁善。经略封疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367626_comment'></div>素有分地。各守土宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367626_comment'></div>尔无有侵。永为亲好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367626_comment'></div>复如开元中故事。昊天上帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367626_comment'></div>山川鬼神。实闻朕言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367626_comment'></div>无谓不信。冬寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367626_comment'></div>赞普外甥比平安。遣书指不多及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367626_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1367626_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367634' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367634' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367634?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请降诞日置天兴节表</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367634")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367634_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367634'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367634'>臣某等言。臣闻天有春秋冬夏之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367634_comment'></div>时也。时有分至启闭之候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367634_comment'></div>节也。至若寒食上已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367634_comment'></div>端午重阳。或因人崇尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367634_comment'></div>亦播为风俗。况历运光启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367634_comment'></div>圣人降生。固宜纪载震之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367634_comment'></div>与八节同号。故玄宗生日命曰天长节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367634_comment'></div>肃宗生日命曰天平地成节。并以饮食宴乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367634_comment'></div>布庆万方。使赐及同轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367634_comment'></div>风流异代。陛下纂祖宗纯懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367634_comment'></div>与天地同德。礼乐克修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367634_comment'></div>宪章咸备。而圣诞之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367634_comment'></div>未有嘉名。将何以表出震之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367634_comment'></div>庆流虹之瑞。率土延企。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367634_comment'></div>思扇旧风。是以臣等禺禺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367634_comment'></div>不胜大愿。愿以十月十三日为天兴节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367634_comment'></div>其王公士庶。上寿作乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367634_comment'></div>悉如开元乾元故事。上以殷荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367634_comment'></div>崇先天不违之德。下以布泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367634_comment'></div>锡万代无疆之休。使凤鸣河清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367634_comment'></div>实在兹日。臣无任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367634_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1367634_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367778' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367778' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367778?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故左<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作右）</span>金吾卫将军河南阎公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1367778'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367778'>公讳用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367778_comment'></div>远祖曰文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367778_comment'></div>周昭王瑕之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367778_comment'></div>生而手有文曰阎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367778_comment'></div>康王奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367778_comment'></div>命封阎城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367778_comment'></div>文四十五代孙满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367778_comment'></div>仕后魏太祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367778_comment'></div>为诸曹大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367778_comment'></div>自马邑家河南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367778_comment'></div>其裔孙庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367778_comment'></div>在隋为少司空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367778_comment'></div>庆生毗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367778_comment'></div>毗生立本立德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367778_comment'></div>唐永徽中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367778_comment'></div>立本为中书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367778_comment'></div>立德为工部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367778_comment'></div>立德生元邃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367778_comment'></div>以司空尚书之馀裕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367778_comment'></div>官至泽州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367778_comment'></div>邃生巨源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367778_comment'></div>常宰射洪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367778_comment'></div>有仁政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367778_comment'></div>射洪人咏歌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367778_comment'></div>公射洪第二子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367778_comment'></div>温毅逊直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367778_comment'></div>廉恪宽信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367778_comment'></div>读论语老子周易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367778_comment'></div>被服其教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367778_comment'></div>初仕彭州参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367778_comment'></div>常摄督邮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367778_comment'></div>一日纠案本州𠌤谬不法数十事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367778_comment'></div>太守徐知人以为材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367778_comment'></div>后有诏择舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367778_comment'></div>以公魁伟爽悟有酝藉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367778_comment'></div>乃登其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367778_comment'></div>会戎侵我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367778_comment'></div>天子方爱人息战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367778_comment'></div>将以辞让屈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367778_comment'></div>诏公使西域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367778_comment'></div>以王命谕祸福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367778_comment'></div>戎人顿首请罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367778_comment'></div>介马不汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367778_comment'></div>戈鋋不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367778_comment'></div>而虏军却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367778_comment'></div>迁右卫郎将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367778_comment'></div>知引驾仗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367778_comment'></div>金吾将军李质上殿不解佩刀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367778_comment'></div>公呵下殿陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367778_comment'></div>请按以法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367778_comment'></div>左右皆震悚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367778_comment'></div>自是环卫加肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367778_comment'></div>先是有司以三卫执扇登殿引跸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367778_comment'></div>公奏曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367778_comment'></div>三卫皆趫悍有材力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367778_comment'></div>不当升阶陛迩御座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367778_comment'></div>请以宦者代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367778_comment'></div>上曰可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367778_comment'></div>遂为故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367778_comment'></div>天宝二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367778_comment'></div>册拜公长女为王子义王玭妃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367778_comment'></div>加公左骁卫将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367778_comment'></div>迁荣王傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367778_comment'></div>初玄宗惩诸侯王之国任事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367778_comment'></div>率多骄蹇不奉法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367778_comment'></div>而人受其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367778_comment'></div>故开元之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367778_comment'></div>皇子皇孙虽荷封建之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367778_comment'></div>未尝离阿保之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367778_comment'></div>悉无出宫閤任卿大夫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367778_comment'></div>公以为王居深宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367778_comment'></div>则傅相职废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367778_comment'></div>上疏陈古义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367778_comment'></div>请诸王申辅导之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367778_comment'></div>议虽废格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367778_comment'></div>上以为忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367778_comment'></div>公已白首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367778_comment'></div>位为将军诸侯傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367778_comment'></div>太夫人尚无恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367778_comment'></div>以银印赤绂侍朝夕膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367778_comment'></div>色难无违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367778_comment'></div>时人荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367778_comment'></div>太夫人捐馆舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367778_comment'></div>礼五十不毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367778_comment'></div>公泣血死孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367778_comment'></div>既免丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367778_comment'></div>天子复目以端士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367778_comment'></div>俾傅寿王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367778_comment'></div>加朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367778_comment'></div>上幸温泉。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1367778_comment'></div>公献四言诗十二章讽谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1367778_comment'></div>优诏褒叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1367778_comment'></div>后迁左金吾将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1367778_comment'></div>天宝十五载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1367778_comment'></div>二京<span id='poem_sentence_105_1367778_comment'></div>专静冲懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1367778_comment'></div>慈惠而明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1367778_comment'></div>用德礼以佐君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1367778_comment'></div>殁于私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1367778_comment'></div>殁六载而公薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1367778_comment'></div>事君之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1367778_comment'></div>资于爱亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1367778_comment'></div>以德资身。<div id='poem_sentence_143_1367778_comment'></div>仪刑闺门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1367778_comment'></div>礼乐是悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1367778_comment'></div>孝慈是敦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367639_comment'></div>冀回日月之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367639_comment'></div>曲念蝼蚁之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367639_comment'></div>伏奉丁酉诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367639_comment'></div>未蒙矜允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367639_comment'></div>捧读圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367639_comment'></div>五情殒裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367639_comment'></div>臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367639_comment'></div>伏以适四方宣王命之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367639_comment'></div>必择职位素贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367639_comment'></div>闻望炳著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367639_comment'></div>学能专对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367639_comment'></div>才有馀力者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367639_comment'></div>以充其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367639_comment'></div>臣以宗室未属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367639_comment'></div>妄荷宠命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367639_comment'></div>惟才与智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367639_comment'></div>俱不如人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367639_comment'></div>况今衰羸残喘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367639_comment'></div>加以病苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367639_comment'></div>支离沈瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367639_comment'></div>历夏及秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367639_comment'></div>终日不过一食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367639_comment'></div>不杖不能自起。<div id='poem_sentence_27_1367639_comment'></div>虽欲自强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367639_comment'></div>必中道委顿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367639_comment'></div>玺书诏旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367639_comment'></div>废失是忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367639_comment'></div>臣伏见广德二年七月赦书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367639_comment'></div>罢天下起复之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367639_comment'></div>许终丧礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367639_comment'></div>此陛下孝德过于两汉。<div id='poem_sentence_37_1367639_comment'></div>岂独令臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367639_comment'></div>隔在赦外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367639_comment'></div>又尚书右丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367639_comment'></div>会府之枢辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367639_comment'></div>御史大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367639_comment'></div>天下之绳墨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367639_comment'></div>宣慰巡检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367639_comment'></div>朝廷之大寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367639_comment'></div>今臣受此三职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367639_comment'></div>而以起复为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367639_comment'></div>因臣过举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367639_comment'></div>破陛下法令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367639_comment'></div>使百寮师师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367639_comment'></div>何以取则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367639_comment'></div>臣夙遭不造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367639_comment'></div>备生人之艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367639_comment'></div>官始一命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367639_comment'></div>先臣弃背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367639_comment'></div>慈母鞠育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367639_comment'></div>至于成立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367639_comment'></div>遭罹二京覆没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367639_comment'></div>弱弟以宗室见害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367639_comment'></div>臣茕然茹痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367639_comment'></div>独侍板舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367639_comment'></div>备尝险阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367639_comment'></div>冀及荣养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367639_comment'></div>才擢掖垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367639_comment'></div>慈颜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1367639", 1367639, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>违代</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367639_comment'></div>罔极之痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367639_comment'></div>终天莫追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367639_comment'></div>今灵筵未尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367639_comment'></div>坟土尚湿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367639_comment'></div>遽令臣荷金印之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367639_comment'></div>处黄华之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367639_comment'></div>使繐帷廓然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367639_comment'></div>奠祭无主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367639_comment'></div>此恒情之所不忍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367639_comment'></div>陛下其忍之乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367639_comment'></div>伏乞以圣慈曲临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367639_comment'></div>皇明下照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367639_comment'></div>矜臣尪瘵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367639_comment'></div>察臣不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367639_comment'></div>更择时彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367639_comment'></div>授之使职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367639_comment'></div>许臣得以羸骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367639_comment'></div>终其丧纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367639_comment'></div>实天地之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367639_comment'></div>钟于臣身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367639_comment'></div>倘残魂未灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367639_comment'></div>朽质可委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367639_comment'></div>誓当摩顶至踵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367639_comment'></div>以答圣造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1367639_comment'></div>臣无任哀瘵恳迫之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_90_1367639_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年</a><div id='poem_1367632' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367632' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367632?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺擒周智光表</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367632")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367632_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367632'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367632'>臣等言。臣闻征而无战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367632_comment'></div>王者之师也。将而必诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367632_comment'></div>春秋之义也。臣伏见周智光傲很<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1367632", 1367632, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>顽虐</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367632_comment'></div>昏迷猖狂。敢专生杀之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367632_comment'></div>以慢王度。崇饰奸慝之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367632_comment'></div>自干天诛。陛下谓罪在已躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367632_comment'></div>视人如子。永言式遏之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367632_comment'></div>不得已而用师。而将才受钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367632_comment'></div>兵未血刃。已枭元恶之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367632_comment'></div>载安旧污之俗。昔汉征黥布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367632_comment'></div>望阵而忧。殷伐鬼方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367632_comment'></div>积年乃克。岂若今日陛下朝命将帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367632_comment'></div>夕歼渠魁。制胜神速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367632_comment'></div>从古未有。臣无任庆快之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367632_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1367632_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367773' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367773' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367773?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故正议大夫右散骑常侍赠礼部尚书李公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367773")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367773_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367773'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367773'>岁在丁未七月丁卯。有唐故右散骑常侍李季卿薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367773_comment'></div>享年五十九。文经邦国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367773_comment'></div>行满天下。无人非鬼责之悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367773_comment'></div>以近后剧。无中人十金之产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367773_comment'></div>以补祭于身殁。顾谓宗子家老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367773_comment'></div>必以巾车一乘。敛手足形还葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367773_comment'></div>其孤冯翊县令霸等。泣奉遗命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367773_comment'></div>以某月庚寅。附宅兆于长安九陴原之先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367773_comment'></div>名公上士。护丧会葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367773_comment'></div>同道必至。哀缠都邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367773_comment'></div>初公烈考曰适。神龙中历官中书舍人昭文馆学士工部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367773_comment'></div>才高而明。为文章蓍龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367773_comment'></div>公生而好学。地使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367773_comment'></div>豁然宏达。天所纵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367773_comment'></div>临大节而贾勇。不私其身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367773_comment'></div>进贤不进不止。事君以忠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367773_comment'></div>当昔天步方艰。王师有征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367773_comment'></div>公入参谏臣。出佐军政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367773_comment'></div>直躬咨诹。戎臣赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367773_comment'></div>其后领二曹。判二州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367773_comment'></div>再司王言。三贰京尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367773_comment'></div>由秘书少监为吏部侍郎。复兼御史大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367773_comment'></div>慰抚山东淮南。明年劳旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367773_comment'></div>典选如故。大历三年拜右常侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367773_comment'></div>其勤王家。十有馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367773_comment'></div>举措由道。行止以直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367773_comment'></div>居贞守忠。欲不能惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367773_comment'></div>思贤求才。若渴若饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367773_comment'></div>推心吐诚。亲疏以之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367773_comment'></div>执德之经。不为利回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367773_comment'></div>正进退于忠信。视得失如洟涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367773_comment'></div>凡君子在位。则不仁者远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367773_comment'></div>攸徂之邦。宜皆蒙福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367773_comment'></div>遽夺公算。是不惠于斯人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367773_comment'></div>天难忱斯。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367773_comment'></div>诸公以为不可奈何者寿夭之数。若奋扬景行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367773_comment'></div>宜在知已。由是尚书右丞长乐贾至作铭以铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367773_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1367773_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367794' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367794' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367794?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为吏部杨侍郎祭李常侍文</a><span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367794'>年月日。某官某乙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367794_comment'></div>谨以清酌之奠。敬祭于故右散骑常侍赠礼部尚书李公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367794_comment'></div>呜呼。冲粹之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367794_comment'></div>生德于公。忠孝贞谅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367794_comment'></div>聪明宏达。卓荦特立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367794_comment'></div>英明虚受。自司翰持衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367794_comment'></div>观风执法。周旋三阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367794_comment'></div>出入十载。能直其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367794_comment'></div>而正其身。致命临节仁而有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367794_comment'></div>造次颠沛。义形于色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367794_comment'></div>庄敬发于谈笑。孝谨扇乎闺门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367794_comment'></div>若天祚明德。神与正直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367794_comment'></div>公宜锡庆钟寿。俾大而昌于何官不至三事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367794_comment'></div>年不及六十。积德无报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367794_comment'></div>为仁者惑焉。今行及先远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367794_comment'></div>将安宅兆。嗟来桑扈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367794_comment'></div>往无返期。追思生平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367794_comment'></div>夙昔欢好。恳款交臂之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367794_comment'></div>殷勤同心之言。今则冥寞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367794_comment'></div>无非梦想。非夫人之为恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367794_comment'></div>吾谁为恸。不知神之所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367794_comment'></div>彼乎此乎。旨酒一樽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367794_comment'></div>庶以为别。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367794_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1367794_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367635' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367635' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367635?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺栎阳县醴泉表</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367635")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367635_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367635'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367635'>臣等言。伏见京兆尹李勉奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367635_comment'></div>栎阳县有醴泉涌出。饮之者痼疾皆愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367635_comment'></div>臣闻王者泽周庶类。则神降百祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367635_comment'></div>天地之心。去人不远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367635_comment'></div>陛下厚德载物。与坤同符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367635_comment'></div>以善利人。如水润下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367635_comment'></div>故后土献瑞。涌泉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1367635", 1367635, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>疗疾</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367635_comment'></div>灵源酌而不竭。沈痼饮而皆痊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367635_comment'></div>勿药之喜。万人是赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367635_comment'></div>仰窥天意。岂不以是彰陛下之德施乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367635_comment'></div>不然。何众庶禺禺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367635_comment'></div>强名圣水。彼丹井<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1367635", 1367635, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>朱草</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367635_comment'></div>白麟赤雁。徒称太平之瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367635_comment'></div>未闻功施于人。方之圣泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367635_comment'></div>岂踰神异。臣等无任喜庆之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367635_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1367635_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367706?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故左补阙安定皇甫公集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367706")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367706_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367706'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367706'>五言诗之源。生于国风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367706_comment'></div>广于离骚。著于李苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367706_comment'></div>盛于曹刘。其所自远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367706_comment'></div>当汉魏之间。虽以朴散为器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367706_comment'></div>作者犹质有馀而文不足。以今揆昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367706_comment'></div>则有朱弦疏越太羹遗味之叹。历千馀岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367706_comment'></div>至沈詹事宋考功。始裁成六律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367706_comment'></div>彰施五色。使言之而中伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367706_comment'></div>歌之而成声。缘情绮靡之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367706_comment'></div>至是乃备。虽去雅寖远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367706_comment'></div>其丽有过于古者。亦犹路鼗出于土鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367706_comment'></div>篆籀生于鸟迹也。沈宋既殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367706_comment'></div>而崔司勋颢王右丞维复崛起于开元天宝之间。得其门而入者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367706_comment'></div>当代不过数人。补阙其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367706_comment'></div>补阙讳冉。字茂政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367706_comment'></div>元晏先生之后。银青光禄大夫泽州刺史讳敬德之曾孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367706_comment'></div>朝散大夫饶州乐平县令讳价之孙。中散大夫潭州刺史讳顗之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367706_comment'></div>十岁能属文。十五岁而老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367706_comment'></div>右丞相曲江张公深所叹异。谓清颖秀拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367706_comment'></div>有江徐之风。伯父秘书少监彬尤器之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367706_comment'></div>自是令闻休畅。举进士第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367706_comment'></div>历无锡县尉左金吾兵曹。今相国太原公之推毂河南也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367706_comment'></div>辟为书记。大历二年迁左拾遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367706_comment'></div>转右补阙。奉使江表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367706_comment'></div>因省家至丹阳。朝廷虚三署郎位以待君之复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367706_comment'></div>不幸短命。年方五十四而殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367706_comment'></div>呜呼惜哉。君忠恕廉恪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367706_comment'></div>居官可纪。孝友恭让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367706_comment'></div>自内形外。言必依仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367706_comment'></div>交不苟合。得丧喜愠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367706_comment'></div>罕见于容。故睹君述作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367706_comment'></div>知君所尚。以景命不永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367706_comment'></div>斯文未臻其极也。盖存于遗札者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367706_comment'></div>凡三百有五十篇。其诗大略以古之比兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367706_comment'></div>就今之声律。涵咏风骚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367706_comment'></div>宪章颜谢。至若丽曲感动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367706_comment'></div>逸思奔发。则天机独得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367706_comment'></div>有非师资所奖。每舞雩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1367706", 1367706, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>咏归</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367706_comment'></div>或金谷文会。曲水修褉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367706_comment'></div>南浦怆别。新声秀句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367706_comment'></div>辄加于常时一等。才钟于情故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367706_comment'></div>君母弟殿中侍御史曾字孝常。与君同禀学诗之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367706_comment'></div>君有诲诱之助焉。既而丽藻竞爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367706_comment'></div>盛名相亚。同乎声者方之景阳孟阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367706_comment'></div>孝常既除丧。惧遗制之坠于地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367706_comment'></div>以及与茂政前后为谏官。故衔痛编次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367706_comment'></div>以论撰见托。遂著其始终以冠于篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367706_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1367706_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年</a>　是年有文，姑系于此。作品：《送蒋员外奏事毕还扬州序》《送韦司直还福州序》《开府仪同三司试太常卿怀州刺史赠太子少傅杨公遗爱碑》《唐故秘书监赠礼部尚书姚公墓志铭》《唐太尉少卿兼万州刺史贺若公故夫人河南郡君元氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1367704' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367704' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367704?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送蒋员外奏事毕还扬州序</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367704")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367704_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367704'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367704'>扬州牧赵国崔公。使其部从事侍御史吴兴蒋晁如京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367704_comment'></div>条奏官府之废置。岁月之要会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367704_comment'></div>其来也。吴楚之众君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367704_comment'></div>酒而诗之。而薛水部弁李司直翰双为之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367704_comment'></div>以冠篇首。既将命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367704_comment'></div>赵公拜左仆射。蒋侯加尚书郎之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367704_comment'></div>其还也。之子日执书卷以言于朝曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367704_comment'></div>始者与数贤别。赖斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367704_comment'></div>故常若在眼。今幸而迁秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367704_comment'></div>行车在门。明旦离群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367704_comment'></div>想今日之会。亦犹于此而思彼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367704_comment'></div>非置书袖中。人谓我何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367704_comment'></div>然后西人之旧者。皆赋韵道别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367704_comment'></div>而鄙夫和之。诗大略盖美蒋侯以才智任职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367704_comment'></div>有周爰咨诹之用。而将事不坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367704_comment'></div>专对不辱。能一其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367704_comment'></div>以佐大府之政。政靡小大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367704_comment'></div>惟公是谋。谋之臧归于府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367704_comment'></div>不知我者则谓我专。赵公所以有成琎坐啸之论而无惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367704_comment'></div>示乐羊谤书之箧而不疑。斯可谓之明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367704_comment'></div>今也于归。腰曳两绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367704_comment'></div>然浊泾素浐。春水始生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367704_comment'></div>秦原青青。诸草皆秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367704_comment'></div>可共乐也。而又别焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367704_comment'></div>凡我同寮。是以有瞻望不及之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367704_comment'></div>故送远之志。悉形于文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367704_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1367704_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367697' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367697' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367697?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送韦司直还福州序</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367697")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367697_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367697'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367697'>远别非难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367697_comment'></div>行路难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367697_comment'></div>行路非难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367697_comment'></div>相逢难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367697_comment'></div>始者与吾子会于抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367697_comment'></div>以吾一日长乎子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367697_comment'></div>子尝敦弟兄之好而不吾先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367697_comment'></div>自云摇雨散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367697_comment'></div>凡四悲秋而一会面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367697_comment'></div>亦既道旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367697_comment'></div>别又继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367697_comment'></div>斯亦可以怆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367697_comment'></div>然君子患德之不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367697_comment'></div>不患人不我知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367697_comment'></div>吾子克慎厥身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367697_comment'></div>以荷先大夫之覆露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367697_comment'></div>贲然将命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367697_comment'></div>为邦司直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367697_comment'></div>被服文行而镞砺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367697_comment'></div>扬其家声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367697_comment'></div>吾惟子之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367697_comment'></div>岂行迈与聚散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367697_comment'></div>足贻志士之忻戚乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367697_comment'></div>是别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367697_comment'></div>祗以歌咏贶吾子而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1367697_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367756' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367756' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367756?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故开府仪同三司试太常卿怀州刺史赠太子少傅杨公遗爱碑颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367756")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367756_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367756'>皇帝嗣位二载。河内得贤二千石曰猗氏杨承仙者。刚毅公廉。仁明爱人。起鞞鼓间。为唐循吏。天生贞方。非有经术润饰。推诚御众。以身率先。民用不扰。政是以茂。于时王师始平河北。而覃怀才归于我。大兵之后。城郭为墟。相国梁公。拔公于戎马之上。表为刺史。俾慰安斯人。公既至。则吊其疮痍。剪其荆棘。省事节用。宽其征而均其力。然后浚决古沟。引丹水以溉田。田之污莱。遂为沃野。衣食河内数千万口。流人襁负。不召自至。如归市焉。鳏煢无告不能自耕者。贷其种与农器而教之。视五谷所宜。督其程课。劳来不怠。使民无不咸返其本。每循行属县。问所疾苦。时其饥饱。心为惨怛。如身之恤臂指。慈父之视幼子也。性严不残。而恭于奉法。训军以律。禁暴以肃。有抵刑者。虽拔葵犯禾。杀之无赦。由是兵不为盗。猛兽不食人。河内之犬。无夜吠者。人人得敦其业而厚其生。上奇其能。以玺书劳勉。封宏农郡公。邑二千户。拜其男锐河南府参军。方倚以牧人。不遐其福。大历二年八月六日。公薨于州。春秋五十四。皇帝悼惜。诏曰。军兴已来。列郡凋耗。二千石少能以教化称者。唯承仙苦心精力。惠此一州。家给而人知礼节。气和而岁无灾害。三年有成。表课第一。贤守既殁。谁其嗣之。宜赠太子少傅。好事者撰公景行。谓公清直强力。能勤其官。百城之州。三军之帅。可使居其任。量不及而殁。惜哉。初岐国公鲁炅之守襄邓也。公为新军佐。敢殊死督战。奋士卒。先蔺石。乱中败面灭鼻。而不言病。卒以是挫敌。军中服其义勇。及凉公秉钺而委质焉。前后保河阳。守高平。安潞镇邺。董戎壶口。戮力危机之中。贾勇仓猝之间。惟尽敌是求。未尝顾身。元戎赖之。卒成大勋。由是历羽林金吾光禄大夫。加开府仪同三司。试太常卿。而后至于是州也。公尝表请归葬。途由于洛。洛阳人闻杨怀州之至也。环而观之。及其还也。怀人数千须于路。其亡也。阖境相吊。童子不巷歌。凡立诚应物者。信不足则行失。饰知沽名者。实不足则名丧。若杨公者。非仁必由已。而诚在言前。则不能使千万人悦之之速如是。某官某耆寿某等。愿复攀公之朱轓。望公之清扬而靡因也。故立石为碑。慰彼永思云。其词曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367756_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367756'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367756'>吴公文翁，遭时无危。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367756'>因而绥之，其绩易施。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367756'>公之来斯，大盗始夷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367756'>师旅饥馑，丁于此时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367756'>顽民反侧，比屋流离。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367756'>饮公醇仁，而忘怨咨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367756'>饥者得食，寒者得衣。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367756'>岂知典谟，以吏为师。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367756'>岂必法令，信则不欺。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367756'>功倍古人，爱及煢嫠。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1367756'>人之戴公，父兮母兮。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1367756'>公之品望，与古贤希。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1367756'>宜从人欲，俾寿无期。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1367756'>呜呼不佣，舍我曷归。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1367756'>公俾我活，何以报之。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1367756'>我思公兮，涕泪此碑。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1367756_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1367756'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1367756_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367774' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367774' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367774?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故秘书监赠礼部尚书姚公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367774")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367774_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367774'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367774'>有唐秘书监永安县侯姚公讳子彦。字伯英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367774_comment'></div>其先冯翊莲勺人也。至高祖僧洪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367774_comment'></div>徙家河东。祖思聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367774_comment'></div>秘书少监。父坦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367774_comment'></div>汝州梁县丞。赠秘书监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367774_comment'></div>公忠谅孝爱。宽仁愿恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367774_comment'></div>质方气冲。天所授也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367774_comment'></div>而力行博学。温故知新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367774_comment'></div>错综六艺。以作词赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367774_comment'></div>初举进士。又举词藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367774_comment'></div>皆升甲科。尉清苑获嘉永宁三县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367774_comment'></div>开元二十九年。诏立黄老学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367774_comment'></div>亲问奥义。对策者五百馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367774_comment'></div>公与今相国河南元公载及广平宋少贞等十人。以条奏精辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367774_comment'></div>才冠等列。授右拾遗内供奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367774_comment'></div>历左补阙。于时天下无金革之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367774_comment'></div>选多士。命百官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367774_comment'></div>先文行而后名法。而柱下方书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367774_comment'></div>南宫章奏。主张纶翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367774_comment'></div>典司礼文。尤精其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367774_comment'></div>非盛名莫居。由是迁公殿中侍御史礼部员外郎礼部郎中知制诰中书舍人太常少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367774_comment'></div>天宝十四年。奉诏宣慰江东淮南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367774_comment'></div>览观风俗。无何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367774_comment'></div>二京陷覆。太夫人捐馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367774_comment'></div>公外罹忧患。内缠茕疚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367774_comment'></div>衔愤泣血。毁瘠灭性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367774_comment'></div>乘舆反正。公适外除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367774_comment'></div>拜太子右庶子。于时迍难始康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367774_comment'></div>百揆草创。官复其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367774_comment'></div>人亦求旧。俄又授公中书舍人礼部侍郎光禄卿左散骑常侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367774_comment'></div>加银青光禄大夫。复知制诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367774_comment'></div>广德二年授秘书监。以儒行懿德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367774_comment'></div>策名三朝。遗迹故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367774_comment'></div>周遍台阁。资忠体和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367774_comment'></div>惟道是居。正身奉上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367774_comment'></div>中立不倚。恐惧戒慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367774_comment'></div>形于隐微。故遭值<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1367774", 1367774, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>倾否</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367774_comment'></div>出入夷险。而未尝有悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367774_comment'></div>名与身偕。德善是依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367774_comment'></div>明哲以保故也。享寿七十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367774_comment'></div>大历二年四月某日。薨于位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367774_comment'></div>五月某日。诏赠礼部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367774_comment'></div>知言者以为寿富康宁。攸好德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367774_comment'></div>考终命。洪范谓之向用五福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367774_comment'></div>而公居四焉。以清俭贻厥子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367774_comment'></div>故所不至者富焉尔。非明德介祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367774_comment'></div>何以享兹。有子曰骁曰骥曰骖曰骃曰骕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367774_comment'></div>号于昊天。痛欲报之罔极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367774_comment'></div>衔恤问礼。抆血襄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367774_comment'></div>十月丁酉。卜兆此原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367774_comment'></div>惟盛德与公器。若川流之无还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367774_comment'></div>垂芳如之何。刻铭于其墓之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367774_comment'></div>将以志不朽。其词云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367774_comment'></div>恂恂秘书。蕴粹含和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367774_comment'></div>服膺孔门。行邻四科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367774_comment'></div>遭时之康。天下尚文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367774_comment'></div>公奋羽翰。翱翔庆云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367774_comment'></div>晚逢中兴。贵德尚齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367774_comment'></div>公秉懿范。入作卿士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367774_comment'></div>逮事三后。出入二纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367774_comment'></div>典礼司书。媚于天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367774_comment'></div>居贞保俭。与禄终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367774_comment'></div>郁郁佳城。烈烈馀美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367774_comment'></div>日月有逝。令闻无已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367774_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1367774_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367766' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367766' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367766?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐太府少卿兼万州刺史贺若公故夫人河南郡君元氏墓志铭</a><span
