class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367766_comment'></div>魏景穆皇帝九代孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367766_comment'></div>祖讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367766_comment'></div>皇朝赠太子少保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367766_comment'></div>父讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367766_comment'></div>克荷前烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367766_comment'></div>不幸早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367766_comment'></div>夫人在孕而孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367766_comment'></div>鞠育于叔父相国颍川公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367766_comment'></div>天机聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367766_comment'></div>生知仁孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367766_comment'></div>被服法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367766_comment'></div>综习文史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367766_comment'></div>年十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367766_comment'></div>嫁河南贺若璿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367766_comment'></div>璿积功劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367766_comment'></div>剖符为郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367766_comment'></div>夫人辅佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367766_comment'></div>以副笄宜室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367766_comment'></div>能睦其族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367766_comment'></div>且劝以义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367766_comment'></div>而风藻礼范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367766_comment'></div>仪刑闺门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367766_comment'></div>晚节厌离心垢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367766_comment'></div>严持禅诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367766_comment'></div>而道机未宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367766_comment'></div>寿量有极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367766_comment'></div>永泰元年三月某日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367766_comment'></div>终于渠州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367766_comment'></div>享年若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367766_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367766_comment'></div>以夫人之柔明孝慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367766_comment'></div>温惠淑茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367766_comment'></div>况承景穆之馀裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367766_comment'></div>少保之贻则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367766_comment'></div>季父当国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367766_comment'></div>良人专城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367766_comment'></div>河润泽及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367766_comment'></div>福绥宜远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367766_comment'></div>胡弗眉寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367766_comment'></div>钟是短历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367766_comment'></div>颍川公之恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367766_comment'></div>其可既乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367766_comment'></div>大历二年二月二十二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367766_comment'></div>反葬于京兆鄠县之某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367766_comment'></div>宜列景行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367766_comment'></div>贻于彤史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367766_comment'></div>恐陵岸或迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367766_comment'></div>音徽将沫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367766_comment'></div>故月而日之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367766_comment'></div>铭诸坚石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367766_comment'></div>盖犹父之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367766_comment'></div>其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367766_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_1367766'>人亦有言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367766_comment'></div>天祚明德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367766_comment'></div>吁嗟邦媛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367766_comment'></div>未偕寿域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367766_comment'></div>家节既成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367766_comment'></div>蕙芽方植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367766_comment'></div>仁而无报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367766_comment'></div>为善者惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367766_comment'></div>夜台超忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367766_comment'></div>神斯冥默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367766_comment'></div>贞石有磷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367766_comment'></div>德音罔极。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1367766_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年1月</a>　在吏部任上，正月，御史中丞归崇敬奉使新罗员祭册立，独孤及有序行。作品：《送归中丞使新罗吊祭册立序》<div id='poem_1367700' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367700' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367700?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送归中丞使新罗吊祭册立序</a><span class='authorDate'>（768年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367700")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367700_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367700'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367700'>儒家者流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367700_comment'></div>鲜肯冠獬豸冠者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367700_comment'></div>盖抗节刚奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367700_comment'></div>以排击为气使故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367700_comment'></div>今天子以公身衣儒服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367700_comment'></div>力儒行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367700_comment'></div>行之修可移于官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367700_comment'></div>学之精可专对四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367700_comment'></div>是故公任执法之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367700_comment'></div>且使操节以济大海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367700_comment'></div>颁我王度于大荒之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367700_comment'></div>夫新罗嗣王以丧讣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367700_comment'></div>且请命于我矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367700_comment'></div>我则归赗继好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367700_comment'></div>以策命命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367700_comment'></div>实怀远示德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367700_comment'></div>礼之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367700_comment'></div>夫亦将宏宣王风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367700_comment'></div>诞敷微言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367700_comment'></div>使鸡林塞外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367700_comment'></div>一变可至齐鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367700_comment'></div>不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367700_comment'></div>归公何以不陋九夷之行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367700_comment'></div>盖行于忠信者无险易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367700_comment'></div>拘于王程者无远近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367700_comment'></div>故公受诏之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367700_comment'></div>则遗其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367700_comment'></div>视涉海如蹈陆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367700_comment'></div>谓穷发犹跬步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367700_comment'></div>岂鲸怒鳌抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367700_comment'></div>足戒行李。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367700_comment'></div>凡以诗贶别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367700_comment'></div>姑美遣使臣之盛云尔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1367700_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年5月1日</a>　除濠州刺史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年5月</a>　除濠州刺史，尚未到任。作品：《唐故银青光禄大夫太子左庶子严公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1367783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367783' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367783?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故银青光禄大夫太子左庶子严公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（768年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367783")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367783_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367783'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367783'>皇唐太子左庶子河内县子冯翊严公讳损之。故都督洮州诸军事洮州刺史协之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367783_comment'></div>赠太常少卿方约季子。中书侍郎挺之母弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367783_comment'></div>家之庆。天之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367783_comment'></div>钟于公躬。故其德备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367783_comment'></div>少仕昌世。遇权臣恶直官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367783_comment'></div>不登三台。晚值多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367783_comment'></div>安贞不竞。故位不过郡守宫尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367783_comment'></div>前后佐两卫。参四府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367783_comment'></div>领二县。典七州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367783_comment'></div>再入石渠。三升龙楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367783_comment'></div>凡处任十八。享年七十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367783_comment'></div>未尝以利苟合。违道从欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367783_comment'></div>用之则行。见机不俟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367783_comment'></div>动静允迪。劳谦有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367783_comment'></div>广德二年六月二十五日。终于襄阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367783_comment'></div>是岁八月。权窆楚山西原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367783_comment'></div>冢子曰式。官至江陵少尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367783_comment'></div>不幸道夭。仲子曰士元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367783_comment'></div>由殿中侍御史为尚书虞部员外郎。少子曰士良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367783_comment'></div>领秘书著作郎。悉能裕父蛊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367783_comment'></div>懿文德取公器。他日独立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367783_comment'></div>训所至也。大历三年岁在戊申五月二十九日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367783_comment'></div>返葬洛阳先茔。礼之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367783_comment'></div>宗人故太常卿向。尝状公往行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367783_comment'></div>贻诸有司。谓公外宽内刚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367783_comment'></div>廉正笃敬。温而不厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367783_comment'></div>直而不讦。学究原本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367783_comment'></div>行有枝叶。故其适道求友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367783_comment'></div>莅职任事。覈其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367783_comment'></div>不居其华。初公宰氾水也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367783_comment'></div>以庄明慈惠为政。氾水人不敢欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367783_comment'></div>而户口增倍。狱讼衰止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367783_comment'></div>御史中丞萧隐之以状闻。公是以有著作郎之拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367783_comment'></div>其后历太原上谷弋阳馀杭丹阳。虽风俗殊异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367783_comment'></div>治效如一。不曰才乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367783_comment'></div>公在清池。会安禄山与当国者交恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367783_comment'></div>公曰。难作矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367783_comment'></div>遂移疾请告。奸党恶之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367783_comment'></div>是以有弋阳之贬。贬之明年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367783_comment'></div>河北为戎。不曰智乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367783_comment'></div>涉患难不辱身。践禄位不徇名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367783_comment'></div>居义处顺。动罔违吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367783_comment'></div>不曰贞乎。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367783_comment'></div>荣问素业。与时皆逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367783_comment'></div>可称也。而不可追也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367783_comment'></div>今采其实录。刻石示后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367783_comment'></div>盖欲报罔极者之志也。其辞曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367783_comment'></div>君子之道。容民畜众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367783_comment'></div>公宰二邑。二邑无讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367783_comment'></div>与国共理。惟二千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367783_comment'></div>公七剖符。七著成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367783_comment'></div>乃师国子。司成望苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367783_comment'></div>考艺较德。以弼三善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367783_comment'></div>中和其心。正直是践。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367783_comment'></div>道亚羽翼。名掩春华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367783_comment'></div>忠以事君。孝施于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367783_comment'></div>粲粲令子。鲜侔晨葩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367783_comment'></div>若何不吊。盛德既丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367783_comment'></div>音徽永沬。士友孤望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367783_comment'></div>千载九原。游者悽怆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367783_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1367783_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
许昌
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年</a>　至许州访旧居，有诗纪行。作品：《壬辰岁过旧居》<div id='poem_40892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_40892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a -----title
河南
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7166436a546443a6842fa20ed93eafb9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7166436a546443a6842fa20ed93eafb9");'><span id='7166436a546443a6842fa20ed93eafb9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=746&endYear=747')">746-747年</a>，22-23岁</div><div id='7166436a546443a6842fa20ed93eafb9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=746&endYear=746')">746年</a>　在梁宋一带。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>　此年前后游梁宋，识陈兼、贾至、高适等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>　从弟独孤愐赴长安，有序赠别。作品：《送弟愐之京序》<div id='poem_1367721' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367721' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367721?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送弟愐之京序</a><span class='authorDate'>（747年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367721")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367721_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367721'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367721'>苍龙居元枵之岁。与尔吹埙篪于长安灵台之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367721_comment'></div>当时尔方青襟。余适纨裤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367721_comment'></div>各志小学。相期大来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367721_comment'></div>其后尔以经术荐。遂观光于上国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367721_comment'></div>余牢落两河。为病所系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367721_comment'></div>星分雨散。十有二载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367721_comment'></div>中间暂携手一笑者。及今而三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367721_comment'></div>昨日游寓。今成畴昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367721_comment'></div>此会绵邈。空成梦想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367721_comment'></div>岂不欲申橘柚之性。咏和乐之什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367721_comment'></div>乐未终也。别又继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367721_comment'></div>然君子修诚则物应。克已则名彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367721_comment'></div>尔能圭璋特达。甲冑忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367721_comment'></div>致逸足于千里。吾有望焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367721_comment'></div>方务远图。何嗟少别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367721_comment'></div>到秦地有问吾事者。为报江湖閒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367721_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1367721_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='6e24203f33b94d2a9162affde7c5418f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6e24203f33b94d2a9162affde7c5418f");'><span id='6e24203f33b94d2a9162affde7c5418f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=749&endYear=750')">749-750年</a>，25-26岁</div><div id='6e24203f33b94d2a9162affde7c5418f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=749&endYear=750')">749-750年</a>　在梁宋一带。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
商丘（宋城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e31039ad67e64dc788fd6ea469c840da_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e31039ad67e64dc788fd6ea469c840da");'><span id='e31039ad67e64dc788fd6ea469c840da_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=748&endYear=748')">748年</a>，24岁</div><div id='e31039ad67e64dc788fd6ea469c840da' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=748&endYear=748')">748年4月</a>　在宋州，有文送别友人。作品：《宋州送姚旷之江东刘冉之河北序》<div id='poem_1367716' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367716' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367716?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋州送姚旷之江东刘冉之河北序</a><span class='authorDate'>（748年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367716")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367716_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367716'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367716'>春叶尉吴兴姚旷至自洛阳。中山刘冉至自长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367716_comment'></div>俱以文博我。相与交欢于睢涣之涘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367716_comment'></div>始则开青天豁其云雾。亦既窥武库见其矛戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367716_comment'></div>凡旬有五日。而姚适吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367716_comment'></div>刘济河。余归梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367716_comment'></div>各有四方之事。将为千里之别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367716_comment'></div>夏四月。抗手于卢门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367716_comment'></div>议别故也。夫别与会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367716_comment'></div>悲乐存乎其中。故贤智所不能遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367716_comment'></div>然达者游世。随变所适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367716_comment'></div>静而与阴同德。动而与阳同波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367716_comment'></div>异乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1367716", 1367716, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>金柅</span>之有系。匏瓜之莫食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367716_comment'></div>子其行矣。别何为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367716_comment'></div>北斗在已。南风始来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367716_comment'></div>丛台草长。京口水阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367716_comment'></div>何以送远。唯当赋伐木以为仁人之赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367716_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1367716_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
开封

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年</a>　再游汴州，登大梁之墟。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2415adba21474243bdd59ea1964edf00_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=753&endYear=753')">753年</a>　在汴州，李白过汴州往击曹州，有序赠行。作品：《送李白之曹南序》<div id='poem_1367714' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367714' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367714?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送李白之曹南序</a><span class='authorDate'>（753年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367714")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367714_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367714'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367714'>曩子之入秦也。上方览子虚之赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367714_comment'></div>喜相如同时。由是朝诣公车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367714_comment'></div>夕挥宸翰。一旦襆被金马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367714_comment'></div>蓬累而行。出入燕宋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367714_comment'></div>与白云为伍。然则适来时行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367714_comment'></div>适去时止也。彼碌碌者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367714_comment'></div>徒见三河之游倦。百镒之金尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367714_comment'></div>乃议子于得失亏成之间。曾不知才全者无亏成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367714_comment'></div>志全者无得失。进与退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367714_comment'></div>于道德乎何有。是日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367714_comment'></div>出车桐门。将驾于曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367714_comment'></div>仙药满囊。道书盈箧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367714_comment'></div>异乎庄舄之辞越。仲尼之去鲁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367714_comment'></div>送子何所。平台之隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367714_comment'></div>短歌薄酒。击筑相和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367714_comment'></div>大丈夫各乘风波。未始有极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367714_comment'></div>哀乐且不足累上士之心。况小别乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367714_comment'></div>请偕赋诗。以见交态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367714_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1367714_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=753&endYear=753')">753年10月</a>　在汴州，陈兼应辟赴京，有序赠行。作品：《送陈赞府兼应辟赴京序》<div id='poem_1367729' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367729' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_10_1367729_comment'></div>十二载冬十月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367729_comment'></div>果以公才徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367729_comment'></div>龙泉自惜。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1367729_comment'></div>竟为秦人所得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367729_comment'></div>且晋以梁山召伯宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367729_comment'></div>汉以明堂延申公。<div id='poem_sentence_22_1367729_comment'></div>公祗命台铉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367729_comment'></div>将濯缨而孤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367729_comment'></div>当贞女不字。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　路过陈留。作品：《送陈留张少府郧东京赴选序》<div id='poem_1367720' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367720' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367720?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送陈留张少府勋东京赴选序</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1367720'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367720'>每岁孟春。冢宰悬象魏之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367720_comment'></div>以官民材。天下髦士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367720_comment'></div>于是乎云屯词锋。角立智刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367720_comment'></div>今子投袂而起。将鼓行乎其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367720_comment'></div>其于湛卢发硎。批郤如玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367720_comment'></div>繁弱在手。舍拔则获者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367720_comment'></div>吾惟子之望。当知君子广其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367720_comment'></div>达其道。则荣誉贵仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367720_comment'></div>可得而拾。孰云袅袅秋风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367720_comment'></div>悠悠远道。足为志士之感哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367720_comment'></div>杂佩可以申永怀。尊酒可以慰别绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367720_comment'></div>其赠言之分。顾谓坐者志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367720_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1367720_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
烟台（牟平）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bda46814d023432f9bce42053265bef7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bda46814d023432f9bce42053265bef7");'><span id='bda46814d023432f9bce42053265bef7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=751&endYear=751')">751年</a>，27岁</div><div id='bda46814d023432f9bce42053265bef7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=751&endYear=751')">751年</a>　约于此年秋冬至山东登州牟平县境的之罘山观秦皇遗迹，并有诗寄友。作品：《海上寄萧立》<div id='poem_40923' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_40923' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/40923?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海上寄萧立</a><span class='authorDate'>（751年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_40923")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_40923_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_40923'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_40923'>朔风剪塞草，寒露日夜<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作始）</span>结。<div id='poem_sentence_0_40923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_40923'>行行到<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_40923", 40923, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>瀛壖</span>，归思生暮节。<div id='poem_sentence_1_40923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_40923'>驿楼见万里，延首望辽碣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_40923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_40923'>远海入大荒，平芜际<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_40923", 40923, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>穷发</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_40923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_40923'>旧国在梦想，故人胡且越。<div id='poem_sentence_4_40923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_40923'>契阔阻风<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作夙）</span>期，荏苒成<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_40923", 40923, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>雨别</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_40923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_40923'>海西望京口，两地各天末。<div id='poem_sentence_6_40923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_40923'>索居动经秋，再笑知曷月<span class='inlineComment2'>（一本无此二句）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_40923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_40923'>日南望中尽<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作目穷南云尽）</span>，唯见飞鸟灭。<div id='poem_sentence_8_40923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_40923'>音<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作清）</span>尘未易得，何由慰饥渴。<div id='poem_sentence_9_40923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_40923'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_40923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_40923'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(40923)'>评注</a><span -----title
尉氏
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='963b50d512dd491cbcdafcc0b8dadc49_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("963b50d512dd491cbcdafcc0b8dadc49");'><span id='963b50d512dd491cbcdafcc0b8dadc49_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年</a>，28岁</div><div id='963b50d512dd491cbcdafcc0b8dadc49' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年</a>　览阮籍啸台遗迹，并著文刻石。作品：《阮公啸台颂并序》<div id='poem_1367625' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367625' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367625?labeling=true' target='_blank'>阮公啸台颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367625")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367625_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367625'>按晋阳秋。阮公讳籍。字嗣宗。陈留尉氏人也。夫云蒸于山。不择时而出。故公以全德生于衰世。于时中州多故。大道浸□缺于用者知膏火自铄。逃于累者惧木雁两伤。公由是内张道机。外隳天彀。土梗圣智。秕糠轩冕。遂登广武以览古。望梁台而寓词。埋照于竹林。放神于蓬池。德充也尔。其兴怀昔游。故为东平相。怡情善酿。故受步兵校尉。弛张蘧宁之际。出处夷惠之表。否泰莫得介于灵府。名实不足汨其冲气。螭蟠龙卧。与道偕隐。所以沈吟志全。慷慨神王。独立长啸。遗荣此台。当其寓兴也。盖将豪视泰山。囊括浩气。颓然自得。与造化者为友。故卷其用而怀之。世莫得而窥也。其外物所感。则寄之翰墨焉。谓道莫至于专气抱一。于是著释老论。哀莫大于矫时死名。于是有吊比干文。情动于中而形于言。赋咏怀诗。问道苏门。𥬒而不答。作大人先生传。岁在元黓。余登大梁之墟。墟中之人方诵公遗尘。叹元风芜没。议乐石以旌朽壤。余采其故事之存于糟粕者。勒而为啸台颂。颂曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367625_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367625'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367625'>天下多故，贤人谷耻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367625'>隐于沈饮，以俟倾否。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367625'>越礼逃用，晦德忘已。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367625'>不知我者，为我狂且。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367625'>长啸怀人，咏古著书。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367625'>感时而恸，非必穷途。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367625'>沔彼汴水，东流无返。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367625'>迹是人非，荒台可践。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367625'>升高延伫，想见青眼。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367625'>道乌乎在，日逝日远<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1367625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1367625'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1367625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1367625'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_1367625_0'>⑴ 一本作五运相错三徵交戾天地之气有时而闭居子迷阳亦既悬解万象离境一杯韬世大辩不言至清无徒泠然长啸味道之枢神和天倪迹寄穷途物我两忘独与化俱汤汤汴河东流不返之子已往德音日远荒台未倾嘉树勿剪升高延伫思见青眼山有莱隰有薇逝者不作吾谁与归望古刻石永昭清徽</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1367625_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
华阴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c64757d419df457cacf3fe6bf76abeaf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c64757d419df457cacf3fe6bf76abeaf");'><span id='c64757d419df457cacf3fe6bf76abeaf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=756')">755-756年</a>，31-32岁</div><div id='c64757d419df457cacf3fe6bf76abeaf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年3月</a>　由长安返回华阴县，有诗纪事。作品：《三月三日自京到华阴于水亭独酌寄裴六薛八》<div id='poem_40889' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_40889' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/40889?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三月三日自京到华阴于水亭独酌寄裴六薛八</a><span class='authorDate'>（755年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_40889")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_40889_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_40889'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(127, "poem_allusion_40889")'>傲吏</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9085, "poem_allusion_40889")'>席上珍</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_40889_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_40889'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_40889'>祗役匪遑息，经时客三秦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_40889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_40889'>还家问节候，知到上巳辰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_40889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_40889'>山县何所有，高城闭青春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_40889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_40889'>和风不吾欺，桃杏满四邻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_40889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_40889'>旧友适远别，谁当接欢欣。<div id='poem_sentence_4_40889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_40889'>呼儿命长瓢，独酌湘吴醇。<div id='poem_sentence_5_40889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_40889'>一酌一朗咏，既酣意亦申。<div id='poem_sentence_6_40889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_40889'>言筌暂两忘，霞月祗相新。<div id='poem_sentence_7_40889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_40889'>裴子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_40889", 40889, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>尘表</span>物，薛侯<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9085, "poem_sentence_8_40889")'>席上珍</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_40889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_40889'>寄书二<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(127, "poem_sentence_9_40889")'>傲吏</span>，何日同车茵。<div id='poem_sentence_9_40889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_40889'>讵肯使空名，终然羁此身。<div id='poem_sentence_10_40889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_40889'>他<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作何）</span>年解桎梏，长作海上人。<div id='poem_sentence_11_40889_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_40889'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_40889_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年6月</a>　在华阴任，宴临汝县令裴冀于华山黄神谷，并著文。作品：《华山黄神谷宴临汝裴明府序》<div id='poem_1367680' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367680' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367680?labeling=true' target='_blank'>华山黄神谷宴临汝裴明府序</a><span class='authorDate'>（755年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367680")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367680_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367680'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367680'>黄卢子灭景上汉千岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367680_comment'></div>留碧峰白云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367680_comment'></div>以贻后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367680_comment'></div>故清机胜事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367680_comment'></div>未始有极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367680_comment'></div>余吏于华之明年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367680_comment'></div>道侣裴冀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367680_comment'></div>亦再命为临汝令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367680_comment'></div>夏六月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367680_comment'></div>假道敝邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367680_comment'></div>税鞅此山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367680_comment'></div>思欲追高步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367680_comment'></div>诣真境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367680_comment'></div>于是相与携手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367680_comment'></div>及二三友生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367680_comment'></div>童子将命者六七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367680_comment'></div>挈长瓢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367680_comment'></div>荷大壶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367680_comment'></div>以浊醪素琴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367680_comment'></div>会于黄神之谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367680_comment'></div>兴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367680_comment'></div>桉谷之西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367680_comment'></div>顶实三峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367680_comment'></div>东面石壁丛倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367680_comment'></div>刺为洞壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367680_comment'></div>乳窦潜泄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367680_comment'></div>喷成盘涡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367680_comment'></div>两崖合斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367680_comment'></div>若与天接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367680_comment'></div>二三子将极其登探也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367680_comment'></div>至则系马山足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367680_comment'></div>披榛石门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367680_comment'></div>入自洞口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367680_comment'></div>至于梯路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367680_comment'></div>蹋连嶂与謺崿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367680_comment'></div>度岖嵚而蹑凌兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367680_comment'></div>夤缘绝磴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367680_comment'></div>及横岭而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367680_comment'></div>澡身乎飞泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367680_comment'></div>濯缨乎清涟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367680_comment'></div>想夫君俟我于花峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367680_comment'></div>下碧空而婵娟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367680_comment'></div>爱而不见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367680_comment'></div>搔首空山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367680_comment'></div>然后靡灵草以为席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367680_comment'></div>倾流霞而相劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367680_comment'></div>楚歌徐动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367680_comment'></div>沂咏亦发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367680_comment'></div>清商激于琴韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367680_comment'></div>白云起于笔锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367680_comment'></div>是日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367680_comment'></div>高兴尽而世绪遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367680_comment'></div>幽情形而神机王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367680_comment'></div>颓然觉形骸六藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367680_comment'></div>悉为外物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367680_comment'></div>天地万有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367680_comment'></div>无非秋毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367680_comment'></div>亦既醉止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367680_comment'></div>则皆足言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367680_comment'></div>以志仙迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367680_comment'></div>且旌吾友嘉会之在山也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1367680_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年</a>　在华阴任，著文二篇，当代词人无不畏服。作品：《古函谷关铭并序、仙掌铭并序》<div id='poem_1367748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367748' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367748?labeling=true' target='_blank'>古函谷关铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（755年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367748")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367748_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367748'>王者建邦经野。观象立极。于是有重门击柝。以待暴客。故封略土宇。守在关塞。山川邱陵。为之城池。天作崤函。俾屏京室。崇山回合。连冈丛倚。长河屈盘。万里来束。崖奔岭蹙谷抱溪斗。崛起重险。为秦东门。截函夏于阃阈。锁天府于户牖。外扼九州之咽喉。故百二形焉。内拥六合之奥区。故霸王出焉。当其周原鹿骇。战国猬起。嬴氏建瓴山东。择肉宇内。持戟百万。连衡此关。是时也。开门而九国师遁。振策而二周鼎入。奄有大宝。遂吞中区。洎江返秦璧。天祐汉祚。高皇帝提剑而西。以遏乱略。斩白帝。绁降王。举汉中。平咸阳。廓金城以建都。活万姓以三章。取威定功。此焉是保。粤若询事国牒。聆风仙箓。则真气灵踪。起乎其中。柱史一去。流沙万里。留玉函于旧宅。传宝图于本枝。岂上帝乃眷。兴王是感。不然。何锡羡开国。如此其大耶。岁在大火。余适下阳。停骖塞门。凭览旧国。襟带如故。世道不留。秦馀空山。汉遗茂草。恐复舟失于壑。岸化为谷。万载之后。昧者不知。乃刻颂此石。以示来裔。其词曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367748_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367748'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367748'>天地雷雨，英雄交争。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367748'>设险守国，作藩于京。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367748'>姓易时移，山空塞平。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367748'>千秋陵谷，想见精灵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367748'>仙驾长往，雄图杳冥。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367748'>于以志之，勒铭岩扃。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367748_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367748'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1367748_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年</a>　在华阴任。作品：《奉送元城主簿兄赴任序》《为杨右相祭西岳文》<div id='poem_1367676' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367676' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367676?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉送元城主簿兄赴任序</a><span class='authorDate'>（755年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367676")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367676_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367676'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367676'>往岁兄之尉匡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367676_comment'></div>德刑成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367676_comment'></div>礼义举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367676_comment'></div>秕政杜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367676_comment'></div>紊纲缉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367676_comment'></div>人曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367676_comment'></div>莅民如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367676_comment'></div>其达必大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367676_comment'></div>十四年春王正月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367676_comment'></div>再命于元城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367676_comment'></div>元城地雄人悍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367676_comment'></div>土壤赋错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367676_comment'></div>处宋卫中山燕齐赵魏之都会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367676_comment'></div>三川辐凑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367676_comment'></div>四术毂击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367676_comment'></div>兄方以德举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367676_comment'></div>吏此大邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367676_comment'></div>则千里之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367676_comment'></div>兆于是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367676_comment'></div>彼徒劳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367676_comment'></div>其鶱翥之滥觞乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367676_comment'></div>岁物已春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367676_comment'></div>泰山日绿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367676_comment'></div>亦既选吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367676_comment'></div>驾言徂东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367676_comment'></div>岂不知常棣之诗废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367676_comment'></div>则和乐之好缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367676_comment'></div>盍使伯氏仲氏偕咏歌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367676_comment'></div>以赠行迈。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1367676_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367801' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367801' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367801?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为杨右相祭西岳文</a><span class='authorDate'>（755年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367801")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367801_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367801'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367801'>维年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367801_comment'></div>司空右相杨国忠吏部尚书同中书门下平章事韦见素等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367801_comment'></div>谨以少牢之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367801_comment'></div>敬祭于西岳金天王之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367801_comment'></div>顷自献岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367801_comment'></div>达于三月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367801_comment'></div>畜极不雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367801_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1367801", 1367801, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>屯膏</span>未光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367801_comment'></div>元元其咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367801_comment'></div>涤涤是惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367801_comment'></div>国忠等是用虔奉睿虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367801_comment'></div>聿遵祀典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367801_comment'></div>谨遣鸣皋山人韦朝真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367801_comment'></div>敢邀福于大神之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367801_comment'></div>精意才申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367801_comment'></div>而休祐肸蚃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367801_comment'></div>宸衷遥达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367801_comment'></div>而瑞泽滂沛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367801_comment'></div>非神之幽赞叶于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367801_comment'></div>神之景命符于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367801_comment'></div>则畴能降祥荐祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367801_comment'></div>如此其速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367801_comment'></div>故簠簋牺象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367801_comment'></div>敬修享礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367801_comment'></div>虽冥应无方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367801_comment'></div>非馨香所答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367801_comment'></div>而神威如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367801_comment'></div>庶明灵惟歆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367801_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1367801_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年6月</a>　在华阴任，安禄山陷潼关，走避叛军。<br /></div>

-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b6d6e9582fcc4ec08be3f65077aba956_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b6d6e9582fcc4ec08be3f65077aba956");'><span id='b6d6e9582fcc4ec08be3f65077aba956_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年10月14日</a>　迁葬父于洛阳龙门山。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='28743ca625644893ba2f54c20a10b8ca_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("28743ca625644893ba2f54c20a10b8ca");'><span id='28743ca625644893ba2f54c20a10b8ca_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年</a>，45岁</div><div id='28743ca625644893ba2f54c20a10b8ca' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年7月</a>　七月，自濠州归洛阳，迁葬父母及三兄憕五弟丕六弟万于河南府寿安县甘泉乡之原，有灵表、墓志。作品：《唐故朝散大夫颍川郡长史赠秘书监河南独孤公灵表、唐故颍川郡长史赠秘书监独孤公第三子憕墓志、唐故浙江东道节度掌书记越州剡县主簿独孤丕墓志、唐故颍川郡长史赠秘书监独孤公第六子万墓志》<div id='poem_1367789' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367789' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367789?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故朝散大夫颍川郡长史赠秘书监河南独孤公灵表</a><span class='authorDate'>（769年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367789")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367789_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367789'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367789'>公讳某。其先刘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367789_comment'></div>出自汉世祖光武皇帝之裔。世祖生沛献王辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367789_comment'></div>辅生釐王定。定生节王正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367789_comment'></div>正生长子广。嗣王位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367789_comment'></div>次子廙。仕汉为洛阳令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367789_comment'></div>廙生穆。穆生进伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367789_comment'></div>为度辽将军击匈奴。兵少援不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367789_comment'></div>战败。为单于所获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367789_comment'></div>迁居独孤山下。生尸利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367789_comment'></div>单于加以谷蠡王之位。号独孤部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367789_comment'></div>尸利生乌和。乌和生二子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367789_comment'></div>长曰去卑。为右贤王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367789_comment'></div>建安中。献帝自长安东归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367789_comment'></div>有李傕郭氾之乱。右贤王率其部卫车驾还洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367789_comment'></div>遂徙许。复归国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367789_comment'></div>卒。次弟猛代立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367789_comment'></div>生嗣论。嗣论生路孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367789_comment'></div>路孤生眷。眷生罗辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367789_comment'></div>从魏文帝迁都洛阳。遂为司州洛阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367789_comment'></div>始以其部为氏。用勋伐锡爵永安公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367789_comment'></div>位征东将军定州刺史。征东生万龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367789_comment'></div>官至廷尉。谥曰贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367789_comment'></div>廷尉生稽。字延平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367789_comment'></div>善左右射。学究金匮之奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367789_comment'></div>魏世祖初。从平滑台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367789_comment'></div>以功授散骑常侍。历守冀定相三州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367789_comment'></div>时新定律令。慎选廷尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367789_comment'></div>徵公拜焉。再世为法官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367789_comment'></div>俱以廉平不苛显名。当时荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367789_comment'></div>加镇东将军。薨谥曰文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367789_comment'></div>镇东生归。辩聪而才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367789_comment'></div>又为镇东。薨赠太尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367789_comment'></div>太尉生冀。字希颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367789_comment'></div>以博学侍讲东宫。历安南将军定州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367789_comment'></div>赠司徒。司徒生永业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367789_comment'></div>以文武兼备。佐齐王入洛定邺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367789_comment'></div>都督幽洛二州。由行台尚书令升司徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367789_comment'></div>封临川郡王。语在齐史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367789_comment'></div>临川王生子佳。在齐为劲努将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367789_comment'></div>在周为仪同三司。在隋守清远<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作怀朔）</span>镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367789_comment'></div>握节死难。赠并州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367789_comment'></div>并州生义顺。武德中历户部侍郎尚书左丞光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367789_comment'></div>封洛南郡公。洛南生左千牛备身讳元庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367789_comment'></div>公之祖也。千牛生朝散大夫定州长史讳思陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367789_comment'></div>公之父也。二十三叶之德善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367789_comment'></div>钟其人<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作仁）</span>于公。公刚方廉清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367789_comment'></div>贞信宏宽。德厚性和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367789_comment'></div>与四时气侔。非天下之直道不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367789_comment'></div>非先王之法言未尝言。当出处去就之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367789_comment'></div>非抑与不苟求。与朋友交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367789_comment'></div>非同道不苟合。至守王事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367789_comment'></div>临大节。非其正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367789_comment'></div>虽临大兵不惧。恪德危行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367789_comment'></div>居易中立。不可得而亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367789_comment'></div>不可得而疏。读书观忠孝大略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367789_comment'></div>不索隐赜。属词止乎礼义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367789_comment'></div>不止咏情性而已。太极元年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367789_comment'></div>诏举文可以经邦国者。宣劳使源乾曜以公充赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367789_comment'></div>时对策者数百人。公与荥阳郑少微特冠科首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367789_comment'></div>起家拜同州合阳县尉。岁满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367789_comment'></div>授好畤县尉。开元十四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367789_comment'></div>玄宗初登封泰山。注意二千石令长以煦妪下民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367789_comment'></div>授公益州温江令。公治县如治家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367789_comment'></div>明不至察。威不至猛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367789_comment'></div>去烦苛缴绕之政。施德信刑礼以训齐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367789_comment'></div>温江人饮公之化。逋者复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367789_comment'></div>疲者悦。善者劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367789_comment'></div>不善者知耻。益州刺史张敬忠以状闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367789_comment'></div>诏授监察御史。转殿中侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367789_comment'></div>会权臣恶直。斥去不附已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367789_comment'></div>贬公庐州长史。明年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367789_comment'></div>恶直者罢位。公稍移武功令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367789_comment'></div>未到官病免。二十三年除宁州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367789_comment'></div>二十八年迁颍川郡长史。初公为御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367789_comment'></div>尝以直忤吏部侍郎李林甫。是时林甫当国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367789_comment'></div>常欲骋憾于我。而五府三署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367789_comment'></div>每有高选。群公皆昌言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367789_comment'></div>称公全才。且各以臧文窃位自引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367789_comment'></div>由是得免于咎。然十年再迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367789_comment'></div>而位不离郡佐。或劝公卑其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367789_comment'></div>可以取容于世。公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367789_comment'></div>可卑非吾道也。屈伸天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367789_comment'></div>非人也。人其如予何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367789_comment'></div>天宝元年加朝散大夫。二年七<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作二）</span>月七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367789_comment'></div>寝疾终于位。春秋五十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367789_comment'></div>位不尊。寿不遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367789_comment'></div>志不行。善不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367789_comment'></div>其直虚语。守道者相吊以为痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367789_comment'></div>是岁八月。殡于郡东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367789_comment'></div>至德二年岁次丁酉十月十四日。权迁窆于洛阳龙门山西冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1367789_comment'></div>大历四年五月十三日。诏赠秘书监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1367789_comment'></div>命卿之位。锡于身后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1367789_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。夫人河南洛阳人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1367789_comment'></div>薛国长孙览之元孙。咸阳县丞讳顿府君之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1367789_comment'></div>左金吾将军讳子哲府君之妹。禀天元和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1367789_comment'></div>生知孝慈。含德之厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1367789_comment'></div>与坤体合。执笄助祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1367789_comment'></div>四十馀载。人莫见夫人喜怒之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1367789_comment'></div>躬勤顺承。动叶礼经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1367789_comment'></div>宗族以睦。长幼以序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1367789_comment'></div>无言无为。化成于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1367789_comment'></div>公之加命服也。夫人封封邱县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1367789_comment'></div>氾等既孤。夫人弃采蘋之度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1367789_comment'></div>修释氏教。受正观法于长老比邱尼上方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1367789_comment'></div>服勤一年。得四念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1367789_comment'></div>处三昧。视去诸结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1367789_comment'></div>犹弃涕涶。至德二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1367789_comment'></div>随子东征。明年岁在戊戌七月二十四日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1367789_comment'></div>终于会稽。享寿六十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1367789_comment'></div>八月某日。权殡于雷门之南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1367789_comment'></div>氾巨及正等遭天不吊。无恃无怙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1367789_comment'></div>以世故坎壈。不克迁祔者十一年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1367789_comment'></div>欲报顾复。天胡有极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1367789_comment'></div>今年问宅兆于前都水使者张系。系卜甘泉东伊水西甘泉乡之原吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1367789_comment'></div>谨以岁次已酉秋七月壬午。迁公夫人灵坐合安厝于此原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1367789_comment'></div>犹惧陵谷世人之不我期也。故不敢不志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1367789_comment'></div>抆血勒石。以贻后嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1367789_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_117_1367789_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年10月</a>　在洛阳。作品：《唐故给事中赠吏部侍郎萧公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1367782' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367782' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367782?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故给事中赠吏部侍郎萧公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（769年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367782")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367782_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367782'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367782'>公讳直。字正仲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367782_comment'></div>梁长沙王懿七代孙。有唐御史中丞临汝郡守谅之孟子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367782_comment'></div>聪秀英达。忠敏孝敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367782_comment'></div>志强体和。才方而圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367782_comment'></div>果于从政。当断不惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367782_comment'></div>有妙用明识。足以济众利物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367782_comment'></div>与朋友重然诺。见于一贵一贱之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367782_comment'></div>十岁能属文工书。十三游上庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367782_comment'></div>十七举明经上第。名冠太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367782_comment'></div>二十馀以书记参朔方军事。中丞府君之遇谗谪居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367782_comment'></div>公亦播迁汉东。移尉谷熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367782_comment'></div>至德二年。乃由廷尉评授监察御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367782_comment'></div>历河南府户曹京兆府司录参军。其后骤升尚书户部库部司勋吏部四曹郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367782_comment'></div>自殿中进兼侍御史中丞徐州刺史。广德元年中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367782_comment'></div>一岁四迁。更七职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367782_comment'></div>朝廷难奉使之选。谓非公莫可故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367782_comment'></div>永泰元年拜太子左庶子。大历三年授给事中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367782_comment'></div>前后居官二十。辟书记支使判官副使行军司马贰使臣之车者八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367782_comment'></div>出入冠柱后惠文冠者六。所从之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367782_comment'></div>则朔方元帅张怀钦汴州刺史李彦允扬州刺史李成式户部尚书李公峘故相国今户部侍郎第五公琦今相国黄门侍郎王公缙中书侍郎元公载其人也。当乾元上元中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367782_comment'></div>大憝未静。王室之安危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367782_comment'></div>惟方面藩镇是瞻。公所佐之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367782_comment'></div>必以忠力主画。疑谋危事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367782_comment'></div>谈笑而决。刀笔之所加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367782_comment'></div>应机成务。谈者称其多才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367782_comment'></div>初公居先公夫人之丧。外除犹毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367782_comment'></div>其后母弟立卒。公期不绝哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367782_comment'></div>再期悬不乐。食不肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367782_comment'></div>谈者高其孝友。人有缓急大小之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367782_comment'></div>必储必副。内姻外姻与所知之丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367782_comment'></div>必匍匐而救之。赗含加于人一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367782_comment'></div>谈者服其仁爱。其为庶子<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作至是以为庶子）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367782_comment'></div>给事黄门。出入两宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367782_comment'></div>优游三公间。皆得其欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367782_comment'></div>方谓六卿九伯之位。可坐而拾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367782_comment'></div>命不我与。天孤人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367782_comment'></div>岁在丁酉二月二日。终于静安里正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367782_comment'></div>春秋四十六。谈者叹其名与位与才与时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367782_comment'></div>四者皆并。独寿不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367782_comment'></div>时辈以为痛。三月二十五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367782_comment'></div>诏赠吏部侍郎。嗣子策密莒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367782_comment'></div>羸然衔哀。奉丧来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367782_comment'></div>冬十月甲午。卜葬于洛阳龙门冈先中丞茔之左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367782_comment'></div>礼也。先其期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367782_comment'></div>论撰功烈。以墓铭乞其父友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367782_comment'></div>孝也。余欲塞其孝思之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367782_comment'></div>故录其实。以志其大节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367782_comment'></div>不欲华其文也。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367782_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1367782'>天地气和。灵芝吐葩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367782_comment'></div>德善下钟。才子承家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367782_comment'></div>为言为行。是构是荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367782_comment'></div>天子谓公。济美忠文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367782_comment'></div>骆马铁冠。俾佐使臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367782_comment'></div>周爰海隅。抚循斯民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367782_comment'></div>往践诸曹。亦倅戎车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367782_comment'></div>一麾出守。言隼其旟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367782_comment'></div>乃推<span class='inlineComment2'>（大典作擢）</span>铜楼。复登明庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367782_comment'></div>竹花梧叶。栖食兹始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367782_comment'></div>曷云不淑。今也遄已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367782_comment'></div>万里可到。中途而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367782_comment'></div>逝者如斯。化往莫留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367782_comment'></div>瑶林琼树。零落山邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367782_comment'></div>匪石之贞。曷纪德休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367782_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_63_1367782_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年11月</a>　十一月，葬夫人韦氏于洛阳并做墓志。作品：《前左骁卫兵曹参军河南独孤公故夫人韦氏墓志》<div id='poem_1367763' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367763' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367763?labeling=true' target='_blank'>前左骁卫兵曹参军河南独孤公故夫人韦氏墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（769年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367763")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367763_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367763'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367763'>夫人讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367763_comment'></div>字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367763_comment'></div>楚王交傅孟裔孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367763_comment'></div>唐许州司马皎曾孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367763_comment'></div>渭南主簿懿之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367763_comment'></div>兖州金乡县尉商伯季女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367763_comment'></div>秘书省著作郎睦州刺史攒之妹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367763_comment'></div>其先自彭城郡徙京兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367763_comment'></div>从丞相贤后九世至本州大中正穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367763_comment'></div>始有东西眷之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367763_comment'></div>二十五世至徵士夐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367763_comment'></div>居魏周二代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367763_comment'></div>出不降志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367763_comment'></div>处不随俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367763_comment'></div>时人号为逍遥公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367763_comment'></div>夫人之七世祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367763_comment'></div>逍遥公生民部尚书建安公世恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367763_comment'></div>建安生上大将军宋州刺史仁祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367763_comment'></div>将军生给事中旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367763_comment'></div>即许州之祢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367763_comment'></div>夫以四言之遗直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367763_comment'></div>一经之遗烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367763_comment'></div>十徵之高风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367763_comment'></div>焯于古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367763_comment'></div>宜其秉哲垂懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367763_comment'></div>百代不陨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367763_comment'></div>地之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367763_comment'></div>望之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367763_comment'></div>与春秋之唐杜范氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367763_comment'></div>汉晋之袁杨王谢侔其炽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367763_comment'></div>大矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367763_comment'></div>三十八叶之明德茂祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367763_comment'></div>降衷于夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367763_comment'></div>故孝慈贞俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367763_comment'></div>温惠淑慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367763_comment'></div>文敏好礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367763_comment'></div>三者皆天机生知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367763_comment'></div>不待师训而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367763_comment'></div>广德二年夏六月归于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367763_comment'></div>衣服饮食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367763_comment'></div>躬自菲薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367763_comment'></div>夙夜戒敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367763_comment'></div>致孝于荇菜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367763_comment'></div>接娣姒以谦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367763_comment'></div>驭幼贱以敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367763_comment'></div>敦善劝义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367763_comment'></div>恕不知而矜不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367763_comment'></div>喜怒未尝见于容止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367763_comment'></div>其德礼所化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367763_comment'></div>宗族以睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367763_comment'></div>儿童知让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367763_comment'></div>生一子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367763_comment'></div>四岁而夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367763_comment'></div>大历四年夏六月癸丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367763_comment'></div>再孕不育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367763_comment'></div>乙卯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367763_comment'></div>殁于舒州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367763_comment'></div>春秋若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367763_comment'></div>仁厚而不福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367763_comment'></div>德备而不寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367763_comment'></div>是天不惠于我家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367763_comment'></div>向使锡厥永年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367763_comment'></div>正家承筐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367763_comment'></div>宜尔子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367763_comment'></div>百禄是享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367763_comment'></div>非夫人曷归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367763_comment'></div>启手足之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367763_comment'></div>长幼号咷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367763_comment'></div>外姻内姻亲疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367763_comment'></div>皆行哭失声也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367763_comment'></div>宜哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367763_comment'></div>是岁九月甲申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367763_comment'></div>以輤裧裳帷迁于洛阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367763_comment'></div>十一月丁巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367763_comment'></div>安宅兆于舅姑先茔之西南隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367763_comment'></div>恐时逝事迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367763_comment'></div>景行不贻于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367763_comment'></div>故刊石以志卒葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367763_comment'></div>且谨而日之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_78_1367763_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年</a>　秋，离洛阳归濠州，别前有诗与友人赠答。作品：《自东都还濠州奉酬王八谏议见赠》<div id='poem_40905' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_40905' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_40905", 40905, "Clauses/17/Comments/1")'>由缘</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_40905_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 衢州

id='poem_sentence_1_1367796_comment'></div>谨以清酌庶羞之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367796_comment'></div>敬祭于衢州司士参军李君之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367796_comment'></div>安卑道存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367796_comment'></div>宜锡难老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367796_comment'></div>亦高其门。<div id='poem_content_1367795'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367795'>年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367795_comment'></div>某官某乙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367795_comment'></div>谨以觞豆之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367795_comment'></div>敬祭于故某部郎中兼某州刺史员公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367795_comment'></div>吴越𠌤岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367795_comment'></div>元元艰食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367795_comment'></div>帝咨四岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367795_comment'></div>分命于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367795_comment'></div>克勤于邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367795_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1367795", 1367795, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>克俭</span>于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367795_comment'></div>忠而能力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367795_comment'></div>刚亦不吐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367795_comment'></div>出入台阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367795_comment'></div>将十五载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367795_comment'></div>动合律度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367795_comment'></div>言为程式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367795_comment'></div>及兹剖符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367795_comment'></div>衔疾受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367795_comment'></div>而慨然有表正东夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367795_comment'></div>澄清江湖之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367795_comment'></div>海隅苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367795_comment'></div>方望公以大庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367795_comment'></div>朝廷搢绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367795_comment'></div>期公以上台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367795_comment'></div>而悠悠苍天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367795_comment'></div>屈公以下寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367795_comment'></div>时既须而命不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367795_comment'></div>智未穷而生有涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367795_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367795_comment'></div>昔公绣衣持斧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367795_comment'></div>予忝接武于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367795_comment'></div>公负谴<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1367795", 1367795, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>投荒</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367795_comment'></div>予亦左衽异域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367795_comment'></div>山川有间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367795_comment'></div>交情无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367795_comment'></div>各随流波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367795_comment'></div>在天一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367795_comment'></div>险阻艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367795_comment'></div>亦既备尝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367795_comment'></div>邂逅相遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367795_comment'></div>荆蛮之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367795_comment'></div>惠而好我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367795_comment'></div>何日能忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367795_comment'></div>浙右巨镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367795_comment'></div>甬东孤城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367795_comment'></div>风烟相接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367795_comment'></div>吊伐同盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367795_comment'></div>未及前驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367795_comment'></div>莫申微诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367795_comment'></div>遽闻沈疴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367795_comment'></div>忽间死生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367795_comment'></div>九原谁归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367795_comment'></div>万事长往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367795_comment'></div>夙昔欢爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367795_comment'></div>无非梦想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367795_comment'></div>舟逝壑走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367795_comment'></div>吾将安仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367795_comment'></div>只鸡之荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367795_comment'></div>灵兮歆飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1367795_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='58e2b248ae974805b41efc3a942b67d5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("58e2b248ae974805b41efc3a942b67d5");'><span id='58e2b248ae974805b41efc3a942b67d5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>，36岁</div><div id='58e2b248ae974805b41efc3a942b67d5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　服除，入淮南等节度使李峘幕府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年11月</a>　在淮南幕，宋州刺史刘展反，独孤及随李峘于扬州御敌。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
镇江（丹徒）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ba1f40e63f034d8a9256b9d7786c5f0b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ba1f40e63f034d8a9256b9d7786c5f0b");'><span id='ba1f40e63f034d8a9256b9d7786c5f0b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>，36岁</div><div id='ba1f40e63f034d8a9256b9d7786c5f0b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　在淮南幕，扬州失守，随李峘守京口。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宣州（宣城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ca7e40603b10458983449ef1caf84e3c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ca7e40603b10458983449ef1caf84e3c");'><span id='ca7e40603b10458983449ef1caf84e3c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>，36岁</div><div id='ca7e40603b10458983449ef1caf84e3c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　在淮南幕，京口失守，随李峘奔宣城。<br /></div>
