-----title
南昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b853a785ac8a4fa8985e8be8bab7a437_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b853a785ac8a4fa8985e8be8bab7a437");'><span id='b853a785ac8a4fa8985e8be8bab7a437_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=761')">760-761年</a>，36-37岁</div><div id='b853a785ac8a4fa8985e8be8bab7a437' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年12月</a>　在淮南幕，宣城失守，随李峘奔洪州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=761&endYear=761')">761年1月</a>　在淮南幕，正月，刘展之乱平，有为李峘奏破刘展兵捷表。作品：《为江淮都统使奏破刘展兵捷书表》<div id='poem_1367649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367649?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为江淮都统使奏破刘展兵捷书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（761年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367649")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367649'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367649'>臣闻圣人之生。不能使大盗不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367649_comment'></div>唐尧之代。时则有四凶在列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367649_comment'></div>王制所以诛不恪。讨不庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367649_comment'></div>小者市朝。大者原野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367649_comment'></div>奸宄草窃。何代无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367649_comment'></div>刘展包藏祸心。为日固久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367649_comment'></div>敢肆奸慝。乘间阻兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367649_comment'></div>长驱凶徒。掩臣未备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367649_comment'></div>以伪言乱众。谓天命在已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367649_comment'></div>于是有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1367649", 1367649, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>豕食</span>淮泗。鲸吞荆吴之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367649_comment'></div>使黎庶播越。人神愤怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367649_comment'></div>臣职司靖难。敢不戮力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367649_comment'></div>当凭庙略。以殄寇仇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367649_comment'></div>谨遣副使少府少监摄侍御史李藏用屯兵杭州。伺隙进讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367649_comment'></div>且分处隘害。以遏其唐突。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367649_comment'></div>贼众狃于初役。师轻而骄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367649_comment'></div>不虞吾军能折其锐也。乃以今月三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367649_comment'></div>使其伪将军张干朱法云等。领步卒七千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367649_comment'></div>马军六百。径入杭州东门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367649_comment'></div>焚烧闾阎。鼓噪而进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367649_comment'></div>藏用引其精锐。设伏于途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367649_comment'></div>羸师张之。使入死地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367649_comment'></div>然后整堂堂之阵。以薄其垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367649_comment'></div>使左厢兵马使潭州长史李澄为左军。左第一将张嵓光先锋将李强李陵等佐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367649_comment'></div>都押衙高干为右军。左押衙杨履和都虞候魏守寂佐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367649_comment'></div>左第二将皇甫山栖左三将梁朝康承寂左四将吴季之李楚玉颜光允等。督游军之骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367649_comment'></div>以弥缝其阙。表里合战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367649_comment'></div>奇正夹攻。以将帅之馀勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367649_comment'></div>因黎元之积愤。奋皆敢死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367649_comment'></div>登必争先。赤羽交而三军风生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367649_comment'></div>金鼓鸣而万夫气作。自卯至午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367649_comment'></div>覆而败之。神扶电扫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367649_comment'></div>雷落山破。噍类无馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367649_comment'></div>只车莫返。锋镝之血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367649_comment'></div>朱殷长江。甲齐崇山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367649_comment'></div>尸作京观。实赖陛下聪明齐圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367649_comment'></div>与日月合照。故能虑图发于樽俎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367649_comment'></div>而威灵加于远方。臣等尽敌如拾芥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367649_comment'></div>成功如指掌。恶气沴祲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367649_comment'></div>扫荡无馀。海隅苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367649_comment'></div>比屋何幸。臣无任庆快之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367649_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1367649_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=761&endYear=761')">761年1月</a>　在淮南幕，正月，刘展之乱平，有贺田神功平刘展表。作品：《为江淮都统使贺田神功平刘展表》<div id='poem_1367647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为江淮都统使贺田神功平刘展表</a><span class='authorDate'>（761年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367647")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367647'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367647'>臣某言。得田神功等状称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367647_comment'></div>官军以正月二十六日过江。大破贼众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367647_comment'></div>擒元恶于算山之下。凶残扑灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367647_comment'></div>江界无事。臣某诚欢诚喜顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367647_comment'></div>臣闻四时成岁。秋为司杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367647_comment'></div>故圣人则之。以作五兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367647_comment'></div>盖奸宄贼寇。或乘衅而起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367647_comment'></div>则干戈弧矢。亦有时而用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367647_comment'></div>陛下率遏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1367647", 1367647, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>乱略</span>。再造区宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367647_comment'></div>欃枪旬时。竹破瓦解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367647_comment'></div>蕞尔狂狡。敢干天诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367647_comment'></div>作为长蛇。荐食江汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367647_comment'></div>乃矫诬我天命。攘窃我王师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367647_comment'></div>暴殄我城邑。俶扰我边鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367647_comment'></div>荆吴之人。若坠泉谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367647_comment'></div>万姓业业。奔走无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367647_comment'></div>陛下神聪不测。睿算无方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367647_comment'></div>将欲擒之。必固纵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367647_comment'></div>先侈其心。而厚其毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367647_comment'></div>然后制胜两楹之下。授略千里之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367647_comment'></div>使神功等一战而陷阵。再战而逐北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367647_comment'></div>三战而擒渠魁。系颈以索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367647_comment'></div>覆巢倾穴。刮野扫地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367647_comment'></div>如烈风之破骇浪。严霜之陨落叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367647_comment'></div>浃辰之内。平扬州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367647_comment'></div>定淮南。下朱方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367647_comment'></div>收三吴。流亡者复故业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367647_comment'></div>涂炭者返寿域。扇以皇风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367647_comment'></div>与之更始。遂令东土耆老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367647_comment'></div>复见汉官威仪。非陛下乃文乃武之鸿烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367647_comment'></div>日用不知之元化。孰能阴骘圣功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367647_comment'></div>如此其速。臣无任庆忭之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367647_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1367647_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=761&endYear=761')">761年2月</a>　在淮南幕，有文为李峘东归作。作品：《祭纛文》<div id='poem_1367810' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367810' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367810?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为李峘祭纛文</a><span class='authorDate'>（761年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367810")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367810_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367810'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367810'>年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367810_comment'></div>都统江淮之南节度观察处置等使户部尚书李峘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367810_comment'></div>谨以少牢之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367810_comment'></div>敬祭于六纛之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367810_comment'></div>天地不仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367810_comment'></div>神明无亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367810_comment'></div>惟正是与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367810_comment'></div>若响之答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367810_comment'></div>敢有象恭滔天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367810_comment'></div>搆衅称乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367810_comment'></div>国有明罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367810_comment'></div>神其舍诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367810_comment'></div>贼臣刘展。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367810_comment'></div>假宠多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367810_comment'></div>敢包狼心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367810_comment'></div>窃发虿毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367810_comment'></div>将敷虐于我上下神祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367810_comment'></div>使东溟扬波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367810_comment'></div>群动昏垫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367810_comment'></div>皇帝震怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367810_comment'></div>按剑授钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367810_comment'></div>命我上将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367810_comment'></div>厎天之伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367810_comment'></div>于是有虎牙鹰扬之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367810_comment'></div>蛇矛犀渠之群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367810_comment'></div>横行而东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367810_comment'></div>我伐用张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367810_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1367810", 1367810, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>月羽</span>云旗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367810_comment'></div>以先启行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367810_comment'></div>方将历浔阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367810_comment'></div>下南陵。<div id='poem_sentence_52_1367810_comment'></div>为神祇羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367810_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1367810_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=761&endYear=761')">761年3月</a>　为会师平叛的庐州刺史徐浩写真图撰赞文。作品：《尚书右丞徐公写真图赞并序》<div id='poem_1367742' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367742' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367742?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书右丞徐公写真图赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（761年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367742")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367742_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367742'>侍御史韩公至(一作志)清。以学艺书画之美。闻于天下。辛丑岁三月。以王事靡盬。馆于豫章。与前尚书右丞徐公同舍于慧命寺之净室。尝以暇日。裂素洒翰。画徐公之容。陈于公之座隅。而美目方口。和气秀骨。毫釐无差。若分形于镜。入自外者。或欲擎跽曲拳。俯偻拜谒。不知其画也。众君子嗟叹之不足。则言以赞其美。及亦继唱于后。乃赞之曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367742_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367742'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367742'>哲匠运思，天姿是具。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367742'>假之笔精，实以神遇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367742'>居然成象，豁若披雾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367742'>瞻仰神锋，如窥武库。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367742'>婉婉高识，昂昂独步。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367742'>绝顶孤松，空陂白鹭。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367742'>不犯之色，匪躬之故。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367742'>孰知其<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作造）</span>化，亦在毫素。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367742_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367742'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1367742_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: 苏州（吴县）

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=761&endYear=761')">761年12月15日</a>　在苏州，于虎丘山夜宴，有序纪事。作品：《建丑月十五日虎邱山夜宴序》<div id='poem_1367681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367681' class='poemTitle class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367681_comment'></div>高枕无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367681_comment'></div>则琴壶以宴朋友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367681_comment'></div>啸歌以展霞月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367681_comment'></div>吾党之职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367681_comment'></div>吾是以有今兹虎邱之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367681_comment'></div>岩岩虎邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367681_comment'></div>奠吴西门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367681_comment'></div>崒然如香楼金道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367681_comment'></div>自下方而踊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367681_comment'></div>锁丹霞白云于莲宫之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367681_comment'></div>会之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367681_comment'></div>和气满谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367681_comment'></div>阳春逼人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367681_comment'></div>岩烟扫除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367681_comment'></div>肃若有待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367681_comment'></div>余与夫不乱行于鸥鸟者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367681_comment'></div>衔流霞之杯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367681_comment'></div>而群嬉乎其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367681_comment'></div>笑向碧潭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367681_comment'></div>与松石道旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367681_comment'></div>兕觥既发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367681_comment'></div>宾主醉止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367681_comment'></div>狂歌送酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367681_comment'></div>坐者皆和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367681_comment'></div>吴趋数奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367681_comment'></div>云去日没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367681_comment'></div>梵天月白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367681_comment'></div>万里如练。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367681_comment'></div>松荫依依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367681_comment'></div>状若留客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367681_comment'></div>于斯时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367681_comment'></div>抚云山为我辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367681_comment'></div>视竹帛如草芥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367681_comment'></div>颓然乐极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367681_comment'></div>众虑皆遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367681_comment'></div>于是奋髯屡舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367681_comment'></div>而叹今夕何夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367681_comment'></div>同者八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367681_comment'></div>醉罢皆赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367681_comment'></div>以为此山故事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1367681_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年4月</a>　在苏州。作品：《观世音菩萨等身绣像赞并序》<div id='poem_1367746' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367746' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367746?labeling=true' target='_blank'>观世音菩萨等身绣像赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367746")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367746_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367746'>元年建寅月。前相州安阳县令何昌系。以是月甲子。当受生之辰。痛欲报而罔极。哀现在之无住。顾非大雄之慈。法云之悲。则莫能救拯我无明苦果。敷佑我宏誓愿力。乃彰施五色。以刺绣成文。写菩萨之真相。等观音之全身。于是乎谛观睟容。瞻仰圣位。知海潮之梵音不远。莲花之法座可识。将令功德池水。溉灌其三业。菩提根芽。发生于一雨。至哉。安阳之树善也宏矣。欲广其善。利以偈赞云。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367746_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367746'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367746'>法云垂荫，光破<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1367746", 1367746, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>黑业</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367746_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367746'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1367746", 1367746, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>五眼</span>周视，四魔怖慑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367746_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367746'>以色观空，于相见法。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367746_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367746'>永植慈缘，恒沙亿劫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367746_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367746'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1367746_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年9月</a>　在苏州，是年苏州大疫。作品：《吊道殣文并序》<div id='poem_1367811' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367811' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367811?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吊道殣文</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367811")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367811_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367811'>辛丑岁大旱。三吴饥甚。人相食。明年大疫。死者十七八。城郭邑居。为之空虚。而存者无食。亡者无棺殡悲哀之送。大抵虽其父母妻子。亦啖其肉而弃其骸于田野。由是道路积骨。相支撑枕藉者。弥二千里。春秋已来不书。或谓县官处师旅饥馑之弊。宜穰灾于未然。既将不时赈恤。又苦之以杼轴。故及是。及以为不然。当阳九之厄。阴阳错而灾沴降。天也非人也。于是延陵包佶。作道殣文。盖小雅云汉之流。及亦斐然献吊。且告之运命云。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367811_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367811'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367811'>八风不和。六气不均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367811_comment'></div>上天疾威。大厉荐臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367811_comment'></div>俾灾流行。殄歼斯人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367811_comment'></div>北自淮沂。达于海隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367811_comment'></div>札瘥天昏。亦既毒痡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367811_comment'></div>匪蹈密网。匪罹萑蒲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367811_comment'></div>饥馑降丧。沦胥以铺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367811_comment'></div>人生寄世。孰非远客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367811_comment'></div>嗟尔赋命。天年逼迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367811_comment'></div>生不糊其口。死不掩其骼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367811_comment'></div>旷野茫茫。僵尸累累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367811_comment'></div>髑髅峥嵘。如堆如坻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367811_comment'></div>里闾无烟。鸡犬去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367811_comment'></div>死非尔所。鬼其馁而。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367811_comment'></div>水陷历阳。贵贱同之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367811_comment'></div>秦坑赵卒。内填长平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367811_comment'></div>实天不佣。谓祸莫京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367811_comment'></div>尔复胡为。无辜命并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367811_comment'></div>将天阏之。则如勿生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367811_comment'></div>司杀之柄。孰云孔明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367811_comment'></div>伊昔太古。上元之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367811_comment'></div>天无鞠凶。物无疵厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367811_comment'></div>父不丧子。兄不哭弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367811_comment'></div>亦有华胥。民寿千年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367811_comment'></div>阴阳常和。玉烛常然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367811_comment'></div>彼何人斯。而生斯时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367811_comment'></div>圣人既兴。大盗亦随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367811_comment'></div>外户反闭。贤愚相欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367811_comment'></div>我先王乃作五兵。固不得已而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367811_comment'></div>尧舜既殁。揖让不传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367811_comment'></div>黄钺白旄。谓之应天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367811_comment'></div>德乃下衰。干戈相连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367811_comment'></div>阳九祅兴。灾缠凶年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367811_comment'></div>鸟皆夜鸣。人失其全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367811_comment'></div>食尽力疲。守死道边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367811_comment'></div>不自予后。不自尔先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367811_comment'></div>万世一时。运有固然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367811_comment'></div>帝在法宫。清问下民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367811_comment'></div>青旗鸾辂。时令惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367811_comment'></div>叶风和布。天下皆春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367811_comment'></div>尔往莫及。委骸穷尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367811_comment'></div>命不可问。呜呼苍旻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367811_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1367811_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年10月</a>　在苏州。作品：《扬州庆云寺律师一公塔铭并序》<div id='poem_1367753' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367753' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367753?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故扬州庆云寺律师一公塔铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367753")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367753_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367753'>公讳灵一。俗姓吴。广陵人也。神气清和。方寸地灵。与太初元精。合其纯粹。闻思修惠。介然生知。九岁出家。三千断结。严持律藏。将绍法宝。示人文学。以诱世智。初不计身中有我。我中有身。德充报圆。缘断相灭。宝应元年冬十月十六日。终于杭州龙兴寺。春秋三十有六。临灭顾命。以香木茶毗。为送终之节。门弟子虔奉遗旨。粤以是月某日。焚身于某山。起塔于某原。从拘尸城之制也。右补阙赵郡李纾。殿中丞侍御史顿邱李汤。尝以文字言语。游公廊庑。至是相与追录遗懿。以诒尘劫。谓公贞静直方。渊远宏大。而密识洞鉴。天倪道机。注不满。酌不竭。冲如也。自受生至于出家。贪恚不入念。哀乐不见色。自出家至于涅槃。六根不染欲界之尘。自知道至于返真。双履不践居士之门。公之严持也。初公之先世为富家。既削发。推万金之产。悉以让诸孤昆季。所取者独衲衣锡杖。及身而三。舍七界五欲。如弃涕唾。公之纯白也。其所底止。必择山间树下无尘垢之地。初舍于会稽南山之南悬溜寺焉。与禅宗之达者释隐空虔印静虚相与讨十二部经第一义谛之旨。既辨惑。徙居馀杭宜丰寺。邻青山。对佳境。以岭松涧石为梵宇。竹风月露为丈室。超然独往。与法印俱。自是师资两忘。空色皆遣。暴风偃山。而正智不动。巨浪沃日。而浮囊自安。于是著法性论以究实谛。公之悬解也。公智刃先觉。法施无方。每禅诵之隙。辄赋诗歌事。思入无间。兴含飞动。潘阮之遗韵。江谢之阙文。公能缀之。盖将吻合词林。与儒墨同其波流。然后循循善诱。指以学路。由是与天台道士潘清广陵曹评赵郡李华颍川韩极中山刘颖襄阳朱放赵郡李纾顿邱李汤南阳张继安定皇甫冉范阳张南史清河房从心相与为尘外之友。讲德味道。朗咏终日。其终篇必博之以文。约之以修。量其根之上下而投之以法味。欲使俱入不二法流。公示教之攘门也。内张天机。外与物接。舍法无我。以虚受人。旷焉若空谷之响。止水之象。优而柔之。使自得之。其道枢未始不无为也。而饮其和者。亦虚而来。实而归。明徵其所以然。则不得其眹。公应之无涯也。宜丰寺地临高隅。初无井泉。公之戾止。有灵泉呀然而涌。喷金沙之溜。于禅庭左右。挹之弥清。之无穷。公精至感物也。呜呼。日发天启寿量彼一劫住世圣道以拯拔丧得大云而凉火宅。其公乎。吁嗟昊穹。夺我善友。使生不极其涯。道不竟其源。岂前已就。诸有可出。将转现他方乎。为应化之始终。法身之去来。非思议所及乎。凡今学徒戒归。若涉大水而无梁。抽毫强名。以志陈迹。其铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367753_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367753'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367753'>茫茫五浊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367753'>爱习如债。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1367753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1367753'>飞鸟无迹。<div id='poem_sentence_25_1367753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1367753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1367753'>来者曷问。<div id='poem_sentence_28_1367753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1367753'>言之糟粕。<div id='poem_sentence_29_1367753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1367753'>留为秘印<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1367753_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1367753'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_8_1367753_0'>⑴ 英华作卓尔立志于焉悬解持佛秘藏俾道勿坏</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_30_1367753_0'>⑵ 谨按自知道至于返真以下文苑英华作双舄不践居士之门六根不染欲界之尘学无常师悟不以渐内以了因證心果外以惠用接物与止水空谷同其应和而法施不住天机无方精义元言或形于章句骚雅之遗韵陶谢之缺文公能缀之其终篇必以了义博约和者量其根之上下而投以法味饱其风者亦虚而来实而归或以足言言必缘情一缘则万缘作而诸相见无乃不可乎曰佛法自利他不系于权实将善诱之心咱和之固曰示入固波可也公又尝谓无生正位实相宗本二乘所感谈者莫究于是著法性论以辨之而迦叶后问惠远奥旨騞焉疑断涣若冰释者是以为向使大启寿量好务宏道则法王度闻非公孰寄呜呼生不极其涯道不竟其源岂应物之缘住世之数止于是乎为世缔之始终报身之去来非思议之所及乎清尘缅然学者安仰若涉大水而无舟航儒生强名以志陈迹</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1367753_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

湖州（武康）

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年11月</a>　在湖州武康令任。作品：《送贺若员外巡按毕归朝序》<div id='poem_1367684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送贺若员外巡按毕归朝序</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367684")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367684'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367684'>今年春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367684_comment'></div>上以富人侯为丞相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367684_comment'></div>百揆时叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367684_comment'></div>九州赋错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367684_comment'></div>方欲齐职贡之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367684_comment'></div>崇厎慎之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367684_comment'></div>使六府修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367684_comment'></div>九叙成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367684_comment'></div>谓尚书吏部郎贺若公贞明直躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367684_comment'></div>特达公器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367684_comment'></div>才足以茂功蒇事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367684_comment'></div>政足以宏道救物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367684_comment'></div>故俾绣衣持斧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367684_comment'></div>巡抚江介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367684_comment'></div>分王命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367684_comment'></div>公电发神机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367684_comment'></div>霜淬智刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367684_comment'></div>其始至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367684_comment'></div>问谣俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367684_comment'></div>省疾苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367684_comment'></div>命司书示年数之上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367684_comment'></div>削郡县之版图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367684_comment'></div>且为之实其多与寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367684_comment'></div>以差等井赋焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367684_comment'></div>然后劳之来之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367684_comment'></div>安之集之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367684_comment'></div>俾其有宁宇而族聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367684_comment'></div>以宣天子之宏恩而煦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367684_comment'></div>于是乎民之乐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367684_comment'></div>如饥者之得以食也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367684_comment'></div>寒者之获以纩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367684_comment'></div>乃使苞茅之贡必叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367684_comment'></div>而杼轴之诗亦不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367684_comment'></div>冬十一月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367684_comment'></div>爰命郡吏致事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367684_comment'></div>言旋于京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367684_comment'></div>且将捧府檄于南陔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367684_comment'></div>侍版舆以西上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367684_comment'></div>事有成而功不伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367684_comment'></div>以是觐扬天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367684_comment'></div>以尽考绩之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367684_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367684_comment'></div>夫其由家以及于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367684_comment'></div>资事亲以事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367684_comment'></div>甘旨之未遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367684_comment'></div>勤于王家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367684_comment'></div>奔走之不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367684_comment'></div>以显亲身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367684_comment'></div>斯真能奉慈训不废陈力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367684_comment'></div>将君命不违色养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367684_comment'></div>忠孝之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367684_comment'></div>又人子人臣之所难及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367684_comment'></div>而况奸宄已弭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367684_comment'></div>干戈将戢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367684_comment'></div>天子方以律令章程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367684_comment'></div>责成三府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367684_comment'></div>然则操六辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367684_comment'></div>骤四骆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367684_comment'></div>周爰咨询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367684_comment'></div>以成天下之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367684_comment'></div>在是行乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367684_comment'></div>翰飞方骋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367684_comment'></div>瞻望何及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367684_comment'></div>唯献酬东阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367684_comment'></div>弼成大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367684_comment'></div>使烝人粒海水静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367684_comment'></div>农夫高枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367684_comment'></div>及亦预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367684_comment'></div>凡执手于路者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367684_comment'></div>请偕赋鸿雁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367684_comment'></div>取之子于征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367684_comment'></div>劬劳于野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367684_comment'></div>爰及矜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367684_comment'></div>哀此𩻴寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367684_comment'></div>以为善颂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1367684_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
南丰
-----detail

showDetail'><a href='/Writing/40917?labeling=true' target='_blank'>癸卯岁赴南丰道中闻京师失守寄权士繇韩幼深</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a onclick='ShowAllusionComment(596, "poem_allusion_40917")'>不须向新亭</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5689, "poem_allusion_40917")'>世间歧路</span></div><div "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>策名</span>不遭时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_40917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_40917'>胡尘晦落日，西望泣路岐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_40917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_40917'>猛虎啸北风，麇麚皆载驰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_40917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_40917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_40917'>白云失帝乡，远水恨天涯。<div id='poem_sentence_10_40917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_40917'>昂藏双威凤，曷月还西枝。<div id='poem_sentence_11_40917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_40917'>努力爱华发，盛年振羽仪。<div id='poem_sentence_12_40917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_40917'>但令<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_40917", 40917, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>迍难</span>康，不负沧洲期。<div id='poem_sentence_13_40917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_40917'>莫作新亭泣，徒使夷吾嗤。<div id='poem_sentence_14_40917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_40917'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_40917_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南宁
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='06f630852c214cdb9048dc4b3adf66d7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("06f630852c214cdb9048dc4b3adf66d7");'><span id='06f630852c214cdb9048dc4b3adf66d7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=764')">763-764年</a>，39-40岁</div><div id='06f630852c214cdb9048dc4b3adf66d7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　冬末，至邕州，为经略使幕府判官。作品：《马退山茅亭记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　是年或在邕州，有文，姑系于此。作品：《唐故朝议大夫申王府司马上柱国赠太常卿韦公神道碑铭》<div id='poem_1367758' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367758' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367758?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故朝议大夫申王府司马上柱国赠太常卿韦公神道碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367758")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367758_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367758'>楚元王傅后五世。长孺相汉。始自鲁国徙家杜陵。其后十六世孙景略。仕魏为青州刺史。青州生隋仓部侍郎南皮公瓒。南皮公生三子皆才。同时为郎。长曰季武。实居主爵。次曰叔谐。典司库部。季曰叔谦。历吏部考功。时人号为三列宿。考功生知人。以司库员外郎为职方郎中。自长孺至青州。二丞相。一侍中。十一二千石。自南皮至职方。二叶五尚书郎。为当世言婚宦者谓之郎官韦家。楩楠瑶琨。非崇山浚源不生。故公侯卿大夫。实钟德门。事业名声。与冠盖俱。四牡龙旂之庆。百代弥炽。盛矣哉。公讳缜。字某。职方之仲子也。性忠廉无邪。温直好礼。用诚明博厚。祇若祖考之训。虽颠沛不违仁。非得之不苟求。言足以成事而济众。默足以居易而慎独。乡举经行。吏部登贤能。拔授秘书省校书郎。亲累徙官。再迁至亳州临涣县令。宽仁恺悌之政。行乎千室。期年而颂声兴。迁薛王府文学。转秘书郎。王宫图牒。天禄典籍。公皆以儒服参焉。艺文修而彝章叙。历佐濮徐仙三州。清恪如一。入为申王府司马。以达才居陪臣之列。宏道以奉职。安义以直已。谏从政肃。繄忠亮是赖。掌邦典者。谓王门之治。可移于公卿。方议登之三府。会寝疾终于位。是岁开元十二年岁在甲子冬十月二十二日。春秋若干。夫人河南元氏。益州唐安县主簿知柔之女。承先祖供祭祀之谓职。闵勤劳劝以义之谓德。庄敬恭顺婉娩听从之谓礼。顾复劳瘁均养善训之谓慈。夫人兼有焉。某年月日。春秋若干卒。某年月日。合葬于某原。呜呼。才宜贵。仁宜寿。世禄宜富。三者公夫人皆居其地。不臻其分。乡党宗族。以命不可说相吊焉。惟明德必有后之言也信。有若孟子幼成。博见利器。铿若金锡。天宝十年。自尚书兵部郎出守汉中兼山南西道采访处置使。移典河内。河内人至今颂之。仲子幼卿。洛阳县丞。叔子幼奇。宋州楚邱县令。季子幼章。有贞干密识。恭宽而明。前后八执宪而再起草。自兵部郎中持节典泗楚二州。锡金印紫绶。咨以屯田赡军食。如汉营平侯故事。以言以立。皆公之教训也。宝应二年春三月。以子为大夫。故诏追赠公太常卿。君子谓公之义方。庆及其身。而楚州之孝诚格于宗祏。礼也。犹以为与化俱者人事。不我期者邱陇。虽大宗小宗。可详诸姓氏谱。命官日时。各存乎屋壁之志。若遗直与故事。非金石刻。则无以示后世也。由是楚州稽首于庙。见托撰德。垂懿万亿。孝思罔极。其铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367758_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367758'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367758'>肃肃乃祖，翼商屏周。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367758'>总群邦兮，退傅间生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367758'>扶扬重侯，德乃降兮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367758'>龟纽虎符，黼衣彤弓。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367758'>世相副兮，百代纯嘏。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367758'>钟仁于公，德斯懋兮。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367758'>为邦三年，足民知方。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367758'>政之臧兮，校文石渠。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367758'>观书鲁堂，志自强兮。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367758'>三佐列郡，曳裾游梁。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1367758'>道未光兮，已矣介福。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1367758'>不充景行，吁嗟命兮。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1367758'>一经之遗，垂裕果盛。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1367758'>哀荣并兮，子子孙孙。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1367758'>丕承忠敬，荷馀庆兮。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1367758_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1367758'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1367758_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年</a>　年初，在邕州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
抚州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='83ff986a19ec419080201797d899ef36_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("83ff986a19ec419080201797d899ef36");'><span id='83ff986a19ec419080201797d899ef36_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年</a>，40岁</div><div id='83ff986a19ec419080201797d899ef36' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年</a>　夏秋之际在抚州。作品：《抚州南城县客馆新亭记》<div id='poem_1367735' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367735' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367735?labeling=true' target='_blank'>抚州南城县客馆新亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（764年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367735")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367735_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367735'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367735'>古者国野之道。十里有庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367735_comment'></div>庐有饮食。三十里有宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367735_comment'></div>宿有路室。于是乎宾客有止息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367735_comment'></div>羁旅有寄寓。而是邦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367735_comment'></div>与两越七闽。犬牙其疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367735_comment'></div>守官者以为地遐途穷。而琐琐行迈之罕到也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367735_comment'></div>则杀其礼而阙其物焉。无修除之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367735_comment'></div>无井树之设。及客至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367735_comment'></div>则候人不为导。里不授馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367735_comment'></div>而盘飧薪刍之贶弆如也。由是途而往者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367735_comment'></div>佥曰陋如之何。是岁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367735_comment'></div>台司审县尹之寄。擢王公昕为南城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367735_comment'></div>公至之日。则制其事典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367735_comment'></div>陈其艺极。视年之上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367735_comment'></div>去民之疾苦。凡三月而南城之人和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367735_comment'></div>于是饰厩置以候宾客。葺旅次以待羁旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367735_comment'></div>夏六月。筑其馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367735_comment'></div>辨其域于道周。作新亭于馆之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367735_comment'></div>厦屋耽耽。俯瞰浚壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367735_comment'></div>宾位在左。主位在右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367735_comment'></div>然后铲硗确。堙坎窞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367735_comment'></div>以为大逵。属之于溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367735_comment'></div>设双船于清津。以备径渡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367735_comment'></div>每将之迎之。则自郊劳至于致饩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367735_comment'></div>无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1367735", 1367735, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>旷礼</span>。无违物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367735_comment'></div>而兹亭之经始也。取废彻之材以利用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367735_comment'></div>用乃有节。入鞭扑之赎以庀工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367735_comment'></div>工忘其劳。崇栋宇之制以礼宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367735_comment'></div>宾至如归。三者不愆于素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367735_comment'></div>功是以懋。政是以立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367735_comment'></div>若行者有犯軷之祭。居者修饮饯之好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367735_comment'></div>登斯临斯。酾酒以赠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367735_comment'></div>溪云竹风。生于栋牖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367735_comment'></div>而绿野青山为之亭障。三爵之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367735_comment'></div>可以送千里之目。可以道四方之志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367735_comment'></div>兹又胜会之佳境也。凡厎绩以兴利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367735_comment'></div>革故以谋始。修礼以备物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367735_comment'></div>僝功以成务。政之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367735_comment'></div>宜其刊作者之茂实。以示后嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367735_comment'></div>不然。他山之石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367735_comment'></div>何以在此。是岁广德二年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367735_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1367735_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
九江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c23231bf9b074e70b2de2f67a78dd626_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c23231bf9b074e70b2de2f67a78dd626");'><span id='c23231bf9b074e70b2de2f67a78dd626_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=765')">764-765年</a>，40-41岁</div><div id='c23231bf9b074e70b2de2f67a78dd626' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年</a>　冬末，在江州。作品：《卢郎中寻阳竹亭记》<div id='poem_1367737' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367737' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367737?labeling=true' target='_blank'>卢郎中浔阳竹亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（764年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367737")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367737_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367737'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367737'>古者半夏生。木槿荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367737_comment'></div>君子居高明。处台榭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367737_comment'></div>后代作者。或用山林水泽鱼鸟草木以博其趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367737_comment'></div>而佳景有大小。道机有广狭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367737_comment'></div>必以寓目放神。为性情筌蹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367737_comment'></div>则不俟沧洲而閒。不出户庭而适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367737_comment'></div>前尚书右司郎中卢公。地甚贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367737_comment'></div>心甚远。欲卑其制而高其兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367737_comment'></div>故因数仞之邱。伐竹为亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367737_comment'></div>其高出于林表。可用远望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367737_comment'></div>工不过凿户牖。费不过剪茅茨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367737_comment'></div>以俭为饰。以静为师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367737_comment'></div>辰之良。景之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367737_comment'></div>必作于是。凭南轩以瞰原隰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367737_comment'></div>冲然不知锦帐粉闱之贵于此亭也。亭前有香草怪石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367737_comment'></div>杉松罗生。密筱翠竿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367737_comment'></div>腊月碧鲜。风动雨下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367737_comment'></div>声比箫籁。亭外有山围湓城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367737_comment'></div>峰名香炉。归云轮囷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367737_comment'></div>片片可数。天香天鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367737_comment'></div>若在耳鼻。是其所以誇逋客而傲汉貂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367737_comment'></div>百里奚爵禄不入。故饭牛而牛肥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367737_comment'></div>卢公恬智相养。于是竹亭构而天机畅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367737_comment'></div>尝试论亭之趣。夫物不感则性不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367737_comment'></div>故景对而心驰也。欲不足则患不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367737_comment'></div>故意惬而神完也。耳目之用系于物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367737_comment'></div>得丧之源牵于事。哀乐之柄成乎心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367737_comment'></div>心和于内。事物应于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367737_comment'></div>则登临殊途。其适一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367737_comment'></div>何必嬉东山。褉兰亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367737_comment'></div>爽志荡目。然后称赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367737_comment'></div>公欲其迹之可久。故命余为志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367737_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1367737_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　初春，仍在江南，与李纾、李嘉祐唱和。作品：《将赴京答李纾赠别》<div id='poem_40865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_40865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/40865?labeling=true' target='_blank'>将赴京答李纾赠别</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_40865")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_40865_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' "poem_allusion_40865")'>胶漆</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7261, "poem_allusion_40865")'>日三秋</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_40865_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_sentence_0_40865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_40865'>帝乡今独往，沟水便分流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_40865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
滁州（钟离）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='58153fa6a3cd4a5a83fd8b6be3f8efa3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("58153fa6a3cd4a5a83fd8b6be3f8efa3");'><span id='58153fa6a3cd4a5a83fd8b6be3f8efa3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=769')">768-769年</a>，44-45岁</div><div id='58153fa6a3cd4a5a83fd8b6be3f8efa3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年闰6月12日</a>　到濠州任，有谢表。作品：《谢濠州刺史表》<div id='poem_1367655' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367655' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367655?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢濠州刺史表</a><span class='authorDate'>（768年闰6月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367655")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367655_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367655'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367655'>臣及言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367655_comment'></div>臣伏奉今年五月一日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367655_comment'></div>授臣使持节濠州诸军事濠州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367655_comment'></div>臣顷待罪礼官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367655_comment'></div>备位郎署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367655_comment'></div>职旷无补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367655_comment'></div>增惧且愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367655_comment'></div>陛下不以臣愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367655_comment'></div>擢居二千石之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367655_comment'></div>今之刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367655_comment'></div>古之诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367655_comment'></div>州人安否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367655_comment'></div>系在一吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367655_comment'></div>臣非其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367655_comment'></div>无以称旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367655_comment'></div>奉诏之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367655_comment'></div>惧有甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367655_comment'></div>以闰六月十二日到所部上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367655_comment'></div>惟当奉宣圣猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367655_comment'></div>竭诚帅下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367655_comment'></div>瞻恋天造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367655_comment'></div>酬效无阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367655_comment'></div>臣无任喜惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367655_comment'></div>谨附驿奉表陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367655_comment'></div>臣及诚惶诚恐顿首顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1367655_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年8月4日</a>　在濠州任，八月，荐朱巨川为钟离令。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年2月</a>　在濠州任。作品：《唐故朝议大夫高平郡别驾权公神道碑铭并序》<div id='poem_1367759' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367759' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367759?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故朝议大夫高平郡别驾权公神道碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（769年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367759")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367759_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367759'>开元天宝之际。玄宗始以八柄付三公。由是台司得专其废置。其中或凭宠固位。惧天下有异已者。诸附离之者皆出入三台。若公才令名。以望见惮。则稍稍优其俸而黜其职。故天水权公幼明由新安县令为绛郡司马高平郡别驾而殁。同于道者皆窃叹之。是岁天宝六载秋八月也。殁后廿有二载。岁次巳未春二月。返葬洛阳故茔。夫人新郑县君荥阳郑氏祔焉。县君某县某官某之孙某之子。以仁俭好礼。辅佐懿德。柔明之风。训齐闺门。寿六十五。大历二年十月某日。终于丹阳。初公娶于博陵崔氏。生子曰骅而终。新郑以继室。生四子。曰轶。曰申。曰器。曰舒。舒不幸短命。骅轶申器。悉忠信好学。善属文。位未显而令名归之。庆之垂训之流也。至是既卜宅兆。骅等惧日月逾远。后裔不知其先人之德善。谓及忝乡举之旧。故使录而铭之云。公讳彻。字幼明。陇西天水人也。权氏之先。出于颛顼。其远相殷武丁之小子。生而有文在手曰权。因以权受封。且命氏焉。至周为楚武王所灭。国除。其后有仕陇西者。遂家于天水。历汉魏晋宋间。子孙世都尉为郡守。至裔孙翼。与王景略同佐苻坚。官至仆射。后仆射数世至景宣。景宣生士玢。并知名于时。士玢生万春。历华州刺史。封千金县公。华州嗣右领军将军曰文奖。领军嗣永兴令曰怀育。公永兴之嗣也。奕叶之明德粹气。丛于其躬。故融而为仁行。播而为文学。童子时。舅氏崔湜奇其文。尝谓有何无忌之似。其乡举也。考功郎中苏颋拔诸群萃之中。连尉湖城汾阴新繁渭南河南五县。开元二十三年拜监察御史。会监祭太庙。先时同事者约相与偕赴。及将赴祭。约者有故不至。遽不暇告。公曰。人约我矣。可先已而后信乎。遂不赴。坐是降为河南府法曹。君子义之。初选部旧制。每岁孟冬以书判选多士。至开元十八年。乃择公廉无私工于文者。考校甲乙丙丁科。以辨论其品。是岁。公受诏与徐安贞王敬从吴巩裴朏李宙张烜等十学士参焉。凡所升奖。皆当时才彦。考判之目。由此始也。于是天下无兵百二十馀载。搢绅之徒。用文章为耕耘。登高不能赋者。童子大笑。公攘臂其间。以仁义为已任。片言只字。动为学者所法。时辈荣之。而居家清方。惟德礼是仗。润身饬吏。不过经术。不矫持操以游媚贵倖。行威作福者忌之。由是官徙而阶不迁。从法曹数岁而后有新安之拜。及至历绛郡高平。任愈疏远。安贞中立。未尝易方。虚舟其心。与位升降。春秋六十四而终。盖道之行止。与时不并。论者以汉梁叔敬桓君山为比。公所著文二十卷。其立言之宗。赵郡李华编而序之。若世系事业。则书诸斯文。其文曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367759_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367759'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367759'>咺兮权公，有德有言。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367759'>忠恕廉清，道直而温。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367759'>行有馀力，言足成文。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367759'>居官釐绩，勤约是守。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367759'>与明以信，宁黜不苟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367759'>迹屈志伸，义彰身后。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367759'>冉政游学，左诗潘诔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367759'>风流遗烈，足以遗子。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367759'>九原与归，末由也已。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367759'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1367759_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年3月</a>　在濠州任，约于此年三月游庄周台，有诗纪事。作品：《垂花坞醉后戏题赋得俱字韵并序》（紫蔓青条拂酒壶）<div id='poem_40849' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_40849' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/40849?labeling=true' target='_blank'>垂花坞醉后戏题<span class='inlineComment2'>（赋得俱字韵。并序。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（769年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_40849")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_40849_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_40849'>庄周台南十许步，有丘一成。上有樛藤垂花，而蔓草荒之，且隔大沟，路不可陟。道士张太和伐薪为堰，封土以壅浍。余亦命薙氏治芜秽而刬宿莽，遂辟为登赋之位，位广二席，席间足以函尊酒二簋。三月戊子，及群英由堰而升焉。诸花倒垂，下拂杯案，紫葩缡縰，如钗如旒。众君子瞻弄之不足，故秉烛进酒，以继落日，欲称醉而不能也。因命其地曰垂花坞，堰曰缘花堰，亦饰之以诗云。</div><div id='poem_preface_40849_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_40849'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(74, "poem_allusion_40849")'>鯈鱼</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_40849_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_40849'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_40849'>紫蔓青条拂酒壶，落花时与竹风俱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_40849_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_40849'>归时自负花前醉，笑向<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(74, "poem_sentence_1_40849")'>鯈鱼</span>问乐无。<div id='poem_sentence_1_40849_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_40849'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_40849_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年6月</a>　在濠州任，六月，夫人韦氏卒。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6cf9d5b7ee384330bdedb1fbf092c5f7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6cf9d5b7ee384330bdedb1fbf092c5f7");'><span id='6cf9d5b7ee384330bdedb1fbf092c5f7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=770')">769-770年</a>，45-46岁</div><div id='6cf9d5b7ee384330bdedb1fbf092c5f7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年</a>　在濠州任，此年有李华集序。作品：《检校尚书吏部员外郎赵郡李公中集序》<div id='poem_1367723' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367723' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367723?labeling=true' target='_blank'>检校尚书吏部员外郎赵郡李公中集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（769年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367723")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367723_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367723'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367723'>志非言不形。言非文不彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367723_comment'></div>是三者相为用。亦犹涉川者假舟楫而后济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367723_comment'></div>自典谟缺。雅颂寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367723_comment'></div>世道陵夷。文亦下衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367723_comment'></div>故作者往往先文字后比兴。其风流荡而不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367723_comment'></div>乃至有饰其词而遗其意者。则润色愈工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367723_comment'></div>其实愈丧。及其大坏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367723_comment'></div>俪偶章句。使<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1367723", 1367723, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>枝对叶比</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367723_comment'></div>以八病四声为梏拲。拳拳守之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367723_comment'></div>如奉法令。闻皋繇史克之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367723_comment'></div>则呷然笑之。天下雷同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367723_comment'></div>风驱云趋。文不足言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367723_comment'></div>言不足志。亦犹木兰为舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367723_comment'></div>翠羽为楫。玩之于陆而无涉川之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367723_comment'></div>痛乎流俗之惑人也旧矣。帝唐以文德敷祐于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367723_comment'></div>民被王风。俗稍丕变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367723_comment'></div>至则天太后时。陈子昂以雅易郑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367723_comment'></div>学者浸而向方。天宝中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367723_comment'></div>公与兰陵萧茂挺长乐贾幼几勃焉复起。振中古之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367723_comment'></div>以宏文德。公之作本乎王道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367723_comment'></div>大抵以五经为泉源。抒情性以托讽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367723_comment'></div>然后有歌咏。美教化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367723_comment'></div>献箴谏。然后有赋颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367723_comment'></div>悬权衡以辩天下公是非。然后有论议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367723_comment'></div>至若记序编录铭鼎刻石之作。必采其行事以正褒贬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367723_comment'></div>非夫子之旨不书。故风雅之指归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367723_comment'></div>刑政之本根。忠孝之大伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367723_comment'></div>皆见于词。于时文士驰骛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367723_comment'></div>飙扇波委。二十年间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367723_comment'></div>学者稍厌折杨皇荂。而窥咸池之音者什五六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367723_comment'></div>识者谓之文章中兴。公实启之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367723_comment'></div>公名华。字遐叔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367723_comment'></div>赵郡人。安邑令府君第三子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367723_comment'></div>质直而和。纯固而明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367723_comment'></div>旷达而有节。中行而能断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367723_comment'></div>孝敬忠廉。根于天机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367723_comment'></div>执亲之丧。哀达神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367723_comment'></div>其任职釐绩。外若坦荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367723_comment'></div>内持正性。谏不犯颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367723_comment'></div>见义乃勇。举善惟惧不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367723_comment'></div>务去恶如复仇。与朋友交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367723_comment'></div>然诺著于天下。其伟词丽藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367723_comment'></div>则和气之馀也。学博而识有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367723_comment'></div>才多而体愈迅。每述作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367723_comment'></div>笔锋风生。听者耳骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367723_comment'></div>开元二十三年举进士。天宝二年举博学宏词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367723_comment'></div>皆为科首。由南和尉擢秘书省校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367723_comment'></div>八年历伊阙尉。当斯时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367723_comment'></div>唐兴百三十馀年。天下一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367723_comment'></div>朝廷尚丈。夫羿工乎中微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367723_comment'></div>拙于使人无已誉。公才与时并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367723_comment'></div>故不近名而名彰。时辈归望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367723_comment'></div>如鳞羽之于虬龙也。十一年拜监察御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367723_comment'></div>会权臣窃柄。贪猾当路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367723_comment'></div>公入司方书。出按二千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367723_comment'></div>持斧所向。郡邑为肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367723_comment'></div>为奸党所嫉。不容于御史府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367723_comment'></div>除右补阙。禄山之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367723_comment'></div>方命圯族者蔽天聪明。勇者不得奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367723_comment'></div>明者不得谋。公危行正词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367723_comment'></div>献纳以诚。累陈诛凶渠完封疆之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367723_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1367723", 1367723, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>阍犬</span>迎吠。故书留不下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367723_comment'></div>时继太夫人在邺。初潼关败书闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367723_comment'></div>或劝公走蜀诣行在所。公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367723_comment'></div>奈方寸何。不若间行问安否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367723_comment'></div>然后辇母安舆而逃。谋未果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367723_comment'></div>为盗所获。二京既复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367723_comment'></div>坐谪杭州司功参军。太夫人弃敬养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367723_comment'></div>公自伤悼以事君故。践危乱而不能安亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367723_comment'></div>既受污。非其疾而贻亲之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367723_comment'></div>及随牒愿终养。而遭天不吊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367723_comment'></div>由是衔罔极之痛者三。故虽除丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367723_comment'></div>抱终身之戚焉。谓志已亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367723_comment'></div>息陈力之愿焉。因屏居江南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367723_comment'></div>省躬遗名。誓心自绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367723_comment'></div>无何。诏复授左补阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367723_comment'></div>又加尚书司封员外郎。玺书连徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367723_comment'></div>公卿已下。倾首延伫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367723_comment'></div>至之日将以司言处公。公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367723_comment'></div>焉有隳节夺志者。可以荷君之宠乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367723_comment'></div>遂移疾请告。故相国梁公岘之领选江南也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367723_comment'></div>表为从事。加检校吏部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367723_comment'></div>明年遇风痹。徙家于楚州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367723_comment'></div>疾痼贫甚。课子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367723_comment'></div>力农圃。赡衣食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367723_comment'></div>雅好修无生法。以冥寂思虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367723_comment'></div>视爵禄形骸。与遗土同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367723_comment'></div>惟吴楚之士君子。撰家传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367723_comment'></div>修墓版。及都邑颂贤守宰功德者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367723_comment'></div>靡不赍货币。越江湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1367723_comment'></div>求文于公。得请者以为子孙荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1367723_comment'></div>公遇暇日。时复缀录以应其求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1367723_comment'></div>过是而往。不复著书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1367723_comment'></div>少时所著者。多散落人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1367723_comment'></div>自志学至校书郎已前八卷。并常山公主志文窦将军神道碑崔河南生祠碑礼部李侍郎碑安定三孝论哀旧游诗韩幼深避乱诗序祭王员外端沈起居兴宗裴员外腾文别元旦诗并杨骑曹集序王常山碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1367723_comment'></div>并因乱失之。名存而篇亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1367723_comment'></div>自监察御史已后所作颂赋诗歌碑表叙论志记赞祭。凡一百四十三篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1367723_comment'></div>公长子羔字宗绪。编为二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1367723_comment'></div>号中集。其中陈王业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1367723_comment'></div>则无疆颂。主文而谲谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1367723_comment'></div>则言医含元殿赋。敦礼教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1367723_comment'></div>则哀节妇赋灵武二孝赞。表贤达盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1367723_comment'></div>则崔宾客集序元鲁山碣房太尉德政碑平原张公颂梁国李公传德先生诔权著作墓志李太夫人传卢夫人颂。一死一生之间抒其交情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1367723_comment'></div>则祭萧功曹刘评事张评事文。吟咏情性达于事变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1367723_comment'></div>则咏古诗。思旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1367723_comment'></div>则三贤论。辨卿大夫之族姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1367723_comment'></div>则卢监察神道碑。自叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1367723_comment'></div>则别相里造范伦序。诠佛教心要而合其异同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1367723_comment'></div>则南泉真禅师左溪朗禅师碑。其馀虽波澜万变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1367723_comment'></div>而未始不根于典谟。故览公之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1367723_comment'></div>知公之质。不俟觌容貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1367723_comment'></div>听词气。假令束带立于史臣之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1367723_comment'></div>足以润色王度。天而病之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1367723_comment'></div>时不幸欤。公之病也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1367723_comment'></div>尝以斯文见托。诒某书曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1367723_comment'></div>桓谭论扬雄当有身后名。华亦谓足下一桓谭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1367723_comment'></div>及于公才。宜播其述作之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1367723_comment'></div>明于后人。故拜命之辱而不让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1367723_comment'></div>今乃著其文德。为之冠于篇首焉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1367723_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_119_1367723_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1367723'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_118_1367723_0'>⑴ 自监察御史已下文苑英华作自监察御史已后迄至于今所著述者公长男羔字宗绪编而集之断自监察御史已前十卷号为前集其后二十卷颂赋诗碑表叙论志记赞祭文凡一百四十四篇为中集其中陈王业则无疆颂议世道则卜原论质文论主文而谲谏则言医含元殿赋敦礼教则哀节妇赋灵武二孝赞与外孙女二孩书表贤达盛德则元鲁山碣房太尉颂德铭崔宾客集序平原张公颂梁国李公传德先生诔权著作墓表李夫人传卢夫人颂一死一生之间抒其交情则祭萧功曹刘评事张博士文吟咏情性达于事变则咏古诗辨卿大夫族姓则卢监察神道碑思旧则三贤论自叙则别相里造范伦序诠佛教心要而会其异同则南泉真禅师左溪朗禅师碑其馀虽比兴万变而未始不根于道德故览公之文知公之质不俟觌容貌听词气而后睹其行若使束带立于史臣之位其备献替足以润色王度正一代之训典天而病之国不幸也然遐叔身甚病而心甚壮文益赡而才不竭则前路逸气讵可度矣他日继于此而作者当为后集及常游公之藩也久故录其述作之所以然著于篇</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1367723_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=770&endYear=770')">770年7月18日</a>　移舒州刺史加朝散大夫。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b753ef30542447cd8042e4ba06822407_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b753ef30542447cd8042e4ba06822407");'><span id='b753ef30542447cd8042e4ba06822407_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年</a>，50岁</div><div id='b753ef30542447cd8042e4ba06822407' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年3月</a>　三月，赴常州刺史任，途经滁州，晤刺史李幼卿。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
潜山（怀宁）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='24be4a80d1af4562aa4eaea09ac93f26_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("24be4a80d1af4562aa4eaea09ac93f26");'><span id='24be4a80d1af4562aa4eaea09ac93f26_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=770&endYear=770')">770年9月27日</a>　到舒州任，有谢表。作品：《谢舒州刺史兼加朝散大夫表》<div id='poem_1367656' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367656' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367656?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢舒州刺史兼加朝散大夫表</a><span class='authorDate'>（770年9月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367656")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367656_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367656'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367656'>臣及言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367656_comment'></div>臣奉七月十八日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367656_comment'></div>加臣朝散大夫使持节舒州诸军事舒州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367656_comment'></div>充当州团练守捉使兼知淮南岸当界缘江贼盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367656_comment'></div>臣典濠州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367656_comment'></div>无政可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367656_comment'></div>人幸不扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367656_comment'></div>时和所致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367656_comment'></div>流者稍复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367656_comment'></div>年登之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367656_comment'></div>臣亦何敢贪此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367656_comment'></div>以为已能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367656_comment'></div>陛下过听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367656_comment'></div>骤降殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367656_comment'></div>既增之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367656_comment'></div>又命以服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367656_comment'></div>无德受赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367656_comment'></div>愧孰甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367656_comment'></div>仰戴皇渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367656_comment'></div>且荣且惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367656_comment'></div>今以九月二十七日到州上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367656_comment'></div>州经积年寇盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367656_comment'></div>疮痍之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367656_comment'></div>百姓流窳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367656_comment'></div>十不一存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367656_comment'></div>臣以奉宣圣慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367656_comment'></div>与之休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367656_comment'></div>劳来鳏寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367656_comment'></div>薄其徭赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367656_comment'></div>是以招携亡者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367656_comment'></div>辑柔存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367656_comment'></div>庶经秋之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367656_comment'></div>赖获安集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367656_comment'></div>非曰能尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367656_comment'></div>冀竭力焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367656_comment'></div>臣无任感戴之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367656_comment'></div>谨奉表陈谢以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1367656_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=770&endYear=770')">770年</a>　在舒州任，有文祭相里造。作品：《祭相里造文》<div id='poem_1367804' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367804' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367804?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭相里造文</a><span class='authorDate'>（770年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367804")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367804_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367804'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367804'>年月日。舒州刺史独孤及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367804_comment'></div>敬以清酌之奠。敬祭于河南少尹赠礼部侍郎相里公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367804_comment'></div>呜呼。往岁尝与公度论死生变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367804_comment'></div>岂不知身与万物。悉当归无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367804_comment'></div>犹谓不惑于道者。可以不夺其算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367804_comment'></div>岂图论犹在耳。目未及瞬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367804_comment'></div>而公度之身。复为异物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367804_comment'></div>益知观化而怛。自古皆妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367804_comment'></div>而哀来从中。妄岂易遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367804_comment'></div>呜呼公度。有志有文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367804_comment'></div>量足韬世。善可救物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367804_comment'></div>宰赐言语。冉季政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367804_comment'></div>古莫两大。繄公兼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367804_comment'></div>伊昔密荐可否。廷折凶佞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367804_comment'></div>京师童儿。亦知公名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367804_comment'></div>其后江人杭人。颂德不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367804_comment'></div>洛表耆老。徯公而苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367804_comment'></div>秉公论者。无贤不肖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367804_comment'></div>孰不谓公。致君致身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367804_comment'></div>方自此始。奈何吉未会也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367804_comment'></div>凶问随之。天下悼惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367804_comment'></div>士友悽欷。况某投分于策名之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367804_comment'></div>并命于剖符之列。久要不忘平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367804_comment'></div>实惟公度是望。同心同病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367804_comment'></div>我身子身也。子与化往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367804_comment'></div>奈我心何。名迹留为故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367804_comment'></div>话言存乎耳目。惟音形<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1367804", 1367804, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>眇忽</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367804_comment'></div>无前期可望。每一念至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367804_comment'></div>哀填胸臆。往矣公度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367804_comment'></div>去我何之。勿言一樽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367804_comment'></div>永无共持。倘肯顾飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367804_comment'></div>表公我思。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367804_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1367804_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=770&endYear=770')">770年</a>　在舒州任，与皇甫冉有酬唱。作品：《酬皇甫侍御望天灊山见示之作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（在舒州时作，但年月不能确定，今系于此。）</span><div id='poem_40926' id='poem_sentence_23_1367799_comment'></div>徒虚语耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367799_comment'></div>惟公贞亮温毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367799_comment'></div>强学好古。<div id='poem_sentence_33_1367799_comment'></div>施于有政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367799_comment'></div>故其德形于事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367799_comment'></div>其仁浃于百姓。<div id='poem_sentence_38_1367799_comment'></div>识者揣公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367799_comment'></div>寿与位偕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367799_comment'></div>今也溘焉。<div id='poem_sentence_48_1367799_comment'></div>岂不顾飨于今日蘋藻之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367799_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1367799_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a id='poem_sentence_8_1367657_comment'></div>臣闻尧舜建官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367657_comment'></div>三考黜陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367657_comment'></div>汉代二千石以循良称者。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1367657_comment'></div>十犹六七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367657_comment'></div>徵遣征赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367657_comment'></div>未尝及期。<div id='poem_sentence_23_1367657_comment'></div>幸固深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367657_comment'></div>岂谓皇恩骤降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367657_comment'></div>复以古典命臣。<div
