href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年</a>　在舒州任。作品：《暮春于山谷寺上方遇恩命加官赐服酬皇甫侍御之作》《琅琊溪述并序》<div id='poem_40885' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_40885' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/40885?labeling=true' target='_blank'>暮春于山谷寺上方遇恩命加官赐服詶皇甫侍御见贺之作</a><span class='authorDate'>（771年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_40885")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_40885_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_40885'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_40885'>天书到法堂，朽质被荣光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_40885_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_40885'>自笑无功德，殊恩谬激扬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_40885_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_40885'>还登建礼署，犹忝会稽章。<div id='poem_sentence_2_40885_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_40885'>佳句惭相及，称仁岂易当。<div id='poem_sentence_3_40885_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_40885'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_40885_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367751' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367751' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367751?labeling=true' target='_blank'>琅琊溪述</a><span class='authorDate'>（771年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367751")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367751_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367751'>陇西李幼卿。字长夫。以右庶子领滁州。而滁人之饥者粒。流者占。乃至无讼以听。故居多暇日。常寄傲此山之下。因凿石引泉。酾其流以为溪。溪左右建上下坊。作禅堂琴台以环之。探异好古故也。按图经。晋元帝之居琅琊邸而为镇东也。尝游息是山。厥迹犹存。故长夫名溪曰琅琊。他日赋八题。题于岸石。及亦状而述之。是岁大历六年岁次辛亥春三月丙午日。述曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367751_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367751'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367751'>自有此山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367751_comment'></div>便有此泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367751_comment'></div>不浚不刊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367751_comment'></div>几万斯年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367751_comment'></div>造物遗功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367751_comment'></div>若俟后贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367751_comment'></div>天钟灵奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367751_comment'></div>公润色之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367751_comment'></div>疏为回溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367751_comment'></div>削成崇台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367751_comment'></div>山不过十仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367751_comment'></div>意拟衡霍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367751_comment'></div>溪不袤数丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367751_comment'></div>趣侔江海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367751_comment'></div>知足造适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367751_comment'></div>境不在大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367751_comment'></div>怪石皑皑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367751_comment'></div>涌湍潺潺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367751_comment'></div>洞壑无底。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367751_comment'></div>云兴其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367751_comment'></div>仲春气至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367751_comment'></div>草木华发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367751_comment'></div>亘陵被坂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367751_comment'></div>吐火喷云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367751_comment'></div>公登山乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367751_comment'></div>乐者毕同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367751_comment'></div>无小无大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367751_comment'></div>乘兴从公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367751_comment'></div>公举觞酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367751_comment'></div>酒酣气振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367751_comment'></div>溪水为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367751_comment'></div>而身为宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367751_comment'></div>舍瑟咏歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367751_comment'></div>同风舞雩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367751_comment'></div>时时醉归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367751_comment'></div>与夕鸟俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367751_comment'></div>明月满山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367751_comment'></div>朱轓徐驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367751_comment'></div>石门松风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367751_comment'></div>声类笙竽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367751_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367751_comment'></div>人实宏道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367751_comment'></div>物不自美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367751_comment'></div>向微羊公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367751_comment'></div>游汉之涘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367751_comment'></div>岘山寂寞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367751_comment'></div>千祀谁纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367751_comment'></div>彼美新溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367751_comment'></div>维公嗣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367751_comment'></div>念兹疲人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367751_comment'></div>繄公其肥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367751_comment'></div>后之聆清风而叹息者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367751_comment'></div>挹我于泉乎已而。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1367751_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年</a>　在舒州任，时在五六月，当地大旱。作品：《祭吴塘神祈雨文》<div id='poem_1367807' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367807' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367807?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭吴塘神祈雨文</a><span class='authorDate'>（771年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367807")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367807_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367807'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367807'>某年月日。朝散大夫检校司封郎中兼舒州刺史独孤及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367807_comment'></div>谨以清酌之奠。敢昭告于吴塘神之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367807_comment'></div>山作灵镇。神实司之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367807_comment'></div>人作神主。及实尸之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367807_comment'></div>神非人罔以荐馨香。人非神罔以降福祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367807_comment'></div>馨香不荐。伊人之尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367807_comment'></div>福祥不降。亦神之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367807_comment'></div>及剖符为邦。今二年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367807_comment'></div>制节谨度。不敢怠遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367807_comment'></div>庶无罪悔。以奉禋祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367807_comment'></div>祀未丰洁。政或颇颣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367807_comment'></div>实及之责。非人之愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367807_comment'></div>惟神祐之。俾大有年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367807_comment'></div>今盛夏旱蒸。五稼将枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367807_comment'></div>田畯诉号。靡知其辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367807_comment'></div>神明岂不降鉴下土。油然为云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367807_comment'></div>沛然作雨。使万人欢康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367807_comment'></div>百谷阜滋。洒我公田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367807_comment'></div>遂及我私。我京我庾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367807_comment'></div>维万维亿。岂伊人粒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367807_comment'></div>神亦血食。众心禺禺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367807_comment'></div>非岁曷望。望之济否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367807_comment'></div>惟神所相。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367807_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1367807_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年5月</a>　在舒州任，有文祭岏山神祈雨。作品：《祭岏山神祈雨文》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年</a>　在舒州任，是年贾至卒，有祭文。作品：《祭贾尚书文》<div id='poem_1367803' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367803' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367803?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭贾尚书文</a><span class='authorDate'>（772年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367803")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367803_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367803'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367803'>维大历七年四月二十一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367803_comment'></div>朝散大夫检校尚书司封郎中兼舒州刺史赐紫金鱼袋独孤及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367803_comment'></div>谨以清酌庶羞之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367803_comment'></div>敬祭于故散骑常侍赠礼部尚书贾公六兄之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367803_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367803_comment'></div>性命之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367803_comment'></div>仲尼罕言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367803_comment'></div>顷者与兄存而不论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367803_comment'></div>亦谓景福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367803_comment'></div>必钟德门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367803_comment'></div>未虞昊天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367803_comment'></div>骤忍我欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367803_comment'></div>所以分手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367803_comment'></div>容易前期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367803_comment'></div>日往书札。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367803_comment'></div>祗嗟别离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367803_comment'></div>孰云别中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367803_comment'></div>死生间之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367803_comment'></div>贾生谪去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367803_comment'></div>遭世不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367803_comment'></div>以命问鹏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367803_comment'></div>千古犹痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367803_comment'></div>兄逢盛世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367803_comment'></div>任适梁栋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367803_comment'></div>青云咫尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367803_comment'></div>巨麟始纵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367803_comment'></div>溘尔中止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367803_comment'></div>俄同大梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367803_comment'></div>天下孤望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367803_comment'></div>非兄谁恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367803_comment'></div>追念夙昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367803_comment'></div>尝陪讨论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367803_comment'></div>综覈微言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367803_comment'></div>揭厉孔门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367803_comment'></div>匪究枝叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367803_comment'></div>必探本根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367803_comment'></div>高论拔俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367803_comment'></div>精义入神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367803_comment'></div>誓将以儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367803_comment'></div>训齐斯民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367803_comment'></div>文章陵夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367803_comment'></div>郑声夺伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367803_comment'></div>兄于其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367803_comment'></div>振三代风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367803_comment'></div>复雕为朴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367803_comment'></div>正始是崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367803_comment'></div>学者归仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367803_comment'></div>如川朝宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367803_comment'></div>六义炳焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367803_comment'></div>自兄中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367803_comment'></div>大名全才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367803_comment'></div>仪刑百工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367803_comment'></div>呜呼彼天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367803_comment'></div>胡不祐贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367803_comment'></div>阘茸谗谀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367803_comment'></div>或锡永年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367803_comment'></div>好学不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367803_comment'></div>繄兄复然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367803_comment'></div>岂天地不仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367803_comment'></div>将斯民薄祜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367803_comment'></div>禺禺之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367803_comment'></div>见夺何遽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367803_comment'></div>某获见于兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367803_comment'></div>二十有六年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367803_comment'></div>兄有七年之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367803_comment'></div>蒙以伯仲相视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367803_comment'></div>博文约礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367803_comment'></div>谓仁由已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367803_comment'></div>同心之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367803_comment'></div>期于没齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367803_comment'></div>前后尺牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367803_comment'></div>罗列案几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367803_comment'></div>愔愔清论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367803_comment'></div>恍恍在耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367803_comment'></div>一旦如失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367803_comment'></div>万事遄已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367803_comment'></div>民之所望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367803_comment'></div>今也胡俟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367803_comment'></div>心酸骨悽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367803_comment'></div>容徽自此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367803_comment'></div>永不复见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367803_comment'></div>若魂魄无不之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367803_comment'></div>岂不睹平生心于今日斗酒之奠乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367803_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_88_1367803_comment'></div></div></div><br 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367760")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367760_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367760'>桉前志。禅师号僧璨。不知何许人。出见于周隋间。传教于惠可大师。抠衣于邺中。得道于司空山。谓身相非真。故示有疮疾。谓法无我所。故居不择地。以众生病为病。故至必说法度人。以一相不在内外不在其中间。故足言不以文字。其教大略以寂照妙用摄群品。流注生灭观四维上下。不见法。不见身。不见心。乃至心离名字。身等空界。法同梦幻。亦无得无證。然后谓之解脱。禅门率是道也。上膺付嘱。下拯昏疑。大云垂阴。国土为化。谓南方教所未至。我是以有罗浮之行。其来不来也。其去无去也。既而以袈裟与法。俱付悟者。道存形谢。遗骨此山。今二百岁矣。皇帝即位后五年。岁次庚戍。及剖符是州。登禅师遗居。周览陈迹。明徵故事。其茶毗起塔之制。实天宝景戌中别驾前河南少尹赵郡李公尝经始之。碑版之文。隋内史侍郎河东薛公道衡唐相国刑部尚书赠太尉河南房公琯继论撰之。而尊道之典。易名之礼。则朝廷方以多故而未遑也。长老比邱释湛然。诵经于灵塔之下。与涧松俱老。痛先师名氏未经邦国焉。与禅众寺大律师释澄俊。同寅叶恭。亟以为请。会是岁嵩岳大比邱释惠融至自广陵。胜业寺大比邱释开悟至自庐江。俱纂我禅师后七叶之遗训。日相与叹塔之不命。号之不崇。惧像法之本根坠于地也。愿申无边众生之宏誓。以抒罔极。扬州牧御史大夫张公延赏以状闻。于是七年夏四月。上沛然降兴废继绝之诏。册谥禅师曰镜智。塔曰觉寂。以大德僧七人洒扫供养。天书锡命。晖焕崖谷。众庶踊跃。谓大乘中兴。是日。大比邱众议立石于塔东南隅。纪心法兴废之所以然。及以为初中国之有佛教。自汉孝明始也。历魏晋宋齐。施及梁武。言第一义谛者。不过布施持戒。天下惑于报应。而人未知禅。世与道交相丧。至菩提达摩大师。始示人以诸佛心要。人疑而未思。惠可大师傅而持之。人思而未修。迨禅师三叶。其风浸广。真如法味。日渐月渍。万木之根茎枝叶。悉沐化雨。然后空王之密藏。二祖之微言。始灿然行于世间。浃于人心。当时问道于禅师者。其浅者知有为法。无非妄想。深者见佛性于言下。如灯之照物。朝为凡夫。夕为圣贤。双峰大师道信其人也。其后信公以教传宏忍。忍公传惠能神秀。能公退而老曹溪。其嗣无闻焉。秀公传普寂。寂公之门徒万人。升堂者六十有三。得自在慧者一曰宏正。正公之廊庑龙象又倍焉。或化嵩洛。或之荆吴。自是心教之被于世也。与六籍侔盛。呜呼。微禅师。吾其二乘矣。后代何述焉。庸讵知禅师之下生不为诸佛。故现比邱身以救浊劫乎。亦犹尧舜既往。周公制礼。仲尼述之。游夏宏之。使高堂后苍徐孟戴庆之徒。可得而祖焉。天以圣贤所振为木铎。其揆一也。诸公以为司马子长立夫子世家。谢临川撰慧远法师碑铭。将令千载之后。知先师之全身。禅门之权舆。王命之丕显。在此山也。则扬其风。记其时。宜在法流。及尝味禅师之道也久。故不让。其铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367760_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367760'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367760'>众生佛性，莫非宿植。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367760'>知诱于外，染为妄识。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367760'>如浪斯鼓，与风动息。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367760'>淫騃贪怒，为刃为贼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367760'>生死有涯，缘起无极。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367760'>如来悯之，为辟度门。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367760'>即妄了真，以證觉源。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367760'>启迪心印，贻我后昆。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367760'>閒生禅师，俾以教尊。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367760'>二十八劫，迭付微言。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1367760'>如如禅师，膺期宏宣。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1367760'>世溷法灭，独与道全。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1367760'>童蒙来求，我以意传。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1367760'>摄相归性，法身乃圆。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1367760'>性身本空，我无说焉。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1367760'>如如禅师，道既弃世。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1367760'>将三十纪，妙经乃届。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1367760'>皇明昭贲，亿兆膜拜。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1367760'>凡今后学，入佛境界。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1367760'>于取非取，谁缚谁解。<div id='poem_sentence_19_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1367760'>万有千岁，此法无坏。<div id='poem_sentence_20_1367760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1367760'></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1367760_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年5月</a>　在舒州任，为睢阳太守秘书监李少涵撰写神道碑铭。作品：《唐故睢阳太守赠秘书监李公神道碑铭并序》<div id='poem_1367757' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367757' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367757?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故睢阳太守赠秘书监李公神道碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（772年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367757")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367757_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367757'>汉家之建侯亲亲也。以荆燕吴楚为首封。而后嗣多材。世济厥美。辟疆路叔。更生子骏。比肩而出。庆钟故也。唐有天下。肺腑是依。有若江夏淮安。河閒东平。以明略茂勋。左右大业。其休德粹气。降为百祥。公子公孙。或哲或仁。勤劳王家。焜耀国牒。从东平三叶。后生睢阳。言春秋者。谓公族多士。与炎汉侔矣。公讳少康。字某。太祖景皇帝五代孙。太祖生雍王绘。雍王生东平王绍。东平王生高平王道立。高平王生毕公景淑。初毕公娶于太常京兆韦万石女。有才子三人。伯曰孟康。忠敬直温。谦光不耀。官至太子左赞善大夫。仲曰仲康。宏毅密重。文敏贞谅。由尚书主客郎中剖符楚州。人到于今由其教而思其躅。公楚州之母弟也。纂二昭二穆慎身之烈。迪元方季方裕蛊之范。家贻其谋。天钟其休。故蓄为和气。播为盛德。年始孩而毕公捐馆。七岁受孝经。至丧亲章。捧书孺慕。哀哽不食。邻伍长幼。为之涕泗。既冠。遭太夫人弃孝养。苴貌茹毒。泣血无声者三年。自是孝称乡党。名冠宗室。会垂拱永昌以后。天下有燕啄之谣。七庙支庶。不绝若綖。公正志蒙难。危行全德。贞厉二十年。以俟道长。中兴后乃筮仕。由朝邑县尉凡七徙。官至尚书祠部郎中。以大府上佐授潞州司马。因考绩彰闻。拔为青州刺史。于是海岱贡篚。衣履天下。俗尚夸侈。吏务豪夺。公以德礼示法度。以诛赏禁淫慝。宣明教化。饬行率先。使刺绣倚市者。悉返耕织。于是贪者廉。善者劝。海滨之俗。变至邹鲁。按察使户部侍郎宋遥以状闻。玺书褒异。迁公于常州。赐一子出身。常之吏民。望公风声。其奇邪僭滥者。解印绶自去。比及下车。无为而治。复以高第擢拜徐州刺史。先是岁比大歉。人流者什五六。公条奏逋逃之名。削去其版。然后节用务本。薄征缓刑以来之。岁则大穰。人不患寡。浮游自占者至数千万。优诏嘉叹。赐帛二百匹。玄宗后元年。改宋州为睢阳郡。命公为太守。淮河漕挽。刀布辐凑。万商射利。奸之所由聚也。公谓非胜之艰。安之惟艰。故峻其侵渔之令。宏其并容之仁。吏或不廉不恪。不惠不迪。纠之诘之。必诚必信。公之诚信不欺。故狱市不扰。闾井辑睦。由是饮公醇固之德者。如馁者得哺。寒者得纩。有司方将计课以闻。天不惠于宋。乃崇降厉疾。三年春。赐告归洛阳。是岁十二月丙午薨。春秋六十有四。宗室悽欷。士友失图。宋人徐人。辍舂相唁。明年某月。迁宅兆于京兆见子原先茔。礼也。公雅善属词。有集二十卷。晚节好禅味。耽道论。尝传道德上下经五千言。为之训解。以究微旨。其为政贞方廉静。明达端懿。严不残。直不讦。清不矫时。善不徇名。交友推诚。好恶中节。博见强志。亲仁爱士。居险用晦。遭时利往。行藏之机。与道屈伸。未始以去就宠辱。渎其出处。而寿位未极其量也。故休祐复集于后昆。夫人某县太君广平程氏。生元子曰涵。以忠文孝让。仪刑王室。天子谓可内司九法。外镇百城。大历七年夏五月。由尚书兵部侍郎为御史大夫苏州刺史。巡省江左。迈德诒训之所及也。夫人沛国武氏。以继室生仲子汘。汘弟浓。皆卿材。而不幸早世。某年月日。朝廷建推恩之令。追赠公秘书监。大夫之孝。达于祖祢也。及尝忝礼官之属。知王侯之庙祧昭穆。与功烈德善。故受命于大夫。酌而为志。著之乐石。以代烝夷曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367757_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367757'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367757'>敦叙九族，皇风所始。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367757'>公生德门，运叶麟趾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367757'>王曰叔父，高阳才子。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367757'>缵乃祖服，似续介祉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367757'>厎绩三署，旧章孔修。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1367757'>仁浃鳏寡，道在彝鼎。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1367757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1367757_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年</a>　在舒州任，有文送王判官赴福州。作品：《送王判官赴福州序》<div id='poem_1367686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367686?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送王判官赴福州序</a><span class='authorDate'>（772年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367686")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367686_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367686'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367686'>松梓楩楠。茂于深山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367686_comment'></div>不能逃匠石之顾。贤士君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367686_comment'></div>晦其言迹。不能使人不已知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367686_comment'></div>其势然也。之子言忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367686_comment'></div>行笃敬。以文雅丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367686_comment'></div>则括而羽之。而世皆观颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367686_comment'></div>我独俭德。吾固知长风六翮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367686_comment'></div>必有时而去。及御史大夫李公之命介也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367686_comment'></div>辟书四下。果以嗣宗为首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367686_comment'></div>岁二月。载骤四骆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367686_comment'></div>脂车而东。闽中者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367686_comment'></div>左溟海。右百越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367686_comment'></div>岭外峭峻。风俗剽悍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367686_comment'></div>岁比饥馑。民方札瘥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367686_comment'></div>非威非怀。莫可绥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367686_comment'></div>议者共谓君匡戎幕以义。佐师律以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367686_comment'></div>报国士以直。道罢人以德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367686_comment'></div>使安危悬于指掌。胜负决于谈笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367686_comment'></div>则咨谋之道宏矣。岂椎髻殊俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367686_comment'></div>覆车畏途。足为志士之怵惕哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367686_comment'></div>凡吾与之出祖者。亦既偕赋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367686_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1367686_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=773')">773年4月</a>　在舒州任。作品：《殇子韦八墓志》<div id='poem_1367764' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367764' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367764?labeling=true' target='_blank'>殇子韦八墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（773年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367764")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367764_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367764'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367764'>殇子河南独孤氏。小字韦八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367764_comment'></div>以其弱而未名也。故以字称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367764_comment'></div>北齐司空行台尚书令临川郡王七代孙。有唐安南郡长史府君之曾孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367764_comment'></div>颍川郡长史府君之孙。左骁卫兵曹参军公之元子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367764_comment'></div>秘书省著作郎京兆韦攒之甥。生有奇表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367764_comment'></div>温明聪秀。覃吁于保姆傅婢之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367764_comment'></div>嶷然异于凡童。气闲体和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367764_comment'></div>取与必时。诸父诸姑每谓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367764_comment'></div>兴我家者。必此儿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367764_comment'></div>宾客之至者。看玉人不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367764_comment'></div>倘假以寿命。则成器致位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367764_comment'></div>未易度也。不幸多病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367764_comment'></div>大历六年岁次辛亥十二月二十二日。夭于舒州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367764_comment'></div>寿止五岁三十甲子。长幼惋毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367764_comment'></div>六姻悼惜。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367764_comment'></div>天将不昌我后裔乎。不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367764_comment'></div>曷使此孩不至于成欤。大历八年夏四月十六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367764_comment'></div>以其丧归洛阳。祔于王父母宅兆之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367764_comment'></div>其仲父衔涕书其始终。记于墓云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367764_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1367764_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=773')">773年12月23日</a>　擢拜常州刺史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=773')">773年</a>　或是年在常州有祭亡妻文，姑系于此。作品：《祭亡妻博陵郡君文》<div id='poem_1367806' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367806' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367806?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭亡妻博陵郡君文</a><span class='authorDate'>（773年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367806")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367806_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367806'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367806'>维大历八年二月十五日。检校司封郎中兼舒州刺史独孤及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367806_comment'></div>谨以清酌菜果之奠。祭于故博陵郡君之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367806_comment'></div>呜呼。及顾惟鄙薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367806_comment'></div>谬忝好合。采蘩助祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367806_comment'></div>岁时未几。执手偕老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367806_comment'></div>昊天遽夺。齐体苦晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367806_comment'></div>遗迹太早。犹未知寿域有涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367806_comment'></div>短长已臻其极耶。将及薄祜速舋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367806_comment'></div>宜为淑明所弃耶。屋壁挂存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367806_comment'></div>琴瑟响绝。修法劝义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367806_comment'></div>今将畴依。日月有时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367806_comment'></div>龟筮告协。将涉故路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367806_comment'></div>祔于先茔。及为印绶所拘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367806_comment'></div>不获亲自封树。岂虞此别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367806_comment'></div>死生间之。往岁方舟偕来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367806_comment'></div>今也单輤独归。郊圻一恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367806_comment'></div>心骨可绝。顷者万事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367806_comment'></div>无非去尘。变化茫茫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367806_comment'></div>往矣何道。今也卮酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367806_comment'></div>将抒永别。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367806_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1367806_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
常州（武进）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a897fa144670443c84ace6d80f679e22_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a897fa144670443c84ace6d80f679e22");'><span id='a897fa144670443c84ace6d80f679e22_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=777')">774-777年</a>，50-53岁</div><div id='a897fa144670443c84ace6d80f679e22' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年3月17日</a>　抵常州，有谢表。作品：《谢常州刺史表》<div id='poem_1367658' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367658' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367658?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢常州刺史表</a><span class='authorDate'>（774年3月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367658")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367658_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367658'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367658'>臣及言。臣伏奉去年十二月二十三日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367658_comment'></div>授臣使持节常州诸军事守常州刺史充当州团练守捉使。臣伏以江东之州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367658_comment'></div>常州为大。陛下不以臣不肖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367658_comment'></div>拔臣于群吏之中。以考则年未久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367658_comment'></div>以劳则功无可录。而除拜之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367658_comment'></div>加于人一等。臣及诚惶诚恐顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367658_comment'></div>臣往岁尝忝谏官。历博士尚书郎之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367658_comment'></div>虽备尝献纳。累黩天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367658_comment'></div>竟无丝发裨补明盛。及典濠舒二州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367658_comment'></div>出入七年。又不能副陛下政平讼息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367658_comment'></div>与吾共此之叹。至如流人自占。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367658_comment'></div>旱不为灾。实由陛下当勤恤之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367658_comment'></div>下哀痛之诏。宽减租税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367658_comment'></div>入三分之二。是以和气旁感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367658_comment'></div>变灾为福。福流臣州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367658_comment'></div>人是以乂。臣宁敢贪天之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367658_comment'></div>以为已力。今陛下赐臣诏曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367658_comment'></div>断狱岁减。流庸日归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367658_comment'></div>以人俗之丰给。当淮湖之灾旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367658_comment'></div>陟尔明效。宜列中朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367658_comment'></div>臣无其实。谬奉殊奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367658_comment'></div>伏览圣旨。惶悚陨越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367658_comment'></div>况陛下励精百揆之始。日以尧吁舜咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367658_comment'></div>旁求俊造。或经时不除一吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367658_comment'></div>除必以公才为先。苟非其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367658_comment'></div>位不虚授。搢绅之辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367658_comment'></div>侥倖望绝。臣当此时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367658_comment'></div>独荷荣寄。人之多幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367658_comment'></div>将自臣始。致寇速谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367658_comment'></div>实忧自贻。今以三月十七日到州上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367658_comment'></div>虽欲勉励疲钝。增修吏职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367658_comment'></div>惧力不逮。上累皇明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367658_comment'></div>奉诏夕惕。且惭且骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367658_comment'></div>无任感戴喜惧之至。谨奉表陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367658_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1367658_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年4月</a>　在常州任。作品：《唐故商州录事参军郑府君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1367779' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367779' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367779?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故商州录事参军郑府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（774年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367779")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367779_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367779'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367779'>公讳密。字慎微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367779_comment'></div>荥阳开封人也。初韩哀侯灭郑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367779_comment'></div>群公子奔陈宋间。始以国为氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367779_comment'></div>惟桓公武公之德盛。故国除而其姓弥大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367779_comment'></div>历汉魏晋迄于今。冠冕婚姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367779_comment'></div>世莫与京。公其裔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367779_comment'></div>齐中书监南兖州刺史谥曰平讳述祖。公之六代祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367779_comment'></div>国朝卫州刺史府君讳某。公之大王父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367779_comment'></div>博州刺史府君讳某。晋州临汾令赠太常少卿府君讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367779_comment'></div>公之祖祢也。公贞方介直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367779_comment'></div>勤而爱人。初仕赵州柏乡尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367779_comment'></div>所涖不过一扃。而政行一邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367779_comment'></div>廉使省风俗至赵。赵父老率吏人数千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367779_comment'></div>遮道称公之能。识者韪公材且得众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367779_comment'></div>满岁。归洛阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367779_comment'></div>家于鸣皋山。南趣深险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367779_comment'></div>以避安禄山之乱。亲故数百家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367779_comment'></div>携老幼往依之。公悉发窦窖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367779_comment'></div>无亲疏皆仰给。饿者窘者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367779_comment'></div>得公全活。先是累岁力耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367779_comment'></div>致粟至千斛。至是而尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367779_comment'></div>谈者称公之义。二京返正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367779_comment'></div>天子选贤守相令长。将苏疮痍之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367779_comment'></div>殿中侍御史王政以公充赋。拜商州洛南令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367779_comment'></div>数月。讼平赋均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367779_comment'></div>监察御史李椅殿中侍御史王延昌御史中丞元公载并表言其状。诏书褒称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367779_comment'></div>加公寿王府户曹参军。洛南如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367779_comment'></div>无何。迁上津令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367779_comment'></div>专知转运水陆漕挽。邦都移用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367779_comment'></div>赖公而济。徙大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367779_comment'></div>商州刺史卢浦以公前后课绩条奏。遂以本官兼商州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367779_comment'></div>御史中丞王延昌表公才任御史。奏未下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367779_comment'></div>会疾终于位。春秋五十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367779_comment'></div>是岁广德元年八月七日也。其年权窆于商州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367779_comment'></div>夫人清河崔氏某之女。生子雅弟干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367779_comment'></div>大历九年岁次甲寅十一月某日。返葬于洛阳北邙山某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367779_comment'></div>礼也。公世业尚文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367779_comment'></div>伯仲皆才。公尤深于诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367779_comment'></div>言合丽则。究缘情之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367779_comment'></div>天性孝悌。检身端方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367779_comment'></div>居官廉。恪其家道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367779_comment'></div>足以劝所不至者。位止于中士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367779_comment'></div>寿不过知天命。命矣夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367779_comment'></div>公母弟尚书刑部郎中宣秘书省著作郎宝。以其兄之德善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367779_comment'></div>授牍于及。及跪读三复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367779_comment'></div>敢以实录刻石。其辞曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367779_comment'></div>缁衣之宜。敝予改为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367779_comment'></div>蔚彼明德。荫此本支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367779_comment'></div>乃公乃侯。典则是贻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367779_comment'></div>丛祉于公。实生令仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367779_comment'></div>试吏柏仁。嶷然忠规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367779_comment'></div>清不夺节。刚不干时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367779_comment'></div>以道蒙难。处险若夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367779_comment'></div>临财务施。依者如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367779_comment'></div>匪爱千钟。仁为吾师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367779_comment'></div>乱已运开。乃从絷维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367779_comment'></div>先礼后刑。以牧煢嫠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367779_comment'></div>商于之人。家肥俗移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367779_comment'></div>督邮廷评。九仞之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367779_comment'></div>曷云不淑。命天功亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367779_comment'></div>明略未申。贻痛所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367779_comment'></div>吉凶匪忱。今古同悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367779_comment'></div>桐乡之爱。怀县之诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367779_comment'></div>令闻禺禺。子孙承之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367779_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1367779_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年6月</a>　在常州任，六月为仲父侍御史独孤屿作墓志铭。作品：《唐故大理寺少卿兼侍御史河南独孤府君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1367772' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367772' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367772?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故大理寺少卿兼侍御史河南独孤府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（774年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367772")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367772_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367772'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367772'>府君讳玙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367772_comment'></div>河南洛阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367772_comment'></div>汉世祖光武皇帝第二子沛献王辅之昭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367772_comment'></div>齐临川郡王河阳道行台仆射洛州刺史永业府君五代孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367772_comment'></div>国朝明威将军文惠府君第二子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367772_comment'></div>越州都督浙江东道节度观察处置使兼御史中丞右金吾大将军峻府君之季弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367772_comment'></div>聪明仁恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367772_comment'></div>专直宽信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367772_comment'></div>扰而毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367772_comment'></div>温而厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367772_comment'></div>弱冠筮仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367772_comment'></div>以艺即戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367772_comment'></div>藏器安卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367772_comment'></div>非其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367772_comment'></div>天宝十四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367772_comment'></div>安禄山反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367772_comment'></div>朝廷以淮淝海沂三吴咽喉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367772_comment'></div>宜择良佐以贰藩镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367772_comment'></div>命府君为泗州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367772_comment'></div>无何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367772_comment'></div>换滁濠二州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367772_comment'></div>倅戎备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367772_comment'></div>参吏职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367772_comment'></div>忠敏肃给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367772_comment'></div>所涖繄赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367772_comment'></div>御史中丞崔公昭之尹河南也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367772_comment'></div>盛选僚佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367772_comment'></div>表府君为太常丞兼殿中侍御史营田判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367772_comment'></div>使罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367772_comment'></div>转湖州别驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367772_comment'></div>大历五年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367772_comment'></div>崔公受诏持节牧宣歙池三州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367772_comment'></div>府君复为从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367772_comment'></div>以太子右谕德兼殿中侍御史迁大理少卿兼侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367772_comment'></div>方谓宜民宜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367772_comment'></div>禄与寿俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367772_comment'></div>遭命不淑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367772_comment'></div>春秋五十五而殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367772_comment'></div>是岁大历九年春三月二十四日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367772_comment'></div>夫人陇西李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367772_comment'></div>以柏舟之誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367772_comment'></div>提携诸孤某等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367772_comment'></div>奉府君之丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367772_comment'></div>言归洛阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367772_comment'></div>某月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367772_comment'></div>窆于某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367772_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367772_comment'></div>府君少孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367772_comment'></div>事兄嫂以友悌称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367772_comment'></div>在邦在家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367772_comment'></div>言信行果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367772_comment'></div>居官祗事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367772_comment'></div>强志能力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367772_comment'></div>及其冠法冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367772_comment'></div>佐太府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367772_comment'></div>上以勤恪周爰成务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367772_comment'></div>下以明诚劳谦应物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367772_comment'></div>和礼正家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367772_comment'></div>敦睦族姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367772_comment'></div>自疏及亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367772_comment'></div>必慈必爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367772_comment'></div>而命不我与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367772_comment'></div>年未下寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367772_comment'></div>天天其椓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367772_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367772_comment'></div>初府君之金吾伯兄拥旄浙东也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367772_comment'></div>拔崔公于郡吏之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367772_comment'></div>升为军司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367772_comment'></div>推诚委政之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367772_comment'></div>犹晋得韩厥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367772_comment'></div>宋得子罕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367772_comment'></div>及中丞之开府辟掾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367772_comment'></div>府君为首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367772_comment'></div>既而府君之丧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367772_comment'></div>中丞哭之恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367772_comment'></div>赠赙赒给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367772_comment'></div>加于人一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367772_comment'></div>由是稚子孀妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367772_comment'></div>得奉丧而西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367772_comment'></div>三月而葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367772_comment'></div>礼无违者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367772_comment'></div>赙布之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367772_comment'></div>足备祭器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367772_comment'></div>君子谓金吾之明哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367772_comment'></div>诒厥兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367772_comment'></div>宣州之交情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367772_comment'></div>见于死生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367772_comment'></div>知已之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367772_comment'></div>斯其行者鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367772_comment'></div>及敢不以直词书仲父之美于墓石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1367772_comment'></div>其辞曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1367772_comment'></div>叔父懿德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1367772_comment'></div>承家令仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1367772_comment'></div>惠迪哲兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1367772_comment'></div>践脩靡违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1367772_comment'></div>移治于官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1367772_comment'></div>发迹淮沂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1367772_comment'></div>及佐皇华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1367772_comment'></div>亦绣其衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1367772_comment'></div>天子命我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1367772_comment'></div>再参军机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1367772_comment'></div>骆马啴啴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1367772_comment'></div>所从其谁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1367772_comment'></div>显允君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1367772_comment'></div>为诸侯师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1367772_comment'></div>府君委质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1367772_comment'></div>咨诹载驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1367772_comment'></div>式壮其猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1367772_comment'></div>耄未及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1367772_comment'></div>阴阳为寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1367772_comment'></div>子鵩洽期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1367772_comment'></div>昔也陟冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1367772_comment'></div>哀哀永思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1367772_comment'></div>今也反真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1367772_comment'></div>匪公曷依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1367772_comment'></div>伯兮叔兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1367772_comment'></div>今乎已而。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1367772_comment'></div>他年九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1367772_comment'></div>公谁与归。</div><div id='poem_sentence_118_1367772_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年</a>　在常州任。作品：《唐故衢州司士参军李府君墓志铭》《唐前楚州司马河南独孤公博陵崔氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1367762' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367762' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367762?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故衢州司士参军李府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（774年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367762")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367762_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367762'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367762'>公讳涛。皇唐太祖景皇帝六代孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367762_comment'></div>曾祖道立。尝典陕济陈三州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367762_comment'></div>封高平郡王。祖景淑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367762_comment'></div>毕国公。父仲康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367762_comment'></div>官至尚书主客郎中楚州刺史。世秉懿德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367762_comment'></div>为公族领袖。语在皇室谱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367762_comment'></div>公纯孝忠厚。贞信廉让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367762_comment'></div>直而逊。明而晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367762_comment'></div>朴而不固。静而应物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367762_comment'></div>克已复礼。时然后言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367762_comment'></div>策名居官。清畏人知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367762_comment'></div>弱岁好学。笃志经术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367762_comment'></div>专戴氏礼。晚节耽太史公书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367762_comment'></div>酌百代之典故。以辅儒道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367762_comment'></div>以经明行修。宗正寺举第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367762_comment'></div>初仕许州临颍县主簿。历宋州宋城县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367762_comment'></div>皆以恭宽信惠。闻于千室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367762_comment'></div>议黜陟幽明者。谓公文行吏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367762_comment'></div>宜登三台。会河朔军兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367762_comment'></div>避地江表。相国崔涣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367762_comment'></div>承诏署衢州司士参军。于时五府辟召之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367762_comment'></div>移于兵间。务苟进者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367762_comment'></div>多由径而致显位。公俭德正志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367762_comment'></div>安贞俟时。未尝以得丧夷险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367762_comment'></div>芥蒂方寸。视荣辱晏如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367762_comment'></div>论者高之。乾元二年某月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367762_comment'></div>寝疾终于扬州。春秋若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367762_comment'></div>某月日。权窆于衢州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367762_comment'></div>呜呼。仁可以师表缙绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367762_comment'></div>而无贵仕。礼可以轨范风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367762_comment'></div>而不遐寿。冲用休绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367762_comment'></div>卷而未形。溘焉化往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367762_comment'></div>使善人相吊。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367762_comment'></div>公殁后十有二载。从父弟涵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367762_comment'></div>以宗室柱石为御史大夫。按节江东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367762_comment'></div>痛仁兄生不登公侯卿大夫之位。殁不备踰月外姻至之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367762_comment'></div>遂茹哀筮日。减月俸以庀丧具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367762_comment'></div>由是大历九年夏四月二十七日。公长子居介及居佐居敬居易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367762_comment'></div>奉公之輤柩归葬于洛阳先使君夫人宅兆之侧。凡今孝乎惟孝友于兄弟者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367762_comment'></div>于此乎观礼。及谓知公者宜莫若懿亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367762_comment'></div>今将以无愧之词。申报幽路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367762_comment'></div>故作铭以刊之于石。其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367762_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1367762'>天地方否。君子安卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367762_comment'></div>世道既夷。隙驹莫追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367762_comment'></div>仁而不寿。才既无施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367762_comment'></div>积善必庆。天何余欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367762_comment'></div>襜襜裳帷。溯江绝淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367762_comment'></div>苍苍故山。玉树斯埋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367762_comment'></div>死丧之威。兄弟孔怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367762_comment'></div>令德家风。与天壤偕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367762_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1367762_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367768' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367768' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367768?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐前楚州司马河南独孤公故夫人博陵崔氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（774年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367768")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367768_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367768'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367768'>夫人讳某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367768_comment'></div>博陵安平人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367768_comment'></div>曾祖恭礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367768_comment'></div>国朝驸马都尉延齐易三州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367768_comment'></div>封博陵郡男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367768_comment'></div>祖兴宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367768_comment'></div>饶州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367768_comment'></div>考隽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367768_comment'></div>亳州临涣县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367768_comment'></div>夫人少孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367768_comment'></div>在家以纯孝称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367768_comment'></div>既笄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367768_comment'></div>庄明而贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367768_comment'></div>柔顺有识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367768_comment'></div>年若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367768_comment'></div>归于独孤氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367768_comment'></div>奉蘋藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367768_comment'></div>供祭祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367768_comment'></div>事长抚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367768_comment'></div>纠合宗族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367768_comment'></div>敬恭而诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367768_comment'></div>孝爱备至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367768_comment'></div>动必由礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367768_comment'></div>非法度未尝践也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367768_comment'></div>生子四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367768_comment'></div>教之以义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367768_comment'></div>夙夜贞励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367768_comment'></div>家道以正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367768_comment'></div>娣姒服其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367768_comment'></div>亲戚称其慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367768_comment'></div>天不降衷于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367768_comment'></div>大历八年十一月某日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367768_comment'></div>享年若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367768_comment'></div>殁于寿州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367768_comment'></div>少长行哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367768_comment'></div>六姻涕泗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367768_comment'></div>伤夫人有宜室之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367768_comment'></div>劝义之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367768_comment'></div>而司命夺其长算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367768_comment'></div>使德与寿反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367768_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367768_comment'></div>明年十一月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367768_comment'></div>公使长男绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367768_comment'></div>奉夫人之丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367768_comment'></div>返葬京师某原先茔之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367768_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367768_comment'></div>刊石以志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367768_comment'></div>庶德不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367768_comment'></div>其铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367768_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1367768'>夫人之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367768_comment'></div>柔明淑慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367768_comment'></div>从夫以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367768_comment'></div>承筐以顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367768_comment'></div>奉若家节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367768_comment'></div>率由彝训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367768_comment'></div>遐福是期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367768_comment'></div>溘至何迅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367768_comment'></div>谓仁者寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367768_comment'></div>天实不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367768_comment'></div>同尘彭殇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367768_comment'></div>归根大运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367768_comment'></div>于以刊石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367768_comment'></div>永播淑闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1367768_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_40918'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_40918_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=775&endYear=775')">775年</a>　在常州任。作品：《唐故虢州宏农县令天水赵府君墓志》《送少微上人之天台国清寺序》《福州都督府新学碑铭并序》<div id='poem_1367780' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367780' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367780?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故虢州宏农县令天水赵府君墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（775年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367780")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367780_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367780'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367780'>府君讳令则。字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367780_comment'></div>天水人也。其先造父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367780_comment'></div>实佐周穆。有平徐偃王之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367780_comment'></div>因封命氏。至晋而大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367780_comment'></div>以成季宣孟之庆。故化家为国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367780_comment'></div>及武灵而称王。语在太史公赵世家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367780_comment'></div>秦灭诸侯。使赵王嘉子公辅主西戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367780_comment'></div>戎人怀之。子孙因家陇西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367780_comment'></div>世为天水著姓。其源远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367780_comment'></div>曾祖元楷。隋殿中监工部尚书淮安公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367780_comment'></div>祖崇基。国朝岐州郿县令符玺郎右卫长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367780_comment'></div>烈考庆逸。正议大夫许州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367780_comment'></div>府君长史第二子也。好古博学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367780_comment'></div>涉猎百家之言。善属文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367780_comment'></div>尤注意诗赋。外刚毅峭直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367780_comment'></div>内温良而仁。率由天性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367780_comment'></div>果于行已。起家幽州蓟县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367780_comment'></div>敏给强济。闻于河朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367780_comment'></div>以直道事人。忤幽州刺史张守圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367780_comment'></div>贬封州开建县尉。遇赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367780_comment'></div>迁建州建安县丞。稍移湖州安吉县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367780_comment'></div>天宝九载。选授虢州宏农县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367780_comment'></div>宏农甸服也。地迩赋殷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367780_comment'></div>号为难治。府君治之如治家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367780_comment'></div>刑以肃淫怠。德以哀鳏寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367780_comment'></div>为政期年。邑民知方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367780_comment'></div>三年绩成。人无不均不安之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367780_comment'></div>虢人颂之。解龟后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367780_comment'></div>贫无馀资。因<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1367780", 1367780, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>游方</span>河朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367780_comment'></div>会天宝十五载。幽都为戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367780_comment'></div>荐瘥钟运。明夷垂翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367780_comment'></div>至德二载某月日。遇疾终于某州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367780_comment'></div>春秋若干。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367780_comment'></div>民莫不谷。我独百罹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367780_comment'></div>才如府君。胡不朋三寿绥百禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367780_comment'></div>而生世坎𡒄。殁身丧乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367780_comment'></div>若之何不吊。命矣夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367780_comment'></div>夫人河南独孤氏。朝议大夫汝南郡长史府君之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367780_comment'></div>武功县丞府君之女。明哲柔懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367780_comment'></div>实天生德。结帨宜室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367780_comment'></div>四十有四载。内修法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367780_comment'></div>辅佐君子。躬勤慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367780_comment'></div>以化闺门。赵氏之家肥族睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367780_comment'></div>繄夫人是赖。有子若干人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367780_comment'></div>训以义方。咸能被服文艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367780_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1367780", 1367780, "Clauses/90/Comments/0")'>干父之蛊</span>。使有德者必寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367780_comment'></div>夫人宜登期颐。奈何不淑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367780_comment'></div>遽夺<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1367780", 1367780, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>长算</span>。天实不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367780_comment'></div>人乌徼福。大历十年五月二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367780_comment'></div>寝疾终于郿县官舍。春秋六十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367780_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。长子湖州安吉县丞琪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367780_comment'></div>琪弟某官瓘。苏州嘉兴县丞璒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367780_comment'></div>太子舍人兼京兆府郿县令玗。晋州临汾县尉佩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367780_comment'></div>临晋县尉珦。珦弟玘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367780_comment'></div>是岁秋八月某日。奉府君夫人之丧合祔于京兆某原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367780_comment'></div>礼也。府君有集若干卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367780_comment'></div>遐迩之志。见于词矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367780_comment'></div>若言行才业。官族岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367780_comment'></div>非铭无以示后裔也。故著于石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367780_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_59_1367780_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367728' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367728' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367728?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送少微上人之天台国清寺序</a><span class='authorDate'>（775年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367728")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367728_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367728'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367728'>或问上人曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367728_comment'></div>文者所以足言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367728_comment'></div>言说将忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367728_comment'></div>文字性离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367728_comment'></div>示入此徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367728_comment'></div>无乃累一相乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367728_comment'></div>答曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367728_comment'></div>称示入者过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367728_comment'></div>以习气未之泯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367728_comment'></div>率性修道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367728_comment'></div>庶几因言遣言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367728_comment'></div>故欲罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367728_comment'></div>而未能耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367728_comment'></div>时人谓上人为知言知道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367728_comment'></div>岁次乙卯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367728_comment'></div>自京持钵而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367728_comment'></div>给事中天水赵公涓赋诗抒别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367728_comment'></div>卿大夫已下属而和者二十七章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367728_comment'></div>既而飞锡济江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367728_comment'></div>休于晋陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367728_comment'></div>又东至于姑苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367728_comment'></div>将涉震泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367728_comment'></div>踰会稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367728_comment'></div>上天台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367728_comment'></div>至国清上方而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367728_comment'></div>趣静境者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367728_comment'></div>不料远近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367728_comment'></div>登渐门者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367728_comment'></div>不计岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367728_comment'></div>则上人还斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367728_comment'></div>讵可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367728_comment'></div>上人之文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367728_comment'></div>可得而闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367728_comment'></div>诸公将议远别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367728_comment'></div>得不以斯文为赠乎。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1367728_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367754' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367754' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367754?labeling=true' target='_blank'>福州都督府新学碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（775年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367754")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367754_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367754'>世与道交相兴丧。宏之者在人。非庚桑楚。不能使畏垒大壤向化。微文翁。蜀学不崇。闽中无儒家流。成公至而俗易。民赖德施。古今一也。初成公之始至也。未及下车。礼先圣先师。退而叹堂室湫狭。敩学荒坠。惧鼓箧之道寝。子衿之诗作。我是以易其地。大其制。新其栋宇。盛其俎豆。俎豆既修。乃以五经训民。考校必精。弦诵必时。于是一年人知敬学。二年学者功倍。三年而生徒祁祁。贤不肖竞劝。家有洙泗。户有邹鲁。儒风济济。被于庶政。大历十年岁在甲寅秋九月。公薨于位。于是群吏庶民。耆儒诸生。雨泣庙门之外。若有望而不至。号曰。岂天不欲斯文之渐渍于东瓯之人欤。不然。何锡厥化而不遐公之年也。吾党瞠然。呜呼曷归。判官膳部员外郎兼侍御史安定皇甫政殿中侍御史颍川韩贽监察御史河南长孙绘率门人部从事州佐县尹相与议。以公之功绩。明示后世。谓及尝同司谏之列。宜备知盛德善政。见托论撰。以实录刻石曰。公讳椅。字某。皇帝之诸父。宗室之才子。宽裕恺悌。孝慈忠敬。庄而成式。文而强力。治王氏易左氏春秋。酌其精义。以辅儒行。故居处执事。著书属词。非周公轨躅不践也。天宝三载应选部辩论。为安阳县尉。中兴之后。历御史尚书郎谏议大夫给事中。十馀年间。周历三台。言中彝伦。动中大本。上交不谄。下交不渎。家贫不乐清近。求为京兆少尹。无何。出守宏农。宏农人和。又移典华阴。兼御史中丞。华阴之近者安。远者来。天子以为才任四岳十二牧之职。大历七年冬十有一月。加御史大夫持节都督福建泉汀漳五州军事领观察处置都防御等使。八年夏四月。龙旂六辔。至自京师。闽粤旧风。机巧剽轻。资货产利。与巴蜀埒富。犹有无诸馀善之遗俗。号曰难治。公将治之也。考礼正刑。节用爱人。颁赋遣役。必齐其劳逸。视年丰耗。量入以制用。削去事之烦苛。法之掊克者。吏不奉职。民不帅教。则惩以薄刑。俾寖迁善。繇是民知方矣。公将安之也。初哥舒晃反书至。公屦及于门。遽命上将帅戈船下濑之师。西与钟陵军会。先拔循潮二州。以援番禺。推诚誓众。士皆奋勇。既而大憝就戮。五岭厎定。民是以康。繄我师是赖。人无奸宄寇贼之虞矣。公将教之也。考頖宫之制。作为此学而寓政焉。躬率群吏之稍食。与赎刑之馀羡。以备经营之费。而不溷于民也。先师寝庙七十子之像在东序。讲堂书室函丈之席在西序。齿冑之位。列于廊庑之左右。每岁二月上丁。习舞释菜。先三日。公斋戒肄礼。命博士率冑子。修祝嘏。陈祭典。释菜之日。衅器用币。笾豆在堂。樽罍在阼。公元端赤舄。正词陈信。是日。举学士之版。视其艺之上下。审问慎思。使知不足。教之导之。讲论以勖之。八月上丁如初礼。岁终。博士以逊业之勤惰。覃思之精粗告于公。敛其才者。进其等而贡之于宗伯。将进。必以乡饮酒之礼礼之。宾主三揖。受爵于两壶之间。堂下乐作。歌以发德。鹿鸣南陔由庚嘉鱼南山有台以将其厚意。繇是海滨荣之。以不学为耻。州县之教。达于乡党。乡党之教。达于众庶矣。公薨之明年。太常议。按公叔发修卫国之班制以交四邻。故易其名曰文。孔文叔其勤公家。夙夜不懈。卫人铭其彝鼎。以公尊教劝学。德洽荒服。乃奏谥曰成。诏赠礼部尚书。而刻金石之礼。则阙而未备。今也敢播德馨。贻之无穷。其铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367754_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367754'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367754'>公之文兮，肃恭且仁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367754'>宣力事君，润饰经术。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367754'>厎绥斯民，公之武兮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367754'>𩻴寡不侮，刚亦不吐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367754'>率师勤王，戡厥丑虏。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367754'>公之移风，经始泮宫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367754'>百堵皆兴，孔堂崇崇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367754'>四科以班，乃侯乃公。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367754'>秩秩祀典，锵锵礼容。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367754'>大昕鼓徵，学士萃止。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1367754'>褒衣方屦，登降以齿。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1367754'>从公于迈，乐我泮水。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1367754'>我廛我里，讲诵资始。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1367754'>比屋为儒，俊选如林。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1367754'>缦胡之缨，化为青衿。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1367754'>公宜难老，为学者司南。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1367754'>板日告凶，实天匪忱。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1367754'>哕哕和鸾兮，不闻遗音。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1367754'>愿言思公兮，如玉如金。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1367754'>馀烈镂石，以塞民心。<div id='poem_sentence_19_1367754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=775&endYear=775')">775年</a>　在常州任，长子郎生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=775&endYear=775')">775年</a>　在常州任。作品：《奉和中书舍人晚秋集贤院赠徐薛二侍郎》<div id='poem_sentence_12_40887_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年</a>　在常州任，约于此年滁州刺史李幼卿卒，有祭文。作品：《祭滁州李庶子文》<div id='poem_1367805' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367805' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367805?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭滁州李庶子文</a><span class='authorDate'>（776年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367805")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367805_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367805'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367805'>年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367805_comment'></div>常州刺史独孤及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367805_comment'></div>谨以清酌嘉蔬之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367805_comment'></div>敬祭于故右庶子滁州刺史扬州大都督府司马兼侍御史陇西李长夫之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367805_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367805_comment'></div>才与上寿并者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367805_comment'></div>吾不得见之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367805_comment'></div>得见中寿者斯可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367805_comment'></div>呜呼长夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367805_comment'></div>曾未半之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367805_comment'></div>官不展才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367805_comment'></div>事不如志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367805_comment'></div>奄谢昭世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367805_comment'></div>溘归黄泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367805_comment'></div>虽欲茹哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367805_comment'></div>哀可茹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367805_comment'></div>追惟长夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367805_comment'></div>行茂神俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367805_comment'></div>孝爱友睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367805_comment'></div>谅直仁勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367805_comment'></div>卓荦夸迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367805_comment'></div>英明旷达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367805_comment'></div>文武志略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367805_comment'></div>邦家必闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367805_comment'></div>为州治行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367805_comment'></div>居百城之最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367805_comment'></div>诗赋歌事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367805_comment'></div>穷六义之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367805_comment'></div>休声喧于里巷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367805_comment'></div>佳句被于管弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367805_comment'></div>圭璋令问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367805_comment'></div>中外注耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367805_comment'></div>谓当入拜九卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367805_comment'></div>出分四岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367805_comment'></div>万人所望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367805_comment'></div>一旦中止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367805_comment'></div>行路悼惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367805_comment'></div>岂直同心者之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367805_comment'></div>沧州长挹之谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367805_comment'></div>玉溪独往之兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367805_comment'></div>竟迫身世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367805_comment'></div>永孤愿言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367805_comment'></div>傥魂而有知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367805_comment'></div>当饮痛泉下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367805_comment'></div>往岁滁城之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367805_comment'></div>俱未以少别为戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367805_comment'></div>临歧道旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367805_comment'></div>坎坎鼓我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367805_comment'></div>酒酣气振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367805_comment'></div>言尽欢甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367805_comment'></div>孰知此际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367805_comment'></div>以是永诀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367805_comment'></div>今万事如昨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367805_comment'></div>书札犹新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367805_comment'></div>惟故人音容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367805_comment'></div>不可复见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367805_comment'></div>悲莫悲兮生别离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367805_comment'></div>况长往之别乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367805_comment'></div>王事拘限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367805_comment'></div>莫由执绋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367805_comment'></div>卮酒豆肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367805_comment'></div>后会无期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367805_comment'></div>彼苍悠悠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367805_comment'></div>逝者何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367805_comment'></div>长夫长夫。<div class='inline' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年11月</a>　在常州任。作品：《常州奏甘露降松树表》<div id='poem_1367659' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367659' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367659?labeling=true' target='_blank'>常州奏甘露降松树表</a><span class='authorDate'>（776年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(18488, "唐", "独孤及", "poem_title_1367659")'>独孤及</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367659'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367659'>臣及言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367659_comment'></div>臣州内厅东阶下二松树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367659_comment'></div>自今年十月十三日夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367659_comment'></div>至今月十八日夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367659_comment'></div>前后二十七度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367659_comment'></div>甘露下降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367659_comment'></div>树根枝叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367659_comment'></div>沾洒皆遍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367659_comment'></div>洁白凝冱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367659_comment'></div>味同饴蜜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367659_comment'></div>馀溜滴地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367659_comment'></div>委积成泥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367659_comment'></div>倾州官吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367659_comment'></div>咸共荣观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367659_comment'></div>臣谨按鹖冠子云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367659_comment'></div>圣王之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367659_comment'></div>上及太清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367659_comment'></div>下及万灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367659_comment'></div>则甘露下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367659_comment'></div>瑞应图曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367659_comment'></div>王者德至于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367659_comment'></div>则甘露降松柏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367659_comment'></div>陛下实行慈俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367659_comment'></div>怀柔远近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367659_comment'></div>无为之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367659_comment'></div>与太古同风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367659_comment'></div>故天地气和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367659_comment'></div>合而呈瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367659_comment'></div>况休徵感应之始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367659_comment'></div>当陛下降生之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367659_comment'></div>皇符昭晰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367659_comment'></div>天意炳焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367659_comment'></div>盖表圣寿宝历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367659_comment'></div>将与天比崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367659_comment'></div>臣为州三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367659_comment'></div>无绩可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367659_comment'></div>疲朽何幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367659_comment'></div>目睹祯祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367659_comment'></div>臣无任喜忭之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367659_comment'></div>谨奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367659_comment'></div>伏望宣付史馆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1367659_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年</a>　在常州任，七弟独孤正卒于鲁陵郡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年</a>　在常州任，次子独孤郁生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年4月29日</a>　在常州任上卒。<br /></div>
